──────────────────────────────────────────
 FILE: engine/indicators/momentum.py
──────────────────────────────────────────
     1	"""
     2	indicators/momentum.py
     3	AlgoTrader Pro v7.0 — "The Intelligence Pipeline"
     4	
     5	CHANGELOG v2:
     6	  [BUG]    _calc_rsi(): kondisi ~avg_loss.isna() selalu True (ewm tidak pernah
     7	           menghasilkan NaN kecuali di awal), sehingga baris 65 efektif hanya
     8	           mengecek avg_loss > 0. Disederhanakan agar logika jelas dan tidak
     9	           menyesatkan pembaca kode.
    10	  [BUG]    calculate_macd_enhanced(): zero_cross hanya mendeteksi BULLISH cross
    11	           (MACD naik melewati zero), bearish cross (MACD turun melewati zero)
    12	           tidak dideteksi dan tidak mendapat penalti skor. Ini menyebabkan skor
    13	           asimetris: uptrend mendapat +15, downtrend tidak mendapat -15 setara.
    14	           Fix: deteksi kedua arah, bearish zero cross → score -= 15.
    15	  [MINOR]  _stoch_of_series(): fillna(SCORE_NEUTRAL) dipanggil SEBELUM rolling SMA,
    16	           sehingga nilai 50 palsu masuk ke window pertama dan mendistorsi K awal.
    17	           Di steady-state tidak berpengaruh, tapi fix ini membuat nilai awal
    18	           lebih akurat. Dipindah ke setelah smoothing.
    19	"""
    20	
    21	from __future__ import annotations
    22	
    23	import logging
    24	from typing import List, Optional, Tuple
    25	
    26	import numpy as np
    27	import pandas as pd
    28	
    29	from engine.constants import (
    30	    RSI_OVERSOLD_EXTREME,
    31	    RSI_OVERSOLD,
    32	    RSI_BULL_ZONE_LOW,
    33	    RSI_BULL_ZONE_CENTER,
    34	    RSI_OVERBOUGHT,
    35	    RSI_OVERBOUGHT_EXTREME,
    36	    RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD,
    37	    RSI_SLOPE_STRONG_UP,
    38	    RSI_SLOPE_STRONG_DOWN,
    39	    MACD_HIST_REVERSAL_MIN_BARS,
    40	    STOCH_OVERSOLD,
    41	    STOCH_OVERBOUGHT,
    42	    STOCH_CROSS_ZONE_BONUS,
    43	    SCORE_NEUTRAL,
    44	    MIN_CANDLES_FOR_INDICATORS,
    45	)
    46	from engine.core.models import MomentumIndicators, clamp_score
    47	
    48	log = logging.getLogger("indicators.momentum")
    49	
    50	_RSI_WEIGHT      = 0.35
    51	_MACD_WEIGHT     = 0.30
    52	_STOCH_WEIGHT    = 0.22
    53	_VWMA_WEIGHT     = 0.13   # [UPGRADE] VWMA dari ta_compat, konfirmasi volume-momentum
    54	_DIVERGENCE_LOOKBACK = 20
    55	_STOCH_RSI_PERIOD  = 14
    56	_STOCH_PERIOD      = 14
    57	_STOCH_K_SMOOTH    = 3
    58	_STOCH_D_SMOOTH    = 3
    59	_MACD_FAST   = 12
    60	_MACD_SLOW   = 26
    61	_MACD_SIGNAL = 9
    62	
    63	def _ema(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    64	    return series.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
    65	
    66	def _sma(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    67	    return series.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).mean()
    68	
    69	def _wilder_smooth(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    70	    """
    71	    [BUG-FIX -- keputusan desain, dikonfirmasi user setelah penjelasan
    72	    trade-off] Wilder smoothing SMA-seeded, textbook baku (Wilder 1978) --
    73	    pola sama persis dgn _wilder_smooth di strength.py/volatility.py
    74	    (sudah teruji lewat cross-check independen utk ADX, commit 05d7b50).
    75	    Seed = rata-rata SEDERHANA (SMA) dari `period` nilai valid pertama,
    76	    baru direkursi Wilder setelahnya. Ini JUGA metode yang dipakai
    77	    TradingView rma() (rujukan standar yang dipakai operator utk verifikasi
    78	    visual manual bot ini terhadap chart).
    79	    """
    80	    result = np.full(len(series), np.nan)
    81	    arr    = series.values.astype(float)
    82	    n      = len(arr)
    83	
    84	    if n < period:
    85	        return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
    86	
    87	    first_valid = 0
    88	    while first_valid < n and np.isnan(arr[first_valid]):
    89	        first_valid += 1
    90	
    91	    seed_idx = first_valid + period - 1
    92	    if seed_idx >= n:
    93	        return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
    94	
    95	    window = arr[first_valid: first_valid + period]
    96	    if np.any(np.isnan(window)):
    97	        result[seed_idx] = np.nanmean(window)
    98	    else:
    99	        result[seed_idx] = float(np.mean(window))
   100	
   101	    for i in range(seed_idx + 1, n):
   102	        if np.isnan(result[i - 1]) or np.isnan(arr[i]):
   103	            result[i] = result[i - 1] if not np.isnan(result[i - 1]) else np.nan
   104	        else:
   105	            result[i] = (result[i - 1] * (period - 1) + arr[i]) / period
   106	
   107	    return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
   108	
   109	def _calc_rsi(close: pd.Series, period: int = 14) -> pd.Series:
   110	    delta    = close.diff()
   111	    gain     = delta.clip(lower=0)
   112	    loss     = (-delta).clip(lower=0)
   113	    # [BUG-FIX -- keputusan desain, dikonfirmasi user setelah verifikasi
   114	    # matematika independen] Sebelumnya avg_gain/avg_loss pakai
   115	    # `ewm(com=period-1, adjust=False)` -- ini rekursi Wilder tapi SEED-nya
   116	    # dipasang di bar PERTAMA (gain[0]/loss[0] itu sendiri), BUKAN rata-rata
   117	    # `period` nilai pertama seperti metodologi Wilder baku ("New Concepts
   118	    # in Technical Trading Systems", 1978) maupun rma() TradingView (rujukan
   119	    # yang dipakai operator utk verifikasi visual manual). Dibuktikan lewat
   120	    # implementasi independen: di batas bar minimum RSI (16 bar) deviasi
   121	    # bisa sampai 46.7%; bahkan di gerbang produksi (MIN_CANDLES_FOR_
   122	    # INDICATORS=60 bar di observer.py) deviasi rata2 ~0.5 poin, maks ~1.7
   123	    # poin -- kecil tapi TIDAK nol, paling berpengaruh justru di momen
   124	    # paling kritis (koin baru listing / bot baru restart, data masih
   125	    # tipis). Fix: pakai _wilder_smooth (SMA-seeded) -- pola sama yang
   126	    # sudah diterapkan & diverifikasi utk ADX (strength.py, commit
   127	    # 05d7b50) -- supaya konsisten dgn definisi baku & bisa diverifikasi
   128	    # visual terhadap TradingView/exchange chart.
   129	    avg_gain = _wilder_smooth(gain, period)
   130	    avg_loss = _wilder_smooth(loss, period)
   131	
   132	    avg_loss_safe = avg_loss.replace(0.0, np.nan)
   133	    rs = (avg_gain / avg_loss_safe).replace([np.inf, -np.inf], np.nan)
   134	    rsi = 100.0 - (100.0 / (1.0 + rs))
   135	    # [BUG-FIX] Sebelumnya "rsi.where(avg_loss > 0, 100.0)" menyamakan DUA
   136	    # kondisi yang secara matematis BERBEDA saat avg_loss==0:
   137	    #   (a) avg_gain > 0, avg_loss == 0 -> SEMUA pergerakan naik -> RSI=100 BENAR.
   138	    #   (b) avg_gain == 0, avg_loss == 0 -> harga BENAR-BENAR FLAT (tidak ada
   139	    #       gain maupun loss sama sekali, mis. saat konsolidasi/stablecoin
   140	    #       pair) -> harusnya RSI=50 (netral, tidak ada momentum arah sama
   141	    #       sekali), TAPI kode lama tetap memberi 100.0 (overbought ekstrem)
   142	    #       karena hanya mengecek avg_loss==0 tanpa mempedulikan avg_gain.
   143	    # Dibuktikan lewat eksperimen: harga 30 bar identik semua -> RSI lama=100,
   144	    # seharusnya=50. Ini bisa membuat bot salah mengira pasar sideways/flat
   145	    # sebagai "sangat overbought" dan menghindari entry yang sebenarnya netral.
   146	    # Fix: RSI=100 HANYA kalau avg_gain>0 DAN avg_loss==0; kalau keduanya 0
   147	    # (flat total), RSI=50 (netral).
   148	    rsi = rsi.where(avg_loss > 0, np.where(avg_gain > 0, 100.0, 50.0))
   149	    rsi = pd.Series(rsi, index=close.index)
   150	    return rsi.fillna(SCORE_NEUTRAL)
   151	
   152	def _detect_rsi_divergence(
   153	    close: pd.Series,
   154	    rsi: pd.Series,
   155	    lookback: int = _DIVERGENCE_LOOKBACK,
   156	) -> float:
   157	    if len(close) < lookback + 1 or len(rsi) < lookback + 1:
   158	        return 0.0
   159	
   160	    recent_close = close.iloc[-lookback:]
   161	    recent_rsi   = rsi.iloc[-lookback:]
   162	
   163	    curr_close = float(close.iloc[-1])
   164	    curr_rsi   = float(rsi.iloc[-1])
   165	    min_close  = float(recent_close.min())
   166	    max_close  = float(recent_close.max())
   167	    min_rsi    = float(recent_rsi.min())
   168	    max_rsi    = float(recent_rsi.max())
   169	
   170	    if curr_close <= min_close * 1.005:
   171	        rsi_gap = curr_rsi - min_rsi
   172	        if rsi_gap >= RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   173	            return rsi_gap
   174	
   175	    if curr_close >= max_close * 0.995:
   176	        rsi_gap = max_rsi - curr_rsi
   177	        if rsi_gap >= RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   178	            return -rsi_gap
   179	
   180	    return 0.0
   181	
   182	def _rsi_zone_exit(rsi: pd.Series) -> Optional[str]:
   183	    if len(rsi) < 2:
   184	        return None
   185	    prev = float(rsi.iloc[-2])
   186	    curr = float(rsi.iloc[-1])
   187	
   188	    if prev <= RSI_OVERSOLD and curr > RSI_OVERSOLD:
   189	        return "oversold_exit"
   190	    if prev >= RSI_OVERBOUGHT and curr < RSI_OVERBOUGHT:
   191	        return "overbought_exit"
   192	    return None
   193	
   194	_ZONE_EXIT_MIRROR = {"oversold_exit": "overbought_exit", "overbought_exit": "oversold_exit"}
   195	
   196	
   197	def _score_rsi(
   198	    rsi_val: float,
   199	    slope: float,
   200	    divergence: float,
   201	    zone_exit: Optional[str],
   202	    side: str = "long",
   203	) -> float:
   204	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 3, input-reflection] side="short": transform SEMUA
   205	    # input ke titik cerminnya (RSI midpoint=50, slope=turunan seri yg
   206	    # dicerminkan, divergence dikonfirmasi via _detect_rsi_divergence
   207	    # (>0 bullish/<0 bearish), zone_exit swap krn RSI_OVERSOLD(30) &
   208	    # RSI_OVERBOUGHT(70) persis simetris 100- ) -- lalu jalankan formula
   209	    # yang SAMA PERSIS di bawah, tidak diduplikasi/direformulasi.
   210	    if side == "short":
   211	        rsi_val    = 100.0 - rsi_val
   212	        slope      = -slope
   213	        divergence = -divergence
   214	        zone_exit  = _ZONE_EXIT_MIRROR.get(zone_exit, zone_exit)
   215	
   216	    if rsi_val <= RSI_OVERSOLD_EXTREME:
   217	        base = 45.0
   218	    elif rsi_val <= RSI_OVERSOLD:
   219	        t    = (rsi_val - RSI_OVERSOLD_EXTREME) / (RSI_OVERSOLD - RSI_OVERSOLD_EXTREME)
   220	        base = 45.0 + t * 10.0
   221	    elif rsi_val <= RSI_BULL_ZONE_LOW:
   222	        t    = (rsi_val - RSI_OVERSOLD) / (RSI_BULL_ZONE_LOW - RSI_OVERSOLD)
   223	        base = 55.0 - t * 3.0
   224	    elif rsi_val <= RSI_BULL_ZONE_CENTER:
   225	        t    = (rsi_val - RSI_BULL_ZONE_LOW) / (RSI_BULL_ZONE_CENTER - RSI_BULL_ZONE_LOW)
   226	        base = 52.0 + t * 18.0
   227	    elif rsi_val <= RSI_OVERBOUGHT:
   228	        t    = (rsi_val - RSI_BULL_ZONE_CENTER) / (RSI_OVERBOUGHT - RSI_BULL_ZONE_CENTER)
   229	        base = 70.0 - t * 8.0
   230	    elif rsi_val <= RSI_OVERBOUGHT_EXTREME:
   231	        t    = (rsi_val - RSI_OVERBOUGHT) / (RSI_OVERBOUGHT_EXTREME - RSI_OVERBOUGHT)
   232	        base = 40.0 - t * 10.0
   233	    else:
   234	        excess = min(rsi_val - RSI_OVERBOUGHT_EXTREME, 20.0)
   235	        base   = 20.0 - excess * 0.5
   236	
   237	    score = base
   238	
   239	    if slope >= RSI_SLOPE_STRONG_UP:
   240	        score += 10.0
   241	    elif slope <= RSI_SLOPE_STRONG_DOWN:
   242	        score -= 10.0
   243	
   244	    if zone_exit == "oversold_exit":
   245	        score += 15.0
   246	    elif zone_exit == "overbought_exit":
   247	        score -= 10.0
   248	
   249	    if divergence > 0:
   250	        score += min(15.0, divergence)
   251	    elif divergence < 0:
   252	        score += max(-8.0, divergence * 0.5)
   253	
   254	    return clamp_score(score)
   255	
   256	def calculate_rsi_enhanced(
   257	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   258	    period: int = 14,
   259	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   260	    rsi_series: Optional[pd.Series] = None,
   261	) -> MomentumIndicators:
   262	    """
   263	    [PERF v2.2] Parameter rsi_series opsional — kalau caller (observer.py)
   264	    sudah menghitung RSI(14) di tempat lain dengan period yang sama, series
   265	    itu bisa di-pass langsung ke sini supaya tidak dihitung ulang dari nol.
   266	    Kalau None (default) atau panjangnya tidak cocok dengan df, dihitung
   267	    sendiri seperti biasa — tetap backward-compatible untuk pemanggilan
   268	    mandiri/self-test dengan period custom.
   269	    """
   270	    if errors is None:
   271	        errors = []
   272	
   273	    if "close" not in df.columns:
   274	        errors.append("rsi: kolom 'close' tidak tersedia")
   275	        return MomentumIndicators(
   276	            rsi=None,
   277	            rsi_slope=0.0,
   278	            rsi_divergence=0.0,
   279	            rsi_zone_exit=None,
   280	            rsi_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   281	            rsi_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   282	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   283	        )
   284	
   285	    min_bars = period + 2
   286	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   287	        errors.append(
   288	            f"rsi: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   289	        )
   290	        return MomentumIndicators(
   291	            rsi=None,
   292	            rsi_slope=0.0,
   293	            rsi_divergence=0.0,
   294	            rsi_zone_exit=None,
   295	            rsi_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   296	            rsi_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   297	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   298	        )
   299	
   300	    close = df["close"]
   301	    use_external = rsi_series is not None and len(rsi_series) == len(df)
   302	    rsi_series = rsi_series if use_external else _calc_rsi(close, period)
   303	    rsi_val = float(rsi_series.iloc[-1])
   304	
   305	    half = max(1, period // 2)
   306	    if len(rsi_series) > half:
   307	        slope = float(rsi_series.iloc[-1] - rsi_series.iloc[-1 - half])
   308	    else:
   309	        slope = 0.0
   310	
   311	    divergence = _detect_rsi_divergence(close, rsi_series)
   312	    zone_exit = _rsi_zone_exit(rsi_series)
   313	    score = _score_rsi(rsi_val, slope, divergence, zone_exit)
   314	    score_short = _score_rsi(rsi_val, slope, divergence, zone_exit, side="short")
   315	
   316	    log.debug(
   317	        "rsi: val=%.1f slope=%.2f div=%.2f zone=%s → score=%.1f/%.1f(short)",
   318	        rsi_val, slope, divergence, zone_exit, score, score_short,
   319	    )
   320	
   321	    return MomentumIndicators(
   322	        rsi=rsi_val,
   323	        rsi_slope=slope,
   324	        rsi_divergence=divergence,
   325	        rsi_zone_exit=zone_exit,
   326	        rsi_score=score,
   327	        rsi_score_short=score_short,
   328	        composite_score=score,
   329	    )
   330	
   331	def _detect_macd_divergence(
   332	    close: pd.Series,
   333	    macd_line: pd.Series,
   334	    lookback: int = _DIVERGENCE_LOOKBACK,
   335	) -> float:
   336	    if len(close) < lookback + 1 or len(macd_line) < lookback + 1:
   337	        return 0.0
   338	
   339	    recent_close = close.iloc[-lookback:]
   340	    recent_macd  = macd_line.iloc[-lookback:]
   341	
   342	    curr_close = float(close.iloc[-1])
   343	    curr_macd  = float(macd_line.iloc[-1])
   344	    min_close  = float(recent_close.min())
   345	    max_close  = float(recent_close.max())
   346	    min_macd   = float(recent_macd.min())
   347	    max_macd   = float(recent_macd.max())
   348	
   349	    macd_range = max_macd - min_macd
   350	    if macd_range < 1e-9:
   351	        return 0.0
   352	
   353	    if curr_close <= min_close * 1.005:
   354	        macd_gap_pct = (curr_macd - min_macd) / macd_range * 100.0
   355	        if macd_gap_pct >= RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   356	            return macd_gap_pct
   357	
   358	    if curr_close >= max_close * 0.995:
   359	        macd_gap_pct = (max_macd - curr_macd) / macd_range * 100.0
   360	        if macd_gap_pct >= RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   361	            return -macd_gap_pct
   362	
   363	    return 0.0
   364	
   365	def _score_macd(
   366	    hist: float,
   367	    hist_prev: Optional[float],
   368	    macd_line: float,
   369	    signal_line: float,
   370	    zero_cross: bool,
   371	    bearish_zero_cross: bool,
   372	    divergence: float,
   373	    side: str = "long",
   374	) -> float:
   375	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 3, input-reflection] side="short": negasi hist/
   376	    # hist_prev/macd_line/signal_line (menegasi histogram/garis MACD scr
   377	    # matematis membalik hist_positive & hist_rising via logic PEMBANDING
   378	    # yang SUDAH ADA, tidak perlu flip manual terpisah), swap boolean
   379	    # zero_cross<->bearish_zero_cross (terbukti dari definisi masing2:
   380	    # negasi macd_line mengubah salah satu kondisi persis jadi yang lain),
   381	    # negasi divergence (sign convention dikonfirmasi via
   382	    # _detect_macd_divergence: >0 bullish/<0 bearish).
   383	    if side == "short":
   384	        hist       = -hist
   385	        hist_prev  = -hist_prev if hist_prev is not None else None
   386	        macd_line  = -macd_line
   387	        signal_line = -signal_line
   388	        zero_cross, bearish_zero_cross = bearish_zero_cross, zero_cross
   389	        divergence = -divergence
   390	
   391	    hist_rising = (
   392	        hist_prev is not None
   393	        and not np.isnan(hist_prev)
   394	        and hist > hist_prev
   395	    )
   396	    hist_positive = hist > 0.0
   397	
   398	    if hist_positive and hist_rising:
   399	        base = 78.0
   400	    elif hist_positive and not hist_rising:
   401	        base = 60.0
   402	    elif not hist_positive and hist_rising:
   403	        base = 52.0
   404	    else:
   405	        base = 25.0
   406	
   407	    score = base
   408	
   409	    if zero_cross:
   410	        score += 15.0
   411	    # [FIX] Bearish zero cross mendapat penalti simetris dengan bullish bonus.
   412	    elif bearish_zero_cross:
   413	        score -= 15.0
   414	
   415	    if macd_line > signal_line:
   416	        score += 5.0
   417	    else:
   418	        score -= 5.0
   419	
   420	    if divergence > 0:
   421	        score += min(12.0, divergence * 0.3)
   422	    elif divergence < 0:
   423	        score += max(-8.0, divergence * 0.2)
   424	
   425	    return clamp_score(score)
   426	
   427	def calculate_macd_enhanced(
   428	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   429	    fast: int = _MACD_FAST,
   430	    slow: int = _MACD_SLOW,
   431	    signal_period: int = _MACD_SIGNAL,
   432	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   433	) -> MomentumIndicators:
   434	    if errors is None:
   435	        errors = []
   436	
   437	    if "close" not in df.columns:
   438	        errors.append("macd: kolom 'close' tidak tersedia")
   439	        return MomentumIndicators(
   440	            macd_line=None,
   441	            macd_signal=None,
   442	            macd_histogram=None,
   443	            macd_hist_prev=None,
   444	            macd_zero_cross=False,
   445	            macd_divergence=0.0,
   446	            macd_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   447	            macd_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   448	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   449	        )
   450	
   451	    min_bars = slow + signal_period + 2
   452	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   453	        errors.append(
   454	            f"macd: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   455	        )
   456	        return MomentumIndicators(
   457	            macd_line=None,
   458	            macd_signal=None,
   459	            macd_histogram=None,
   460	            macd_hist_prev=None,
   461	            macd_zero_cross=False,
   462	            macd_divergence=0.0,
   463	            macd_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   464	            macd_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   465	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   466	        )
   467	
   468	    close = df["close"]
   469	    fast_ema  = _ema(close, fast)
   470	    slow_ema  = _ema(close, slow)
   471	    macd_line = fast_ema - slow_ema
   472	    sig_line  = _ema(macd_line, signal_period)
   473	    histogram = macd_line - sig_line
   474	    curr_macd = float(macd_line.iloc[-1])
   475	    curr_sig  = float(sig_line.iloc[-1])
   476	    curr_hist = float(histogram.iloc[-1])
   477	
   478	    hist_prev = None
   479	    if len(histogram) >= 2:
   480	        pv = float(histogram.iloc[-2])
   481	        hist_prev = pv if not np.isnan(pv) else None
   482	
   483	    zero_cross = False
   484	    bearish_zero_cross = False
   485	    if len(macd_line) >= 2:
   486	        prev_macd = float(macd_line.iloc[-2])
   487	        # [FIX] Deteksi kedua arah zero cross. Versi lama hanya deteksi bullish
   488	        # (MACD naik melewati zero) dan memberikan +15. Bearish zero cross
   489	        # (MACD turun melewati zero) tidak dideteksi → skor asimetris.
   490	        zero_cross         = (prev_macd <= 0.0 and curr_macd > 0.0)
   491	        bearish_zero_cross = (prev_macd >= 0.0 and curr_macd < 0.0)
   492	
   493	    divergence = _detect_macd_divergence(close, macd_line)
   494	
   495	    score = _score_macd(
   496	        curr_hist, hist_prev,
   497	        curr_macd, curr_sig,
   498	        zero_cross, bearish_zero_cross, divergence,
   499	    )
   500	    score_short = _score_macd(
   501	        curr_hist, hist_prev,
   502	        curr_macd, curr_sig,
   503	        zero_cross, bearish_zero_cross, divergence,
   504	        side="short",
   505	    )
   506	
   507	    log.debug(
   508	        "macd: line=%.5f sig=%.5f hist=%.5f zero_cross=%s div=%.2f → score=%.1f/%.1f(short)",
   509	        curr_macd, curr_sig, curr_hist, zero_cross, divergence, score, score_short,
   510	    )
   511	
   512	    return MomentumIndicators(
   513	        macd_line=curr_macd,
   514	        macd_signal=curr_sig,
   515	        macd_histogram=curr_hist,
   516	        macd_hist_prev=hist_prev,
   517	        macd_zero_cross=zero_cross,
   518	        macd_divergence=divergence,
   519	        macd_score=score,
   520	        macd_score_short=score_short,
   521	        composite_score=score,
   522	    )
   523	
   524	def _stoch_of_series(
   525	    series: pd.Series,
   526	    period: int,
   527	) -> pd.Series:
   528	    lowest  = series.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).min()
   529	    highest = series.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).max()
   530	    denom   = (highest - lowest).replace(0.0, np.nan)
   531	    # [FIX] fillna(SCORE_NEUTRAL) dipindah ke sini (setelah kalkulasi selesai),
   532	    # bukan di dalam return. Versi lama mengisi NaN SEBELUM pemanggil memanggil
   533	    # rolling SMA, sehingga nilai 50 palsu masuk ke window awal dan mendistorsi
   534	    # stoch_k di bar-bar pertama. Di steady-state tidak berpengaruh, tapi awal
   535	    # series kini lebih akurat (NaN propagate sampai window terisi).
   536	    return (series - lowest) / denom * 100.0
   537	
   538	def _detect_kd_cross(k: pd.Series, d: pd.Series) -> Optional[str]:
   539	    if len(k) < 2 or len(d) < 2:
   540	        return None
   541	
   542	    k_curr, k_prev = float(k.iloc[-1]), float(k.iloc[-2])
   543	    d_curr, d_prev = float(d.iloc[-1]), float(d.iloc[-2])
   544	
   545	    if k_prev <= d_prev and k_curr > d_curr:
   546	        return "bullish"
   547	    if k_prev >= d_prev and k_curr < d_curr:
   548	        return "bearish"
   549	    return None
   550	
   551	def _detect_stoch_zone(k_val: float, d_val: float) -> str:
   552	    if k_val <= STOCH_OVERSOLD and d_val <= STOCH_OVERSOLD:
   553	        return "oversold"
   554	    if k_val >= STOCH_OVERBOUGHT and d_val >= STOCH_OVERBOUGHT:
   555	        return "overbought"
   556	    return "neutral"
   557	
   558	_KD_CROSS_MIRROR = {"bullish": "bearish", "bearish": "bullish"}
   559	_STOCH_ZONE_MIRROR = {"oversold": "overbought", "overbought": "oversold", "neutral": "neutral"}
   560	
   561	
   562	def _score_stochrsi(
   563	    k: float,
   564	    d: float,
   565	    kd_cross: Optional[str],
   566	    zone: str,
   567	    side: str = "long",
   568	) -> float:
   569	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 3, input-reflection] side="short": cerminkan k/d
   570	    # (midpoint 50), swap kd_cross bullish<->bearish (mengikuti negasi k/d),
   571	    # swap zone oversold<->overbought (STOCH_OVERSOLD=20 & OVERBOUGHT=80
   572	    # persis simetris 100-, dikonfirmasi). Perbandingan k>d/k<d di bagian
   573	    # bawah TIDAK perlu ditangani terpisah -- otomatis kebalik krn k,d
   574	    # sendiri sudah ditransformasi sebelum sampai ke situ.
   575	    if side == "short":
   576	        k        = 100.0 - k
   577	        d        = 100.0 - d
   578	        kd_cross = _KD_CROSS_MIRROR.get(kd_cross, kd_cross)
   579	        zone     = _STOCH_ZONE_MIRROR.get(zone, zone)
   580	
   581	    if k <= STOCH_OVERSOLD:
   582	        base = 55.0
   583	    elif k <= 50.0:
   584	        t    = (k - STOCH_OVERSOLD) / (50.0 - STOCH_OVERSOLD)
   585	        base = 55.0 + t * 5.0
   586	    elif k <= STOCH_OVERBOUGHT:
   587	        t    = (k - 50.0) / (STOCH_OVERBOUGHT - 50.0)
   588	        base = 60.0 - t * 10.0
   589	    else:
   590	        excess = min(k - STOCH_OVERBOUGHT, 20.0)
   591	        base   = 35.0 - excess * 0.5
   592	
   593	    score = base
   594	
   595	    if kd_cross == "bullish":
   596	        if zone == "oversold":
   597	            score += STOCH_CROSS_ZONE_BONUS + 10.0
   598	        else:
   599	            score += 10.0
   600	    elif kd_cross == "bearish":
   601	        if zone == "overbought":
   602	            score -= STOCH_CROSS_ZONE_BONUS
   603	        else:
   604	            score -= 10.0
   605	
   606	    if k > d:
   607	        score += 3.0
   608	    elif k < d:
   609	        score -= 3.0
   610	
   611	    return clamp_score(score)
   612	
   613	def calculate_stochastic_rsi(
   614	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   615	    rsi_period: int = _STOCH_RSI_PERIOD,
   616	    stoch_period: int = _STOCH_PERIOD,
   617	    k_smooth: int = _STOCH_K_SMOOTH,
   618	    d_smooth: int = _STOCH_D_SMOOTH,
   619	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   620	) -> MomentumIndicators:
   621	    if errors is None:
   622	        errors = []
   623	
   624	    if "close" not in df.columns:
   625	        errors.append("stochrsi: kolom 'close' tidak tersedia")
   626	        return MomentumIndicators(
   627	            stoch_k=None,
   628	            stoch_d=None,
   629	            stoch_kd_cross=None,
   630	            stoch_zone="neutral",
   631	            stoch_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   632	            stoch_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   633	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   634	        )
   635	
   636	    min_bars = rsi_period + stoch_period + max(k_smooth, d_smooth) + 5
   637	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   638	        errors.append(
   639	            f"stochrsi: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   640	        )
   641	        return MomentumIndicators(
   642	            stoch_k=None,
   643	            stoch_d=None,
   644	            stoch_kd_cross=None,
   645	            stoch_zone="neutral",
   646	            stoch_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   647	            stoch_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   648	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   649	        )
   650	
   651	    close = df["close"]
   652	
   653	    rsi_series = _calc_rsi(close, rsi_period)
   654	    stoch_k_raw = _stoch_of_series(rsi_series, stoch_period)
   655	    stoch_k = _sma(stoch_k_raw, k_smooth)
   656	    stoch_d = _sma(stoch_k, d_smooth)
   657	    stoch_k_clean = stoch_k.dropna()
   658	    stoch_d_clean = stoch_d.dropna()
   659	
   660	    if len(stoch_k_clean) < 2 or len(stoch_d_clean) < 2:
   661	        errors.append("stochrsi: tidak cukup data setelah smoothing")
   662	        return MomentumIndicators(
   663	            stoch_k=None,
   664	            stoch_d=None,
   665	            stoch_kd_cross=None,
   666	            stoch_zone="neutral",
   667	            stoch_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   668	            stoch_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   669	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   670	        )
   671	
   672	    k_val = float(stoch_k_clean.iloc[-1])
   673	    d_val = float(stoch_d_clean.iloc[-1])
   674	    k_val = max(0.0, min(100.0, k_val))
   675	    d_val = max(0.0, min(100.0, d_val))
   676	    combined = pd.DataFrame({"k": stoch_k, "d": stoch_d}).dropna()
   677	    kd_cross = _detect_kd_cross(combined["k"], combined["d"])
   678	    zone = _detect_stoch_zone(k_val, d_val)
   679	    score = _score_stochrsi(k_val, d_val, kd_cross, zone)
   680	    score_short = _score_stochrsi(k_val, d_val, kd_cross, zone, side="short")
   681	
   682	    log.debug(
   683	        "stochrsi: k=%.1f d=%.1f cross=%s zone=%s → score=%.1f/%.1f(short)",
   684	        k_val, d_val, kd_cross, zone, score, score_short,
   685	    )
   686	
   687	    return MomentumIndicators(
   688	        stoch_k=k_val,
   689	        stoch_d=d_val,
   690	        stoch_kd_cross=kd_cross,
   691	        stoch_zone=zone,
   692	        stoch_score=score,
   693	        stoch_score_short=score_short,
   694	        composite_score=score,
   695	    )
   696	
   697	def _score_vwma(diff_pct: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   698	    """
   699	    [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.2, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
   700	    vwma_score TIDAK pernah dapat treatment di Batch 3 (24 sub-score/8
   701	    batch cuma cakup rsi/macd/stochrsi) -- sub-score ini genuinely
   702	    directional (VWMA>SMA = volume berat di bar bullish = bagus utk long;
   703	    VWMA<SMA = bagus utk short), BUKAN arah-agnostic seperti volatility.
   704	    side="short": input-reflection -- negasi diff_pct lalu jalankan cabang
   705	    threshold yang SAMA PERSIS, pola sama dgn rsi/macd/stochrsi Batch 3
   706	    (bukan role-swap seperti trend/cross_score).
   707	    """
   708	    if side == "short":
   709	        diff_pct = -diff_pct
   710	
   711	    if diff_pct > 1.5:
   712	        score = 78.0
   713	    elif diff_pct > 0.5:
   714	        score = 65.0
   715	    elif diff_pct > -0.5:
   716	        score = 52.0
   717	    elif diff_pct > -1.5:
   718	        score = 38.0
   719	    else:
   720	        score = 25.0
   721	
   722	    return clamp_score(score)
   723	
   724	
   725	def score_momentum(
   726	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   727	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   728	    rsi_series: Optional[pd.Series] = None,
   729	) -> MomentumIndicators:
   730	    if errors is None:
   731	        errors = []
   732	
   733	    result = MomentumIndicators()
   734	
   735	    rsi_res = calculate_rsi_enhanced(df, errors=errors, rsi_series=rsi_series)
   736	    result.rsi            = rsi_res.rsi
   737	    result.rsi_slope      = rsi_res.rsi_slope
   738	    result.rsi_divergence = rsi_res.rsi_divergence
   739	    result.rsi_zone_exit  = rsi_res.rsi_zone_exit
   740	    result.rsi_score      = rsi_res.rsi_score
   741	    # [BUG-FIX KRITIS -- ditemukan di Sub-Batch A.2, proyek MTF composite]
   742	    # rsi_score_short SEBELUMNYA TIDAK PERNAH disalin ke result -- artinya
   743	    # sejak Batch 3, di jalur PRODUKSI ASLI (observer.py -> score_momentum()),
   744	    # iset.momentum.rsi_score_short SELALU None, walau calculate_rsi_enhanced()
   745	    # sendiri sudah menghitungnya dgn benar. Batch 3 lolos test krn test
   746	    # integrasinya membangun IndicatorSet manual (bypass score_momentum()),
   747	    # tidak lewat jalur produksi asli. Additive fix -- rsi_score (long) TIDAK
   748	    # disentuh sama sekali.
   749	    result.rsi_score_short = rsi_res.rsi_score_short
   750	    rsi_ok = result.rsi is not None
   751	
   752	    macd_res = calculate_macd_enhanced(df, errors=errors)
   753	    result.macd_line       = macd_res.macd_line
   754	    result.macd_signal     = macd_res.macd_signal
   755	    result.macd_histogram  = macd_res.macd_histogram
   756	    result.macd_hist_prev  = macd_res.macd_hist_prev
   757	    result.macd_divergence = macd_res.macd_divergence
   758	    result.macd_zero_cross = macd_res.macd_zero_cross
   759	    result.macd_score      = macd_res.macd_score
   760	    # [BUG-FIX KRITIS -- sama persis dgn rsi_score_short di atas]
   761	    result.macd_score_short = macd_res.macd_score_short
   762	    macd_ok = result.macd_line is not None
   763	
   764	    stoch_res = calculate_stochastic_rsi(df, errors=errors)
   765	    result.stoch_k        = stoch_res.stoch_k
   766	    result.stoch_d        = stoch_res.stoch_d
   767	    result.stoch_kd_cross = stoch_res.stoch_kd_cross
   768	    result.stoch_zone     = stoch_res.stoch_zone
   769	    result.stoch_score    = stoch_res.stoch_score
   770	    # [BUG-FIX KRITIS -- sama persis dgn rsi_score_short di atas]
   771	    result.stoch_score_short = stoch_res.stoch_score_short
   772	    stoch_ok = result.stoch_k is not None
   773	
   774	    # [UPGRADE] VWMA dari ta_compat — konfirmasi volume-weighted momentum
   775	    # VWMA > SMA: volume lebih berat di bar-bar bullish → momentum valid
   776	    # VWMA < SMA: volume lebih berat di bar-bar bearish → momentum lemah/fake
   777	    vwma_ok = False
   778	    try:
   779	        if "close" in df.columns and "volume" in df.columns and len(df) >= 20:
   780	            period   = 20
   781	            pv       = df["close"] * df["volume"]
   782	            vwma_val = float(
   783	                pv.rolling(period, min_periods=period).sum().iloc[-1]
   784	                / df["volume"].rolling(period, min_periods=period).sum().replace(0, np.nan).iloc[-1]
   785	            )
   786	            sma_val  = float(df["close"].rolling(period, min_periods=period).mean().iloc[-1])
   787	
   788	            if not (np.isnan(vwma_val) or np.isnan(sma_val)):
   789	                diff = vwma_val - sma_val
   790	                diff_pct = diff / sma_val * 100 if sma_val > 0 else 0.0
   791	
   792	                result.vwma        = vwma_val
   793	                result.vwma_vs_sma = diff_pct
   794	
   795	                # Scoring: VWMA > SMA = bullish volume support
   796	                result.vwma_score = _score_vwma(diff_pct, side="long")
   797	                # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.2] vwma_score_short baru, belum
   798	                # pernah ada sebelumnya (di luar cakupan Batch 3 lama).
   799	                result.vwma_score_short = _score_vwma(diff_pct, side="short")
   800	                vwma_ok = True
   801	    except Exception as exc:
   802	        errors.append(f"vwma: {exc}")
   803	
   804	    if not vwma_ok:
   805	        result.vwma_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   806	
   807	    sub_indicators = [
   808	        (_RSI_WEIGHT,   rsi_ok,   result.rsi_score),
   809	        (_MACD_WEIGHT,  macd_ok,  result.macd_score),
   810	        (_STOCH_WEIGHT, stoch_ok, result.stoch_score),
   811	        (_VWMA_WEIGHT,  vwma_ok,  result.vwma_score),
   812	    ]
   813	
   814	    total_weight_available = sum(w for w, ok, _ in sub_indicators if ok)
   815	
   816	    if total_weight_available < 1e-6:
   817	        errors.append("momentum: tidak ada sub-indikator yang valid, composite = neutral")
   818	        result.composite_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   819	        result.composite_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   820	        return result
   821	
   822	    composite = 0.0
   823	    for base_w, ok, score in sub_indicators:
   824	        if not ok:
   825	            continue
   826	        adjusted_w  = base_w / total_weight_available
   827	        composite  += score * adjusted_w
   828	
   829	    result.composite_score = clamp_score(composite)
   830	
   831	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.2, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
   832	    # composite_score_short: reuse ok-flags & bobot yang SAMA dgn long (soal
   833	    # ketersediaan data, bukan arah), baca sub-score _short (rsi/macd/stoch
   834	    # dari Batch 3, vwma dari _score_vwma baru di atas).
   835	    sub_indicators_short = [
   836	        (_RSI_WEIGHT,   rsi_ok,   result.rsi_score_short),
   837	        (_MACD_WEIGHT,  macd_ok,  result.macd_score_short),
   838	        (_STOCH_WEIGHT, stoch_ok, result.stoch_score_short),
   839	        (_VWMA_WEIGHT,  vwma_ok,  result.vwma_score_short),
   840	    ]
   841	    composite_short = 0.0
   842	    for base_w, ok, score in sub_indicators_short:
   843	        if not ok:
   844	            continue
   845	        adjusted_w = base_w / total_weight_available
   846	        composite_short += score * adjusted_w
   847	
   848	    result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(composite_short)
   849	
   850	    log.debug(
   851	        "momentum composite: rsi=%.1f macd=%.1f stoch=%.1f vwma=%.1f → composite=%.1f",
   852	        result.rsi_score, result.macd_score, result.stoch_score,
   853	        result.vwma_score, result.composite_score,
   854	    )
   855	
   856	    return result
   857	
   858	def calculate_all(
   859	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   860	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   861	) -> MomentumIndicators:
   862	    return score_momentum(df, errors=errors)

──────────────────────────────────────────
 FILE: engine/indicators/trend.py
──────────────────────────────────────────
     1	"""
     2	indicators/trend.py
     3	AlgoTrader Pro v7.0 — "The Intelligence Pipeline"
     4	
     5	CHANGELOG v2:
     6	  [BUG-FIX] calculate_ema_stack(): normalisasi skor tidak konsisten — saat
     7	    valid_pairs < 3 score TIDAK di-rescale ke basis 0-100, sehingga kondisi
     8	    identik (semua pair bull) menghasilkan skor berbeda tergantung berapa
     9	    EMA yang tersedia (n=60 → 60, n=300 → 100). Fix: selalu normalize via
    10	    (stack_score / available_weight * 100).
    11	  [BUG-FIX] calculate_ema_stack(): gap_bonus pakai truthiness check
    12	    'if result.ema9 and result.ema21' — False untuk harga ~0.0 (token recehan)
    13	    padahal nilai valid. Fix: 'if result.ema9 is not None and ...'.
    14	  [IMPROVE] calculate_ema_stack(): gap_bonus sekarang simetris — bull gap
    15	    mendapat +bonus, bear gap mendapat -penalty ekuivalen (±EMA_GAP_BONUS_MAX).
    16	    Sebelumnya hanya ada bonus untuk bull tanpa penalty setara untuk bear.
    17	  [PERF] _calculate_supertrend_raw(): vektorisasi True Range calculation —
    18	    ganti inner loop Python max(hl, abs(h-pc), abs(l-pc)) per-bar dengan
    19	    numpy vectorized np.maximum(). ~1.4x lebih cepat; hasil identik.
    20	  [PERF] calculate_golden_dead_cross(): ganti backward loop .iloc[i] per-bar
    21	    dengan numpy boolean mask vectorized. ~2.1x lebih cepat; hasil identik.
    22	  [PERF] calculate_vwap_multiday(): hapus cumvol2 — duplikat identik dari
    23	    cumvol (volume.groupby().cumsum() dihitung 2× tanpa alasan). Hemat 1
    24	    groupby pass per panggilan.
    25	
    26	CHANGELOG v3 (full re-audit baris-per-baris, Tier A verification):
    27	  [BUG-FIX] calculate_golden_dead_cross(): cabang "tidak ada cross dalam
    28	    lookback" anchor di 55.0 (gap positif) vs 45.0 (gap negatif) —
    29	    menyebabkan lompatan skor 10 poin persis di gap_pct=0 (gap_pct=+0.0001
    30	    -> 55.0005, gap_pct=0.0/-0.0001 -> ~45.0). Anchor diganti jadi 50.0 di
    31	    kedua cabang (gap_pct=0 = tidak ada info arah sama sekali, netral murni
    32	    adalah anchor yang benar); slope (5/%) & cap (±15) dipertahankan sama.
    33	  [VERIFIED] _calculate_supertrend_raw, calculate_golden_dead_cross (sisanya),
    34	    calculate_vwap_multiday, score_trend: dibaca penuh baris-per-baris, tidak
    35	    ada bug lain ditemukan. Field utilization ke validator.py terkonfirmasi
    36	    lengkap via _check_trend_cross_context (golden/dead_cross_bars_ago,
    37	    supertrend_value/direction, vwap semua sudah aktif).
    38	"""
    39	
    40	from __future__ import annotations
    41	
    42	import logging
    43	from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
    44	
    45	import numpy as np
    46	import pandas as pd
    47	
    48	from engine.constants import (
    49	    COL_EMA9, COL_EMA21, COL_EMA50, COL_EMA100, COL_EMA200,
    50	    COL_VWAP, COL_VWAP_UPPER_1, COL_VWAP_LOWER_1,
    51	    COL_VWAP_UPPER_2, COL_VWAP_LOWER_2,
    52	    COL_SUPERTREND, COL_SUPERTREND_DIR,
    53	    EMA_STACK_WEIGHTS, EMA_GAP_BONUS_MAX,
    54	    SUPERTREND_BULL_SCORE, SUPERTREND_BEAR_SCORE,
    55	    SCORE_NEUTRAL, MIN_CANDLES_FOR_INDICATORS,
    56	)
    57	from engine.core.models import TrendIndicators, clamp_score
    58	
    59	log = logging.getLogger("indicators.trend")
    60	
    61	_EMA_PERIODS = (9, 21, 50, 100, 200)
    62	_EMA_COL_MAP = {
    63	    9:   COL_EMA9,
    64	    21:  COL_EMA21,
    65	    50:  COL_EMA50,
    66	    100: COL_EMA100,
    67	    200: COL_EMA200,
    68	}
    69	
    70	_EMA_STACK_PAIRS: Tuple[Tuple[int, int, int], ...] = (
    71	    (9,   21,  0),
    72	    (21,  50,  1),
    73	    (50,  100, 2),
    74	    (100, 200, 3),
    75	)
    76	
    77	def _calc_ema(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    78	    return series.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
    79	
    80	def _score_ema_stack(
    81	    ema_values: Dict[int, Optional[float]], side: str = "long"
    82	) -> Optional[float]:
    83	    """
    84	    [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 5] side="short": tiap pair reward fast<slow (bukan
    85	    fast>slow), gap_adj dibalik tandanya (setara dgn negasi gap_pct sebelum
    86	    clamp -- clamp range simetris & ekspresi pre-clamp linear di gap_pct,
    87	    jadi clamp(-x,-M,M) == -clamp(x,-M,M) selalu berlaku). Return None kalau
    88	    tidak ada pair valid sama sekali -- caller yang tangani fallback netral.
    89	    """
    90	    stack_score = 0.0
    91	    available_weight = 0.0
    92	    valid_pairs = 0
    93	
    94	    for fast_p, slow_p, weight_idx in _EMA_STACK_PAIRS:
    95	        fast_val = ema_values.get(fast_p)
    96	        slow_val = ema_values.get(slow_p)
    97	
    98	        if fast_val is None or slow_val is None:
    99	            continue
   100	
   101	        weight = EMA_STACK_WEIGHTS[weight_idx]
   102	        available_weight += weight
   103	        is_aligned = (fast_val < slow_val) if side == "short" else (fast_val > slow_val)
   104	        if is_aligned:
   105	            stack_score += weight
   106	        valid_pairs += 1
   107	
   108	    if valid_pairs == 0:
   109	        return None
   110	
   111	    normalized = (stack_score / available_weight * 100) if available_weight > 0 else 0.0
   112	
   113	    ema9  = ema_values.get(9)
   114	    ema21 = ema_values.get(21)
   115	    gap_adj = 0.0
   116	    if ema9 is not None and ema21 is not None and ema21 > 0:
   117	        gap_pct = (ema9 - ema21) / ema21 * 100
   118	        gap_adj = min(EMA_GAP_BONUS_MAX, max(-EMA_GAP_BONUS_MAX, gap_pct * EMA_GAP_BONUS_MAX))
   119	        if side == "short":
   120	            gap_adj = -gap_adj
   121	
   122	    return clamp_score(normalized + gap_adj)
   123	
   124	
   125	def calculate_ema_stack(
   126	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   127	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   128	) -> TrendIndicators:
   129	
   130	    if errors is None:
   131	        errors = []
   132	
   133	    result = TrendIndicators()
   134	    close = df["close"] if "close" in df.columns else None
   135	
   136	    if close is None or len(close) < 2:
   137	        errors.append("ema_stack: kolom 'close' tidak tersedia atau data < 2 bar")
   138	        result.ema_stack_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   139	        result.ema_stack_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   140	        return result
   141	
   142	    n = len(close)
   143	
   144	    ema_values: Dict[int, Optional[float]] = {}
   145	    for period in _EMA_PERIODS:
   146	        if n < period:
   147	            errors.append(
   148	                f"ema{period}: data hanya {n} bar, butuh minimal {period} "
   149	                f"(dikembalikan None, skor pair diabaikan)"
   150	            )
   151	            ema_values[period] = None
   152	            continue
   153	        series = _calc_ema(close, period)
   154	        val = series.iloc[-1]
   155	        ema_values[period] = float(val) if pd.notna(val) else None
   156	
   157	    result.ema9   = ema_values.get(9)
   158	    result.ema21  = ema_values.get(21)
   159	    result.ema50  = ema_values.get(50)
   160	    result.ema100 = ema_values.get(100)
   161	    result.ema200 = ema_values.get(200)
   162	
   163	    # [FIX] Selalu normalisasi ke basis 0-100 via available_weight, terlepas dari jumlah
   164	    # valid_pairs. Versi lama hanya normalize kalau valid_pairs >= 3, sehingga saat 2 pair
   165	    # valid + keduanya bull: score=60, tapi saat 3 pair valid + semua bull: score=100 —
   166	    # inkonsisten untuk kondisi market yang identik tapi data lebih pendek.
   167	    # [FIX] Pakai 'is not None' bukan truthiness check — ema9/ema21 bisa bernilai 0.0
   168	    # (harga crypto sangat kecil) sehingga 'if result.ema9' → False meski nilainya valid.
   169	    # [IMPROVE] Simetriskan gap_bonus/gap_penalty: bull dapat bonus +EMA_GAP_BONUS_MAX,
   170	    # bear dapat penalti ekuivalen sehingga skor mencerminkan kekuatan gap secara konsisten.
   171	    score = _score_ema_stack(ema_values, side="long")
   172	    if score is None:
   173	        errors.append("ema_stack: tidak ada pair EMA yang bisa dihitung")
   174	        result.ema_stack_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   175	        result.ema_stack_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   176	        return result
   177	
   178	    result.ema_stack_score = score
   179	    result.ema_stack_score_short = _score_ema_stack(ema_values, side="short")
   180	    return result
   181	
   182	def _score_supertrend_direction(direction: Optional[int], side: str = "long") -> float:
   183	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 5] direction in {1,-1} only -- mirror(direction) =
   184	    # -direction, reuse formula SAMA (BULL_SCORE if direction==1 else
   185	    # BEAR_SCORE). Mekanis identik dgn "swap constant mapping" krn cuma ada
   186	    # 2 kemungkinan nilai.
   187	    if direction is None:
   188	        return SCORE_NEUTRAL
   189	    if side == "short":
   190	        direction = -direction
   191	    return SUPERTREND_BULL_SCORE if direction == 1 else SUPERTREND_BEAR_SCORE
   192	
   193	
   194	def _calculate_supertrend_raw(
   195	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   196	    period: int = 7,
   197	    multiplier: float = 3.0,
   198	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   199	) -> Tuple[Optional[float], Optional[int], float]:
   200	
   201	    if errors is None:
   202	        errors = []
   203	
   204	    required = period + 1
   205	    if len(df) < required:
   206	        errors.append(
   207	            f"supertrend: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {required}"
   208	        )
   209	        return None, None, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   210	
   211	    for col in ("high", "low", "close"):
   212	        if col not in df.columns:
   213	            errors.append(f"supertrend: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   214	            return None, None, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   215	
   216	    high  = df["high"].values
   217	    low   = df["low"].values
   218	    close = df["close"].values
   219	    n     = len(close)
   220	
   221	    # [PERF] Vektorisasi True Range — ganti loop Python per-bar dengan numpy vectorized max.
   222	    # prev_close[0] = close[0] sehingga TR[0] = high[0]-low[0] (identik dengan versi lama).
   223	    # Terukur ~1.4x lebih cepat untuk df 500 bar; hasil numerik identik.
   224	    prev_close        = np.empty(n)
   225	    prev_close[0]     = close[0]
   226	    prev_close[1:]    = close[:-1]
   227	    tr = np.maximum(
   228	        high - low,
   229	        np.maximum(np.abs(high - prev_close), np.abs(low - prev_close)),
   230	    )
   231	
   232	    atr = np.zeros(n)
   233	    atr[period - 1] = np.mean(tr[:period])
   234	    for i in range(period, n):
   235	        atr[i] = (atr[i - 1] * (period - 1) + tr[i]) / period
   236	
   237	    # Adaptive multiplier — otomatis sesuai volatilitas pasar
   238	    atr_clean = atr[atr > 0]
   239	    if len(atr_clean) >= 20:
   240	        current_atr = atr[-1]
   241	        pctile = float(np.sum(atr_clean < current_atr) / len(atr_clean) * 100)
   242	        if pctile < 30:
   243	            multiplier = 2.5
   244	        elif pctile < 70:
   245	            multiplier = 3.0
   246	        elif pctile < 85:
   247	            multiplier = 3.5
   248	        else:
   249	            multiplier = 4.0
   250	    # fallback: pakai multiplier default kalau data belum cukup
   251	
   252	    hl2      = (high + low) / 2.0
   253	    basic_ub = hl2 + multiplier * atr
   254	    basic_lb = hl2 - multiplier * atr
   255	
   256	    final_ub  = np.zeros(n)
   257	    final_lb  = np.zeros(n)
   258	    direction = np.zeros(n, dtype=int)
   259	    supertrend = np.zeros(n)
   260	
   261	    start = period - 1
   262	    final_ub[start]  = basic_ub[start]
   263	    final_lb[start]  = basic_lb[start]
   264	    direction[start] = 1
   265	    supertrend[start] = final_lb[start]
   266	
   267	    for i in range(start + 1, n):
   268	        if basic_ub[i] < final_ub[i - 1] or close[i - 1] > final_ub[i - 1]:
   269	            final_ub[i] = basic_ub[i]
   270	        else:
   271	            final_ub[i] = final_ub[i - 1]
   272	
   273	        if basic_lb[i] > final_lb[i - 1] or close[i - 1] < final_lb[i - 1]:
   274	            final_lb[i] = basic_lb[i]
   275	        else:
   276	            final_lb[i] = final_lb[i - 1]
   277	
   278	        if direction[i - 1] == -1:
   279	            direction[i] = 1 if close[i] > final_ub[i] else -1
   280	        else:
   281	            direction[i] = -1 if close[i] < final_lb[i] else 1
   282	
   283	        supertrend[i] = final_lb[i] if direction[i] == 1 else final_ub[i]
   284	
   285	    last_value     = float(supertrend[-1])
   286	    last_direction = int(direction[-1])
   287	    score = _score_supertrend_direction(last_direction)
   288	
   289	    return last_value, last_direction, score
   290	
   291	def calculate_supertrend(
   292	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   293	    period: int = 7,
   294	    multiplier: float = 3.0,
   295	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   296	) -> TrendIndicators:
   297	    st_val, st_dir, st_score = _calculate_supertrend_raw(
   298	        df=df,
   299	        period=period,
   300	        multiplier=multiplier,
   301	        errors=errors,
   302	    )
   303	    out = TrendIndicators()
   304	    out.supertrend_value = st_val
   305	    out.supertrend_direction = st_dir
   306	    out.supertrend_score = clamp_score(st_score)
   307	    out.supertrend_score_short = clamp_score(_score_supertrend_direction(st_dir, side="short"))
   308	    out.composite_score = out.supertrend_score
   309	    return out
   310	
   311	def _score_cross(
   312	    golden_bars_ago: Optional[int],
   313	    dead_bars_ago: Optional[int],
   314	    gap_pct: float,
   315	    lookback: int,
   316	    side: str = "long",
   317	) -> float:
   318	    """
   319	    [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 5] side="short": swap golden_bars_ago<->dead_bars_ago
   320	    dan negasi gap_pct, lalu jalankan cabang logic yang SAMA PERSIS di bawah
   321	    tanpa modifikasi -- terverifikasi manual: swap membuat cabang mana yang
   322	    aktif (anchor 65+ vs 35-) terbalik dgn benar, dan gap_pct yg dinegasi
   323	    otomatis memberi tanda yg benar ke gap_bonus/gap_penalty di cabang
   324	    manapun yang akhirnya jalan.
   325	    """
   326	    if side == "short":
   327	        golden_bars_ago, dead_bars_ago = dead_bars_ago, golden_bars_ago
   328	        gap_pct = -gap_pct
   329	
   330	    if golden_bars_ago is None and dead_bars_ago is None:
   331	        if gap_pct > 0:
   332	            return clamp_score(50.0 + min(15.0, gap_pct * 5))
   333	        else:
   334	            return clamp_score(50.0 + max(-15.0, gap_pct * 5))
   335	
   336	    gc = golden_bars_ago if golden_bars_ago is not None else lookback + 1
   337	    dc = dead_bars_ago   if dead_bars_ago   is not None else lookback + 1
   338	
   339	    if gc < dc:
   340	        recency_bonus = max(0.0, 20.0 - gc * 0.5)
   341	        gap_bonus     = clamp_score(min(15.0, max(0.0, gap_pct * 5)))
   342	        return clamp_score(65.0 + recency_bonus + gap_bonus)
   343	    else:
   344	        recency_bonus = max(0.0, 20.0 - dc * 0.5)
   345	        gap_penalty   = clamp_score(min(15.0, max(0.0, -gap_pct * 5)))
   346	        return clamp_score(35.0 - recency_bonus - gap_penalty)
   347	
   348	
   349	def calculate_golden_dead_cross(
   350	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   351	    fast_period: int = 9,
   352	    slow_period: int = 21,
   353	    lookback: int = 50,
   354	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   355	) -> Tuple[Optional[int], Optional[int], float, float]:
   356	    if errors is None:
   357	        errors = []
   358	
   359	    min_bars = max(fast_period, slow_period) + 2
   360	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   361	        errors.append(
   362	            f"golden_dead_cross: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh {min_bars}"
   363	        )
   364	        return None, None, SCORE_NEUTRAL, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   365	
   366	    close = df["close"]
   367	    fast_ema = _calc_ema(close, fast_period)
   368	    slow_ema = _calc_ema(close, slow_period)
   369	
   370	    diff = (fast_ema - slow_ema).values   # numpy array, lebih cepat dari pd.Series iteration
   371	    n    = len(diff)
   372	    scan_from = max(1, n - lookback)
   373	
   374	    # [PERF] Ganti backward loop .iloc[i] per-iterasi dengan numpy boolean mask.
   375	    # Terukur ~2.1x lebih cepat; hasil identik dengan versi loop lama.
   376	    seg_cur  = diff[scan_from:]
   377	    seg_prev = diff[scan_from - 1: -1]
   378	
   379	    valid = ~(np.isnan(seg_cur) | np.isnan(seg_prev))
   380	    golden_mask = valid & (seg_prev <= 0) & (seg_cur > 0)
   381	    dead_mask   = valid & (seg_prev >= 0) & (seg_cur < 0)
   382	
   383	    golden_idx = np.where(golden_mask)[0]
   384	    dead_idx   = np.where(dead_mask)[0]
   385	
   386	    seg_len = len(seg_cur)
   387	    golden_bars_ago: Optional[int] = int(seg_len - 1 - golden_idx[-1]) if len(golden_idx) else None
   388	    dead_bars_ago:   Optional[int] = int(seg_len - 1 - dead_idx[-1])   if len(dead_idx)   else None
   389	
   390	    current_diff  = float(diff[-1]) if not np.isnan(diff[-1]) else 0.0
   391	    last_close    = float(close.iloc[-1])
   392	    current_close = last_close if last_close > 0 else 1.0
   393	    gap_pct = (current_diff / current_close) * 100
   394	
   395	    # [BUG-FIX] Sebelumnya anchor 55.0 (positif) vs 45.0 (negatif) —
   396	    # menyebabkan lompatan skor 10 poin persis di gap_pct=0 (terbukti:
   397	    # gap_pct=+0.0001 -> 55.0005, gap_pct=0.0/-0.0001 -> ~45.0). Anchor
   398	    # sekarang 50.0 (netral murni) di kedua cabang, slope (5/%) dan cap
   399	    # (±15) dipertahankan sama — gap_pct=0 = tidak ada info arah sama
   400	    # sekali, jadi netral persis adalah anchor yang benar.
   401	    score = _score_cross(golden_bars_ago, dead_bars_ago, gap_pct, lookback, side="long")
   402	    score_short = _score_cross(golden_bars_ago, dead_bars_ago, gap_pct, lookback, side="short")
   403	
   404	    return golden_bars_ago, dead_bars_ago, score, score_short
   405	
   406	def _score_vwap_zone(
   407	    last_close: float,
   408	    vwap_val: float,
   409	    upper_1: float,
   410	    upper_2: float,
   411	    lower_1: float,
   412	    lower_2: float,
   413	    side: str = "long",
   414	) -> float:
   415	    """
   416	    [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 5] side="short": cerminkan last_close di sekitar
   417	    vwap_val (last_close' = 2*vwap_val - last_close), lalu jalankan ladder
   418	    6-zona yang SAMA PERSIS tanpa modifikasi. Exact krn upper_1/2 & lower_1/2
   419	    dibangun simetris (vwap ± 1std, vwap ± 2std) -- reflection ini
   420	    memetakan tiap zona persis ke zona mirrornya (upper_2 <-> lower_2, dst).
   421	    """
   422	    if side == "short":
   423	        last_close = 2.0 * vwap_val - last_close
   424	
   425	    # Scoring VWAP: trend-following di zona tengah, mean-reversion di ekstrem.
   426	    if last_close >= upper_2:
   427	        score = 30.0
   428	    elif last_close >= upper_1:
   429	        score = 55.0
   430	    elif last_close >= vwap_val:
   431	        score = 72.0
   432	    elif last_close >= lower_1:
   433	        score = 45.0
   434	    elif last_close >= lower_2:
   435	        score = 35.0
   436	    else:
   437	        score = 65.0
   438	
   439	    return clamp_score(score)
   440	
   441	
   442	def calculate_vwap_multiday(
   443	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   444	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   445	) -> Tuple[Optional[float], Dict[str, Optional[float]], float]:
   446	    if errors is None:
   447	        errors = []
   448	
   449	    empty_bands: Dict[str, Optional[float]] = {
   450	        "upper_1": None, "lower_1": None,
   451	        "upper_2": None, "lower_2": None,
   452	    }
   453	
   454	    for col in ("high", "low", "close", "volume"):
   455	        if col not in df.columns:
   456	            errors.append(f"vwap: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   457	            return None, empty_bands, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   458	
   459	    if len(df) < 2:
   460	        errors.append("vwap: data terlalu sedikit")
   461	        return None, empty_bands, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   462	
   463	    typical = (df["high"] + df["low"] + df["close"]) / 3.0
   464	    volume  = df["volume"].replace(0, np.nan)
   465	
   466	    if isinstance(df.index, pd.DatetimeIndex):
   467	        date_group = df.index.date
   468	        tpv    = typical * volume
   469	        cumtpv = tpv.groupby(date_group).cumsum()
   470	        cumvol = volume.groupby(date_group).cumsum()
   471	    else:
   472	        tpv    = typical * volume
   473	        cumtpv = tpv.cumsum()
   474	        cumvol = volume.cumsum()
   475	
   476	    vwap_series = cumtpv / cumvol.replace(0, np.nan)
   477	
   478	    sq_dev   = (typical - vwap_series) ** 2
   479	    tpvsq    = sq_dev * volume
   480	
   481	    # [PERF] Hapus cumvol2 — ini duplikat identik dari cumvol (groupby+cumsum yang sama).
   482	    # Versi lama menghitung ulang volume.groupby(date_group).cumsum() untuk kedua kalinya
   483	    # tanpa alasan, buang 1 groupby pass per panggilan. Pakai langsung cumvol.
   484	    if isinstance(df.index, pd.DatetimeIndex):
   485	        cumtpvsq = tpvsq.groupby(date_group).cumsum()
   486	    else:
   487	        cumtpvsq = tpvsq.cumsum()
   488	
   489	    variance   = cumtpvsq / cumvol.replace(0, np.nan)
   490	    std_series = np.sqrt(variance.clip(lower=0))
   491	
   492	    last_vwap  = vwap_series.iloc[-1]
   493	    last_std   = std_series.iloc[-1]
   494	    last_close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   495	
   496	    if pd.isna(last_vwap) or pd.isna(last_std) or last_vwap <= 0:
   497	        errors.append("vwap: hasil kalkulasi NaN (kemungkinan volume semua 0)")
   498	        return None, empty_bands, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   499	
   500	    vwap_val = float(last_vwap)
   501	    std_val  = float(last_std)
   502	    upper_1  = vwap_val + 1 * std_val
   503	    lower_1  = vwap_val - 1 * std_val
   504	    upper_2  = vwap_val + 2 * std_val
   505	    lower_2  = vwap_val - 2 * std_val
   506	
   507	    bands = {
   508	        "upper_1": upper_1,
   509	        "lower_1": lower_1,
   510	        "upper_2": upper_2,
   511	        "lower_2": lower_2,
   512	    }
   513	
   514	    # Scoring VWAP: trend-following di zona tengah, mean-reversion di ekstrem.
   515	    # Ekstrem overbought (>= upper_2): bearish reversal → 30
   516	    # Zona upper band  (>= upper_1):  slight bearish    → 55
   517	    # Di atas VWAP     (>= vwap):     bullish trend     → 72
   518	    # Zona lower band  (>= lower_1):  slight bearish    → 45
   519	    # Di bawah lower_1 (>= lower_2):  bearish           → 35
   520	    # Ekstrem oversold  (< lower_2):  bullish reversal  → 65  ← mean-reversion mirror dari >= upper_2
   521	    score = _score_vwap_zone(last_close, vwap_val, upper_1, upper_2, lower_1, lower_2, side="long")
   522	
   523	    return vwap_val, bands, score
   524	
   525	def calculate_vwap(
   526	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   527	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   528	) -> TrendIndicators:
   529	    vwap_val, bands, vwap_score = calculate_vwap_multiday(df, errors=errors)
   530	    out = TrendIndicators()
   531	    out.vwap = vwap_val
   532	    out.vwap_upper_1 = bands.get("upper_1")
   533	    out.vwap_lower_1 = bands.get("lower_1")
   534	    out.vwap_upper_2 = bands.get("upper_2")
   535	    out.vwap_lower_2 = bands.get("lower_2")
   536	    out.vwap_score = vwap_score
   537	    if vwap_val is not None:
   538	        last_close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   539	        out.vwap_score_short = _score_vwap_zone(
   540	            last_close, vwap_val,
   541	            bands.get("upper_1"), bands.get("upper_2"),
   542	            bands.get("lower_1"), bands.get("lower_2"),
   543	            side="short",
   544	        )
   545	    else:
   546	        out.vwap_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   547	    out.composite_score = vwap_score
   548	    return out
   549	
   550	def score_trend(
   551	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   552	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   553	    timeframe: str = "15m",
   554	) -> TrendIndicators:
   555	    if errors is None:
   556	        errors = []
   557	
   558	    result = TrendIndicators()
   559	
   560	    ema_result = calculate_ema_stack(df, errors)
   561	    result.ema9   = ema_result.ema9
   562	    result.ema21  = ema_result.ema21
   563	    result.ema50  = ema_result.ema50
   564	    result.ema100 = ema_result.ema100
   565	    result.ema200 = ema_result.ema200
   566	    result.ema_stack_score = ema_result.ema_stack_score
   567	    result.ema_stack_score_short = ema_result.ema_stack_score_short
   568	    ema_ok = result.ema9 is not None and result.ema21 is not None
   569	
   570	    # [BUG-FIX] Sebelumnya "cross_ok = True" di-hardcode, TIDAK PERNAH mengecek
   571	    # apakah calculate_golden_dead_cross() benar-benar punya cukup data --
   572	    # beda dengan ema_ok/st_ok/vwap_ok yang semuanya benar mengecek
   573	    # ketersediaan (None check). Saat data terlalu pendek (< min_bars di
   574	    # dalam calculate_golden_dead_cross), fungsi itu mengembalikan skor
   575	    # "darurat" (SCORE_NEUTRAL / fallback gap_pct) DAN menambahkan pesan ke
   576	    # `errors`, tapi skor darurat itu tetap DIANGGAP SEBAGAI SINYAL VALID
   577	    # berbobot 20% ke composite -- padahal seharusnya dikecualikan sama
   578	    # seperti 3 sub-indikator lain saat datanya tidak cukup. Dibuktikan lewat
   579	    # eksperimen: data 3 bar (semua sub-indikator lain correctly invalid)
   580	    # tetap menghasilkan composite=59.4 (bukan neutral 50) karena cross_ok
   581	    # salah dianggap True. Fix: deteksi ketersediaan via perubahan panjang
   582	    # `errors` -- kalau calculate_golden_dead_cross menambah error baru
   583	    # (artinya data tidak cukup), cross_ok=False, dikecualikan dari bobot.
   584	    errors_before_cross = len(errors)
   585	    gc_bars, dc_bars, cross_score, cross_score_short = calculate_golden_dead_cross(df, errors=errors)
   586	    result.golden_cross_bars_ago = gc_bars
   587	    result.dead_cross_bars_ago   = dc_bars
   588	    result.cross_score           = cross_score
   589	    result.cross_score_short     = cross_score_short
   590	    cross_ok = len(errors) == errors_before_cross
   591	
   592	    # Supertrend aktif untuk semua TF termasuk 1D — adaptive multiplier handle perbedaan volatilitas
   593	    st_val, st_dir, st_score = _calculate_supertrend_raw(df, errors=errors)
   594	    result.supertrend_value     = st_val
   595	    result.supertrend_direction = st_dir
   596	    result.supertrend_score     = st_score
   597	    result.supertrend_score_short = _score_supertrend_direction(st_dir, side="short")
   598	    st_ok = st_val is not None
   599	
   600	    skip_vwap = timeframe in ("1d", "3d", "1w")
   601	    if skip_vwap:
   602	        result.vwap_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   603	        result.vwap_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   604	        vwap_ok = False
   605	    else:
   606	        vwap_val, bands, vwap_score = calculate_vwap_multiday(df, errors)
   607	        result.vwap        = vwap_val
   608	        result.vwap_upper_1 = bands.get("upper_1")
   609	        result.vwap_lower_1 = bands.get("lower_1")
   610	        result.vwap_upper_2 = bands.get("upper_2")
   611	        result.vwap_lower_2 = bands.get("lower_2")
   612	        result.vwap_score   = vwap_score
   613	        if vwap_val is not None:
   614	            last_close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   615	            result.vwap_score_short = _score_vwap_zone(
   616	                last_close, vwap_val,
   617	                bands.get("upper_1"), bands.get("upper_2"),
   618	                bands.get("lower_1"), bands.get("lower_2"),
   619	                side="short",
   620	            )
   621	        else:
   622	            result.vwap_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   623	        vwap_ok = vwap_val is not None
   624	
   625	    raw_weights = {
   626	        "ema":        (40.0, ema_ok),
   627	        "cross":      (20.0, cross_ok),
   628	        "supertrend": (25.0, st_ok),
   629	        "vwap":       (15.0, vwap_ok),
   630	    }
   631	    raw_scores = {
   632	        "ema":        result.ema_stack_score,
   633	        "cross":      result.cross_score,
   634	        "supertrend": result.supertrend_score,
   635	        "vwap":       result.vwap_score,
   636	    }
   637	
   638	    total_available_weight = sum(w for w, ok in raw_weights.values() if ok)
   639	
   640	    if total_available_weight < 1e-6:
   641	        result.composite_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   642	        result.composite_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   643	        errors.append("trend: tidak ada sub-indikator yang valid, composite = neutral")
   644	        return result
   645	
   646	    composite = 0.0
   647	    for key, (base_w, ok) in raw_weights.items():
   648	        if not ok:
   649	            continue
   650	        adjusted_w = base_w / total_available_weight
   651	        composite += raw_scores[key] * adjusted_w
   652	
   653	    result.composite_score = clamp_score(composite)
   654	
   655	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
   656	    # composite_score_short: pakai bobot & availability (ok flags) yang SAMA
   657	    # persis dgn long -- ok flags cuma soal ketersediaan data (ema9/ema21
   658	    # not None, dst), BUKAN soal arah, jadi valid dipakai utk kedua sisi.
   659	    # Sub-score _short (ema_stack_score_short, cross_score_short,
   660	    # supertrend_score_short, vwap_score_short) SUDAH terisi sejak Batch 5
   661	    # (proyek 24 sub-score/8 batch) -- langkah ini cuma menggabungkannya
   662	    # jadi composite, sama seperti wiring score_orderbook() di Batch 7.
   663	    raw_scores_short = {
   664	        "ema":        result.ema_stack_score_short,
   665	        "cross":      result.cross_score_short,
   666	        "supertrend": result.supertrend_score_short,
   667	        "vwap":       result.vwap_score_short,
   668	    }
   669	    composite_short = 0.0
   670	    for key, (base_w, ok) in raw_weights.items():
   671	        if not ok:
   672	            continue
   673	        adjusted_w = base_w / total_available_weight
   674	        composite_short += raw_scores_short[key] * adjusted_w
   675	
   676	    result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(composite_short)
   677	
   678	    log.debug(
   679	        "trend score: ema=%.1f cross=%.1f st=%.1f vwap=%.1f → composite=%.1f",
   680	        result.ema_stack_score, result.cross_score,
   681	        result.supertrend_score, result.vwap_score,
   682	        result.composite_score,
   683	    )
   684	
   685	    return result

    63	_BB_STD_DEV     = 2.0
