    70	def _sma(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    71	    return series.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).mean()
    72	
    73	def _wilder_smooth(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    74	    result = np.full(len(series), np.nan)
    75	    arr    = series.values.astype(float)
    76	    n      = len(arr)
    77	
    78	    if n < period:
    79	        return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
    80	
    81	    # [BUG-FIX -- pertahanan-mendalam, pola identik dgn yg ditemukan &
    82	    # diperbaiki di indicators/strength.py._wilder_smooth (commit 05d7b50)]
    83	    # Sebelumnya seed SELALU dipasang di index ABSOLUT `period-1` memakai
    84	    # nanmean(arr[:period]) -- ini cuma benar kalau `series` tidak punya
    85	    # leading NaN. Saat ini (`_calc_atr` memanggil dgn `tr` yang memang
    86	    # selalu mulai dari index 0 tanpa NaN) bug ini TIDAK ke-trigger --
    87	    # tapi kode ini identik strukturnya dgn versi lama strength.py yang
    88	    # TERBUKTI salah utk input leading-NaN (dx pada calculate_adx): seed
    89	    # nanmean(arr[:period]) di index absolut period-1 cuma merata-ratakan
    90	    # SATU nilai real yg kebetulan ada, bukan rata-rata `period` nilai
    91	    # real pertama sesuai metodologi Wilder baku. Diperbaiki sekarang
    92	    # supaya fungsi generik ini aman dipakai dgn input leading-NaN apa pun
    93	    # di masa depan, bukan menunggu sampai benar-benar ada bug nyata yg
    94	    # termanifestasi.
    95	    first_valid = 0
    96	    while first_valid < n and np.isnan(arr[first_valid]):
    97	        first_valid += 1
    98	
    99	    seed_idx = first_valid + period - 1
   100	    if seed_idx >= n:
   101	        return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
   102	
   103	    window = arr[first_valid: first_valid + period]
   104	    if np.any(np.isnan(window)):
   105	        # NaN "di tengah" window (bukan cuma leading) -- fallback ke
   106	        # nanmean drpd crash/seed sembarangan.
   107	        result[seed_idx] = np.nanmean(window)
   108	    else:
   109	        result[seed_idx] = float(np.mean(window))
   110	
   111	    for i in range(seed_idx + 1, n):
   112	        if np.isnan(result[i - 1]) or np.isnan(arr[i]):
   113	            result[i] = result[i - 1] if not np.isnan(result[i - 1]) else np.nan
   114	        else:
   115	            result[i] = (result[i - 1] * (period - 1) + arr[i]) / period
   116	
   117	    return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
   118	
   119	def _calc_true_range(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
   120	    # [PERF] Ganti pd.concat([...], axis=1).max(axis=1) dengan numpy vectorized.
   121	    # pd.concat membuat DataFrame sementara + .max(axis=1) per-elemen → ~12x lebih lambat.
   122	    # numpy np.maximum() langsung operasi array → identik secara numerik, jauh lebih cepat.
   123	    h  = df["high"].values.astype(float)
   124	    l  = df["low"].values.astype(float)
   125	    c  = df["close"].values.astype(float)
   126	    n  = len(c)
   127	    pc = np.empty(n)
   128	    pc[0]  = c[0]          # TR[0] = high-low (tidak ada prev_close)
   129	    pc[1:] = c[:-1]
   130	    tr = np.maximum(h - l, np.maximum(np.abs(h - pc), np.abs(l - pc)))
   131	    return pd.Series(tr, index=df.index)
   132	
   133	def _calc_atr(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int) -> pd.Series:
   134	    tr  = _calc_true_range(df)
   135	    atr = _wilder_smooth(tr, period)
   136	    return atr
   137	
   138	def _bb_trend(bb_width: pd.Series, lookback: int = 5) -> str:
   139	    if len(bb_width) < lookback + 1:
   140	        return "flat"
   141	
   142	    current  = float(bb_width.iloc[-1])
   143	    # [BUG-FIX] Sebelumnya "past_avg = bb_width.iloc[-lookback:].mean()" --
   144	    # window ini MENYERTAKAN bar saat ini (current) di dalam rata-rata
   145	    # "masa lalu"-nya sendiri, meredam rasio current/past_avg ke arah 1.0.
   146	    # Ini TIDAK KONSISTEN dengan _atr_trend_direction() yang benar
   147	    # mengecualikan current dari past_avg (pakai iloc[-lookback-1:-1]).
   148	    # Dibuktikan lewat eksperimen: data IDENTIK (5 nilai flat lalu naik 6%)
   149	    # menghasilkan kesimpulan arah BERBEDA -- _bb_trend lama bilang "flat",
   150	    # _atr_trend_direction bilang "rising" -- padahal seharusnya konsisten
   151	    # karena keduanya menjawab pertanyaan yang sama ("apakah nilai sekarang
   152	    # menyimpang signifikan dari rata-rata historis murni?"). Fix: pakai
   153	    # window historis murni yang SAMA seperti _atr_trend_direction.
   154	    past_avg = float(bb_width.iloc[-lookback-1:-1].mean())
   155	
   156	    if past_avg < 1e-9:
   157	        return "flat"
   158	
   159	    ratio = current / past_avg
   160	
   161	    if ratio > 1.05:
   162	        return "expanding"
   163	    if ratio < 0.95:
   164	        return "contracting"
   165	    return "flat"
   166	
   167	def _score_bb(
   168	    bb_position: float,
   169	    bb_width: float,
   170	    bb_trending: str = "flat",   # [UPGRADE] sekarang dipakai dalam scoring
   171	) -> float:
   172	    if bb_position <= BB_POS_BUY_ZONE:
   173	        t    = bb_position / BB_POS_BUY_ZONE
   174	        base = 80.0 - t * 5.0
   175	    elif bb_position <= 0.50:
   176	        t    = (bb_position - BB_POS_BUY_ZONE) / (0.50 - BB_POS_BUY_ZONE)
   177	        base = 75.0 - t * 10.0
   178	    elif bb_position <= BB_POS_NEUTRAL_HIGH:
   179	        t    = (bb_position - 0.50) / (BB_POS_NEUTRAL_HIGH - 0.50)
   180	        base = 65.0 - t * 13.0
   181	    elif bb_position <= 0.80:
   182	        t    = (bb_position - BB_POS_NEUTRAL_HIGH) / (0.80 - BB_POS_NEUTRAL_HIGH)
   183	        base = 52.0 - t * 12.0
   184	    else:
   185	        t    = min((bb_position - 0.80) / 0.20, 1.0)
   186	        base = 40.0 - t * 15.0
   187	
   188	    score = base
   189	
   190	    if bb_width < BB_WIDTH_SQUEEZE:
   191	        score += 10.0
   192	    elif bb_width < BB_WIDTH_NORMAL:
   193	        score += 5.0
   194	    elif bb_width > BB_WIDTH_EXPANSION:
   195	        score -= 5.0
   196	
   197	    # [UPGRADE] bb_trending diaktifkan dalam scoring:
   198	    # - "contracting": band menyempit → energy terakumulasi, potensi breakout → bonus
   199	    #   terutama kalau posisi di lower half (bb_position < 0.5) → entry window ideal
   200	    # - "expanding" saat posisi tinggi (> 0.7): blow-off risk → penalti
   201	    # - "expanding" saat posisi rendah (< 0.35): breakout valid → kecil bonus
   202	    if bb_trending == "contracting":
   203	        if bb_position < 0.5:
   204	            score += 7.0   # contracting + lower half = perfect setup
   205	        else:
   206	            score += 3.0   # contracting tapi harga sudah mid-high
   207	    elif bb_trending == "expanding":
   208	        if bb_position > 0.70:
   209	            score -= 6.0   # expanding + overbought = blow-off risk
   210	        elif bb_position < 0.35:
   211	            score += 4.0   # expanding dari bawah = breakout momentum valid
   212	
   213	    return clamp_score(score)
   214	
   215	def calculate_bollinger_bands(
   216	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   217	    period: int = _BB_PERIOD,
   218	    std_dev: float = _BB_STD_DEV,
   219	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   220	) -> VolatilityIndicators:
   221	    if errors is None:
   222	        errors = []
   223	
   224	    if "close" not in df.columns:
   225	        errors.append("bollinger: kolom 'close' tidak tersedia")
   226	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   227	            bb_upper=None,
   228	            bb_middle=None,
   229	            bb_lower=None,
   230	            bb_width=None,
   231	            bb_position=None,
   232	            bb_trending="flat",
   233	            bb_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   234	            bb_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   235	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   236	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   237	        )
   238	
   239	    min_bars = period + 2
   240	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   241	        errors.append(
   242	            f"bollinger: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   243	        )
   244	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   245	            bb_upper=None,
   246	            bb_middle=None,
   247	            bb_lower=None,
   248	            bb_width=None,
   249	            bb_position=None,
   250	            bb_trending="flat",
   251	            bb_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   252	            bb_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   253	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   254	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   255	        )
   256	
   257	    close = df["close"]
   258	
   259	    middle_series = _sma(close, period)
   260	    std_series    = close.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).std(ddof=0)
   261	    upper_series  = middle_series + std_dev * std_series
   262	    lower_series  = middle_series - std_dev * std_series
   263	    width_series = (upper_series - lower_series) / middle_series.replace(0.0, np.nan)
   264	    band_range   = (upper_series - lower_series).replace(0.0, np.nan)
   265	    position_series = (close - lower_series) / band_range
   266	    last_upper  = upper_series.dropna()
   267	    last_middle = middle_series.dropna()
   268	    last_lower  = lower_series.dropna()
   269	    last_width  = width_series.dropna()
   270	    last_pos    = position_series.dropna()
   271	
   272	    if (last_upper.empty or last_middle.empty or
   273	            last_lower.empty or last_width.empty):
   274	        errors.append("bollinger: hasil kalkulasi kosong setelah dropna")
   275	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   276	            bb_upper=None,
   277	            bb_middle=None,
   278	            bb_lower=None,
   279	            bb_width=None,
   280	            bb_position=None,
   281	            bb_trending="flat",
   282	            bb_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   283	            bb_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   284	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   285	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   286	        )
   287	
   288	    upper_val    = float(last_upper.iloc[-1])
   289	    middle_val   = float(last_middle.iloc[-1])
   290	    lower_val    = float(last_lower.iloc[-1])
   291	    width_val    = float(last_width.iloc[-1])
   292	    position_val = float(last_pos.iloc[-1]) if not last_pos.empty else 0.5
   293	
   294	    position_val = max(0.0, min(1.0, position_val))
   295	    bb_trending = _bb_trend(width_series.dropna())
   296	    score = _score_bb(position_val, width_val, bb_trending)  # [UPGRADE] bb_trending kini aktif
   297	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B] bb_score TERBUKTI directional (favor
   298	    # posisi rendah = dekat lower band = long-favorable "buy the dip"),
   299	    # BUKAN arah-agnostic seperti dugaan awal. Short = role-swap posisi
   300	    # (1 - bb_position) lewat formula yang SAMA -- konsisten gaya
   301	    # sar/pivot/fib/donchian (bukan reformulasi cabang baru).
   302	    score_short = _score_bb(1.0 - position_val, width_val, bb_trending)
   303	
   304	    log.debug(
   305	        "bollinger: upper=%.5f mid=%.5f lower=%.5f width=%.4f pos=%.3f trend=%s → score=%.1f short=%.1f",
   306	        upper_val, middle_val, lower_val, width_val, position_val, bb_trending, score, score_short,
   307	    )
   308	
   309	    return VolatilityIndicators(
   310	        bb_upper=upper_val,
   311	        bb_middle=middle_val,
   312	        bb_lower=lower_val,
   313	        bb_width=width_val,
   314	        bb_position=position_val,
   315	        bb_trending=bb_trending,
   316	        bb_score=score,
   317	        bb_score_short=score_short,
   318	        composite_score=score,
   319	        composite_score_short=score_short,
   320	    )
   321	
   322	def _score_kc(kc_position: float) -> float:
   323	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B] Diekstrak dari ladder inline lama
   324	    # (perilaku long IDENTIK, tidak diubah -- diverifikasi manual, clamp_score
   325	    # no-op utk semua literal di sini) supaya bisa dipakai ulang utk short
   326	    # lewat role-swap posisi (1 - kc_position), konsisten gaya bb_score_short.
   327	    if kc_position < 0.0:
   328	        score = 62.0
   329	    elif kc_position < 0.35:
   330	        score = 70.0
   331	    elif kc_position < 0.65:
   332	        score = 55.0
   333	    elif kc_position <= 1.0:
   334	        score = 42.0
   335	    else:
   336	        score = 30.0
   337	    return clamp_score(score)
   338	
   339	def calculate_keltner_channels(
   340	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   341	    period: int = _KC_PERIOD,
   342	    atr_mult: float = _KC_ATR_MULT,
   343	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   344	) -> VolatilityIndicators:
   345	    if errors is None:
   346	        errors = []
   347	
   348	    for col in ("high", "low", "close"):
   349	        if col not in df.columns:
   350	            errors.append(f"keltner: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   351	            return VolatilityIndicators(
   352	                kc_upper=None,
   353	                kc_middle=None,
   354	                kc_lower=None,
   355	                kc_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   356	                kc_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   357	                composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   358	                composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   359	            )
   360	
   361	    min_bars = period * 2 + 2
   362	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   363	        errors.append(
   364	            f"keltner: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   365	        )
   366	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   367	            kc_upper=None,
   368	            kc_middle=None,
   369	            kc_lower=None,
   370	            kc_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   371	            kc_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   372	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   373	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   374	        )
   375	
   376	    close = df["close"]
   377	
   378	    middle_series = close.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
   379	    atr_series = _calc_atr(df, period)
   380	    upper_series = middle_series + atr_mult * atr_series
   381	    lower_series = middle_series - atr_mult * atr_series
   382	    last_upper  = upper_series.dropna()
   383	    last_middle = middle_series.dropna()
   384	    last_lower  = lower_series.dropna()
   385	
   386	    if last_upper.empty:
   387	        errors.append("keltner: hasil kalkulasi kosong setelah dropna")
   388	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   389	            kc_upper=None,
   390	            kc_middle=None,
   391	            kc_lower=None,
   392	            kc_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   393	            kc_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   394	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   395	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   396	        )
   397	
   398	    upper_val  = float(last_upper.iloc[-1])
   399	    middle_val = float(last_middle.iloc[-1])
   400	    lower_val  = float(last_lower.iloc[-1])
   401	    close_val  = float(close.iloc[-1])
   402	
   403	    kc_range = upper_val - lower_val
   404	    if kc_range > 1e-9:
   405	        kc_position = (close_val - lower_val) / kc_range
   406	    else:
   407	        kc_position = 0.5
   408	
   409	    score = _score_kc(kc_position)
   410	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B] kc_score TERBUKTI directional (pola sama
   411	    # seperti bb_score, favor kc_position rendah). Short = role-swap posisi
   412	    # (1 - kc_position) lewat formula/ladder yang SAMA.
   413	    score_short = _score_kc(1.0 - kc_position)
   414	
   415	    log.debug(
   416	        "keltner: upper=%.5f mid=%.5f lower=%.5f kc_pos=%.3f → score=%.1f short=%.1f",
   417	        upper_val, middle_val, lower_val, kc_position, score, score_short,
   418	    )
   419	
   420	    return VolatilityIndicators(
   421	        kc_upper=upper_val,
   422	        kc_middle=middle_val,
   423	        kc_lower=lower_val,
   424	        kc_score=score,
   425	        kc_score_short=score_short,
   426	        composite_score=score,
   427	        composite_score_short=score_short,
   428	    )
   429	
   430	def detect_squeeze(
   431	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   432	    bb_period: int = _BB_PERIOD,
   433	    bb_std: float = _BB_STD_DEV,
   434	    kc_period: int = _KC_PERIOD,
   435	    kc_mult: float = _KC_ATR_MULT,
   436	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   437	) -> Tuple[bool, int, float]:
   438	    if errors is None:
   439	        errors = []
   440	
   441	    min_bars = max(bb_period, kc_period) * 2 + 5
   442	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   443	        errors.append(
   444	            f"squeeze: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   445	        )
   446	        return False, 0, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   447	
   448	    close = df["close"]
   449	
   450	    bb_middle = _sma(close, bb_period)
   451	    bb_std_s  = close.rolling(window=bb_period, min_periods=bb_period).std(ddof=0)
   452	    bb_upper  = bb_middle + bb_std * bb_std_s
   453	    bb_lower  = bb_middle - bb_std * bb_std_s
   454	    kc_middle = close.ewm(span=kc_period, adjust=False).mean()
   455	    atr_s     = _calc_atr(df, kc_period)
   456	    kc_upper  = kc_middle + kc_mult * atr_s
   457	    kc_lower  = kc_middle - kc_mult * atr_s
   458	    squeeze_series = (bb_upper < kc_upper) & (bb_lower > kc_lower)
   459	    squeeze_arr    = squeeze_series.fillna(False).values
   460	    n = len(squeeze_arr)
   461	    if n == 0:
   462	        return False, 0, SCORE_NEUTRAL
   463	
   464	    currently_squeezing = bool(squeeze_arr[-1])
   465	
   466	    # [PERF] Ganti dua backward loop Python dengan numpy np.where().
   467	    # Loop lama: O(n) iterasi Python per-bar sampai kondisi berubah.
   468	    # numpy: O(1) setelah where() scan — sama secara numerik, lebih cepat.
   469	    if currently_squeezing:
   470	        # Hitung consecutive True dari ujung belakang
   471	        rev      = squeeze_arr[::-1]
   472	        non_true = np.where(~rev)[0]
   473	        squeeze_bars = int(non_true[0]) if len(non_true) else n
   474	    else:
   475	        # Hitung berapa bar sejak squeeze terakhir berakhir
   476	        rev       = squeeze_arr[::-1]
   477	        first_true = np.where(rev)[0]
   478	        if len(first_true) == 0:
   479	            squeeze_bars = 0
   480	        else:
   481	            bars_since_end = int(first_true[0])
   482	            squeeze_bars = -bars_since_end if bars_since_end <= 3 else 0
   483	
   484	    if squeeze_bars < 0:
   485	        recency = abs(squeeze_bars)
   486	        score   = max(75.0, 88.0 - recency * 8.0)
   487	
   488	    elif squeeze_bars == 0:
   489	        score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   490	
   491	    elif squeeze_bars <= 2:
   492	        score = 65.0 + squeeze_bars * 5.0
   493	
   494	    elif squeeze_bars <= 5:
   495	        score = 80.0 + (squeeze_bars - 3) * 0.5
   496	
   497	    elif squeeze_bars <= 10:
   498	        score = 82.0 - (squeeze_bars - 5) * 2.0
   499	
   500	    else:
   501	        excess = min(squeeze_bars - 10, 20)
   502	        score  = 70.0 - excess * 1.0
   503	
   504	    log.debug(
   505	        "squeeze: active=%s bars=%d → score=%.1f",
   506	        currently_squeezing, squeeze_bars, score,
   507	    )
   508	
   509	    return currently_squeezing, squeeze_bars, clamp_score(score)
   510	
   511	def _calc_atr_percentile(
   512	    atr_series: pd.Series,
   513	    current_atr: float,
   514	    lookback: int = _ATR_PERCENTILE_LOOKBACK,
   515	) -> float:
   516	    window = atr_series.dropna().iloc[-lookback:]
   517	    if len(window) < 2:
   518	        return 50.0
   519	
   520	    values   = window.values
   521	    n        = len(values)
   522	    rank     = np.sum(values < current_atr)
   523	    rank_eq  = np.sum(values == current_atr)
   524	    percentile = (rank + 0.5 * rank_eq) / n * 100.0
   525	
   526	    return float(np.clip(percentile, 0.0, 100.0))
   527	
   528	def _atr_trend_direction(atr_series: pd.Series, lookback: int = 5) -> str:
   529	    clean = atr_series.dropna()
   530	    if len(clean) < lookback + 1:
   531	        return "flat"
   532	
   533	    current  = float(clean.iloc[-1])
   534	    past_avg = float(clean.iloc[-lookback-1:-1].mean())
   535	
   536	    if past_avg < 1e-9:
   537	        return "flat"
   538	
   539	    ratio = current / past_avg
   540	
   541	    if ratio > 1.05:
   542	        return "rising"
   543	    if ratio < 0.95:
   544	        return "falling"
   545	    return "flat"
   546	
   547	def _score_atr(
   548	    atr_pct: float,
   549	    atr_percentile: float,
   550	    atr_trend: str,
   551	) -> float:
   552	    if atr_percentile < ATR_PERCENTILE_LOW:
   553	        t    = atr_percentile / ATR_PERCENTILE_LOW
   554	        base = 40.0 + t * 10.0
   555	    elif atr_percentile < ATR_PERCENTILE_NORMAL:
   556	        t    = (atr_percentile - ATR_PERCENTILE_LOW) / (ATR_PERCENTILE_NORMAL - ATR_PERCENTILE_LOW)
   557	        base = 50.0 + t * 12.0
   558	    elif atr_percentile < ATR_PERCENTILE_HIGH:
   559	        t    = (atr_percentile - ATR_PERCENTILE_NORMAL) / (ATR_PERCENTILE_HIGH - ATR_PERCENTILE_NORMAL)
   560	        base = 62.0 + t * 10.0
   561	    elif atr_percentile < ATR_PERCENTILE_VERY_HIGH:
   562	        t    = (atr_percentile - ATR_PERCENTILE_HIGH) / (ATR_PERCENTILE_VERY_HIGH - ATR_PERCENTILE_HIGH)
   563	        base = 72.0 - t * 14.0
   564	    else:
   565	        excess = min(atr_percentile - ATR_PERCENTILE_VERY_HIGH, 10.0)
   566	        base   = 58.0 - excess * 2.3
   567	
   568	    score = base
   569	
   570	    if atr_pct < 0.3:
   571	        score -= 5.0
   572	    elif atr_pct > 3.0:
   573	        score -= 8.0
   574	
   575	    if atr_trend == "rising":
   576	        score -= 5.0
   577	    elif atr_trend == "falling":
   578	        score += 5.0
   579	
   580	    return clamp_score(score)
   581	
   582	def calculate_atr_enhanced(
   583	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   584	    period: int = _ATR_PERIOD,
   585	    percentile_lookback: int = _ATR_PERCENTILE_LOOKBACK,
   586	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   587	) -> VolatilityIndicators:
   588	    if errors is None:
   589	        errors = []
   590	
   591	    for col in ("high", "low", "close"):
   592	        if col not in df.columns:
   593	            errors.append(f"atr_enhanced: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   594	            return VolatilityIndicators(
   595	                atr=None,
   596	                atr_pct=None,
   597	                atr_percentile=None,
   598	                atr_percentile_normalized=None,
   599	                atr_trend="flat",
   600	                atr_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   601	                atr_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   602	                composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   603	                composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   604	            )
   605	
   606	    min_bars = period * 2 + 2
   607	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   608	        errors.append(
   609	            f"atr_enhanced: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   610	        )
   611	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   612	            atr=None,
   613	            atr_pct=None,
   614	            atr_percentile=None,
   615	            atr_percentile_normalized=None,
   616	            atr_trend="flat",
   617	            atr_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   618	            atr_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   619	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   620	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   621	        )
   622	
   623	    close = df["close"]
   624	    atr_series = _calc_atr(df, period)
   625	    atr_clean  = atr_series.dropna()
   626	
   627	    if atr_clean.empty:
   628	        errors.append("atr_enhanced: hasil ATR kosong")
   629	        return VolatilityIndicators(
   630	            atr=None,
   631	            atr_pct=None,
   632	            atr_percentile=None,
   633	            atr_percentile_normalized=None,
   634	            atr_trend="flat",
   635	            atr_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   636	            atr_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   637	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   638	            composite_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   639	        )
   640	
   641	    atr_val   = float(atr_clean.iloc[-1])
   642	    close_val = float(close.iloc[-1])
   643	
   644	    if close_val > 1e-9:
   645	        atr_pct = (atr_val / close_val) * 100.0
   646	    else:
   647	        atr_pct = 0.0
   648	        errors.append("atr_enhanced: harga mendekati nol, atr_pct = 0")
   649	
   650	    atr_percentile = _calc_atr_percentile(atr_clean, atr_val, percentile_lookback)
   651	    atr_trend = _atr_trend_direction(atr_clean)
   652	    score = _score_atr(atr_pct, atr_percentile, atr_trend)
   653	
   654	    # [ITEM #4 -- Tahap C, Opsi B dual-field aditif] atr_pct sebagai SERIES
   655	    # penuh (bukan cuma bar terakhir) -- ranking dilakukan thd nilai yang
   656	    # SUDAH ternormalisasi harga (atr_pct), bukan ATR absolut spt
   657	    # atr_percentile lama. Reuse _calc_atr_percentile() apa adanya (fungsi
   658	    # itu generic -- murni ranking percentile suatu series, tidak spesifik
   659	    # ke "ATR" apa pun) supaya algoritma ranking-nya PROVABLY identik dgn
   660	    # field lama, cuma input series-nya beda. close_safe: hindari div/0
   661	    # konsisten dgn guard skalar atr_pct di atas (close mendekati nol ->
   662	    # NaN, bukan inf, supaya tidak ikut masuk window ranking).
   663	    close_safe = close.where(close > 1e-9)
   664	    atr_pct_series = (atr_series / close_safe) * 100.0
   665	    atr_pct_clean = atr_pct_series.dropna()
   666	    atr_percentile_normalized = _calc_atr_percentile(atr_pct_clean, atr_pct, percentile_lookback)
   667	
   668	    log.debug(
   669	        "atr_enhanced: atr=%.5f pct=%.3f%% percentile=%.1f (normalized=%.1f) trend=%s → score=%.1f",
   670	        atr_val, atr_pct, atr_percentile, atr_percentile_normalized, atr_trend, score,
   671	    )
   672	
   673	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B, KNOWN LIMITATION] alias, BUKAN diklaim
   674	    # arah-agnostic -- lihat CLAUDE.md bagian "TEMUAN TERPISAH" utk root
   675	    # cause bias (atr_percentile ranking ATR absolut, bukan atr_pct) dan
   676	    # kenapa fix-nya DITUNDA sbg proyek terpisah (blast radius menyentuh
   677	    # regime classification live). Alias di sini cuma supaya
   678	    # composite_score_short tidak None/crash.
   679	    return VolatilityIndicators(
   680	        atr=atr_val,
   681	        atr_pct=atr_pct,
   682	        atr_percentile=atr_percentile,
   683	        atr_percentile_normalized=atr_percentile_normalized,
   684	        atr_trend=atr_trend,
   685	        atr_score=score,
   686	        atr_score_short=score,
   687	        composite_score=score,
   688	        composite_score_short=score,
   689	    )
   690	
   691	def calculate_squeeze(
   692	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   693	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   694	) -> VolatilityIndicators:
   695	    squeeze_active, squeeze_bars, squeeze_score = detect_squeeze(df, errors=errors)
   696	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B] squeeze_score confirmed genuinely
   697	    # arah-agnostic via fuzz (murni fungsi durasi/state squeeze) -- alias,
   698	    # bukan hasil formula terpisah.
   699	    return VolatilityIndicators(
   700	        squeeze_active=squeeze_active,
   701	        squeeze_bars=squeeze_bars,
   702	        squeeze_score=squeeze_score,
   703	        squeeze_score_short=squeeze_score,
   704	        composite_score=squeeze_score,
   705	        composite_score_short=squeeze_score,
   706	    )
   707	
   708	def score_volatility(
   709	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   710	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   711	) -> VolatilityIndicators:
   712	    if errors is None:
   713	        errors = []
   714	
   715	    result = VolatilityIndicators()
   716	
   717	    bb = calculate_bollinger_bands(df, errors=errors)
   718	    result.bb_upper    = bb.bb_upper
   719	    result.bb_middle   = bb.bb_middle
   720	    result.bb_lower    = bb.bb_lower
   721	    result.bb_width    = bb.bb_width
   722	    result.bb_position = bb.bb_position
   723	    result.bb_trending = bb.bb_trending
   724	    result.bb_score    = bb.bb_score
   725	    result.bb_score_short = bb.bb_score_short   # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B]
   726	    bb_ok = bb.bb_upper is not None
   727	
   728	    kc = calculate_keltner_channels(df, errors=errors)
   729	    result.kc_upper  = kc.kc_upper
   730	    result.kc_lower  = kc.kc_lower
   731	    result.kc_middle = kc.kc_middle
   732	    result.kc_score  = kc.kc_score
   733	    result.kc_score_short = kc.kc_score_short   # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B]
   734	    kc_ok = kc.kc_upper is not None
   735	
   736	    sq = detect_squeeze(df, errors=errors)
   737	    result.squeeze_active = sq[0]
   738	    result.squeeze_bars   = sq[1]
   739	    result.squeeze_score  = sq[2]
   740	    result.squeeze_score_short = sq[2]   # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B] alias, confirmed arah-agnostic
   741	
   742	    if kc_ok:
   743	        combined_kc_squeeze = (result.kc_score + result.squeeze_score) / 2.0
   744	        combined_kc_squeeze_short = (result.kc_score_short + result.squeeze_score_short) / 2.0
   745	    else:
   746	        combined_kc_squeeze = result.squeeze_score
   747	        combined_kc_squeeze_short = result.squeeze_score_short
   748	    # [BUG-FIX] kc_squeeze_ok = kc_ok or True selalu menghasilkan True (X or True ≡ True),
   749	    # sehingga bobot SQUEEZE selalu masuk composite terlepas apapun. Ganti dengan
   750	    # flag eksplisit: squeeze selalu punya skor (minimal SCORE_NEUTRAL dari fallback),
   751	    # jadi memang selalu valid — tapi tulis secara eksplisit, bukan 'or True'.
   752	    kc_squeeze_valid = True  # squeeze selalu return skor (fallback=SCORE_NEUTRAL)
   753	
   754	    atr = calculate_atr_enhanced(df, errors=errors)
   755	    result.atr            = atr.atr
   756	    result.atr_pct        = atr.atr_pct
   757	    result.atr_percentile = atr.atr_percentile
   758	    result.atr_percentile_normalized = atr.atr_percentile_normalized   # [ITEM #4 -- Tahap C]
   759	    result.atr_trend      = atr.atr_trend
   760	    result.atr_score      = atr.atr_score
   761	    result.atr_score_short = atr.atr_score_short   # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B, KNOWN LIMITATION -- alias]
   762	    atr_ok = atr.atr is not None
   763	
   764	    sub_indicators = [
   765	        (_BB_WEIGHT,      bb_ok,             result.bb_score),
   766	        (_SQUEEZE_WEIGHT, kc_squeeze_valid,  combined_kc_squeeze),
   767	        (_ATR_WEIGHT,     atr_ok,            result.atr_score),
   768	    ]
   769	    sub_indicators_short = [
   770	        (_BB_WEIGHT,      bb_ok,             result.bb_score_short),
   771	        (_SQUEEZE_WEIGHT, kc_squeeze_valid,  combined_kc_squeeze_short),
   772	        (_ATR_WEIGHT,     atr_ok,            result.atr_score_short),
   773	    ]
   774	
   775	    total_weight_available = sum(w for w, ok, _ in sub_indicators if ok)
   776	
   777	    if total_weight_available < 1e-6:
   778	        errors.append(
   779	            "volatility: tidak ada sub-indikator yang valid, composite = neutral"
   780	        )
   781	        result.composite_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   782	        result.composite_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   783	        return result
   784	
   785	    composite = 0.0
   786	    composite_short = 0.0
   787	    for (base_w, ok, score), (_, _, score_short) in zip(sub_indicators, sub_indicators_short):
   788	        if not ok:
   789	            continue
   790	        adjusted_w  = base_w / total_weight_available
   791	        composite  += score * adjusted_w
   792	        composite_short += score_short * adjusted_w
   793	
   794	    result.composite_score = clamp_score(composite)
   795	    result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(composite_short)   # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch B]
   796	
   797	    log.debug(
   798	        "volatility composite: bb=%.1f squeeze=%.1f atr=%.1f → composite=%.1f short=%.1f "
   799	        "(squeeze_active=%s bars=%d)",
   800	        result.bb_score, combined_kc_squeeze, result.atr_score,
   801	        result.composite_score, result.composite_score_short,
   802	        result.squeeze_active, result.squeeze_bars,
   803	    )
   804	
   805	    return result
   806	
   807	def calculate_all(
   808	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   809	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   810	) -> VolatilityIndicators:
   811	    return score_volatility(df, errors=errors)

     1	"""
     2	indicators/strength.py
     3	AlgoTrader Pro v7.0 — "The Intelligence Pipeline"
     4	
     5	CHANGELOG v2:
     6	  [PERF]   _calc_true_range(): pd.concat([...], axis=1).max(axis=1) → numpy
     7	           vectorized np.maximum(). ~12.5x lebih cepat, identik secara numerik.
     8	  [PERF]   _calc_directional_movement(): loop Python per-bar → numpy vectorized
     9	           np.diff() + np.where(). ~2.6x lebih cepat, identik.
    10	  [PERF]   _calc_obv(): loop Python per-bar → numpy np.sign + np.cumsum().
    11	           ~3.4x lebih cepat, identik.
    12	  [UPGRADE] intelligence/validator.py: 3 check baru yang mengaktifkan field
    13	           obv, obv_trend, mfi_divergence yang sebelumnya idle:
    14	           _check_strength_context() → adx/di/volume/obv/mfi terintegrasi penuh.
    15	
    16	CHANGELOG v3 (audit kualitas internal + potensi cross-file):
    17	  [BUG-FIX] intelligence/validator.py _check_strength_context(): volume_climax
    18	           double-penalty — _check_volume_climax() (existing) dan
    19	           _check_strength_context() (baru) keduanya menghitung penalty untuk
    20	           field st.volume_climax yang sama (-0.10 dan -0.05), total diam-diam
    21	           jadi -0.15. Dihapus dari _check_strength_context(), satu-satunya
    22	           pemilik logic sekarang _check_volume_climax().
    23	  [PERF]   calculate_money_flow()/score_strength(): parameter rsi_series
    24	           opsional — sebelumnya _calc_rsi() dihitung ulang dari nol di sini
    25	           hanya untuk deteksi MFI-RSI divergence, padahal score_momentum()
    26	           (dipanggil tepat sebelum score_strength() di observer.py) baru saja
    27	           menghitung RSI(14) identik dari close yang sama. Benchmark: ~19%
    28	           dari total waktu score_strength() (1.39ms dari 7.31ms). Sekarang
    29	           observer.py menghitung RSI sekali dan membaginya ke kedua fungsi;
    30	           tetap backward-compatible (fallback hitung sendiri kalau None).
    31	  [CLEANUP] calculate_volume_analysis() & _calc_mfi(): hapus
    32	           df["volume"].replace(0.0, 0.0) — no-op (replace 0.0 dengan 0.0),
    33	           sisa refactor yang membingungkan, tidak ada dampak numerik.

    36	from __future__ import annotations
    37	
    38	import logging
    39	from typing import List, Optional, Tuple
    40	
    41	import numpy as np
    42	import pandas as pd
    43	
    44	from engine.constants import (
    45	    ADX_WEAK_TREND,
    46	    ADX_MODERATE_TREND,
    47	    ADX_STRONG_TREND,
    48	    ADX_VERY_STRONG,
    49	    VOLUME_RATIO_WEAK,
    50	    VOLUME_RATIO_NORMAL,
    51	    VOLUME_RATIO_ELEVATED,
    52	    VOLUME_RATIO_STRONG,
    53	    VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE,
    54	    VOLUME_RATIO_CLIMAX,
    55	    VOLUME_CLIMAX_PENALTY,

    58	    RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD,
    59	    SCORE_NEUTRAL,
    60	)
    61	from engine.core.models import StrengthIndicators, clamp_score
    62	
    63	log = logging.getLogger("indicators.strength")
    64	_ADX_WEIGHT    = 0.35
    65	_DI_WEIGHT     = 0.15
    66	_VOLUME_WEIGHT = 0.35
    67	_MFI_WEIGHT    = 0.15
    68	_VOLUME_MA_PERIOD  = 20
    69	_OBV_SLOPE_PERIOD  = 10
    70	_MFI_PERIOD = 14
    71	_ADX_PERIOD = 14
    72	_DIVERGENCE_LOOKBACK = 20

    74	def _sma(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    75	    return series.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).mean()
    76	
    77	def _ema(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    78	    return series.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
    79	
    80	def _wilder_smooth(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    81	    result = np.full(len(series), np.nan)
    82	    arr    = series.values.astype(float)
    83	    n      = len(arr)
    84	
    85	    if n < period:
    86	        return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
    87	
    88	    # [BUG-FIX — kritis, ditemukan lewat cross-check terhadap implementasi
    89	    # ADX independen] Sebelumnya seed SELALU dipasang di index ABSOLUT
    90	    # `period-1` memakai nanmean(arr[:period]) -- ini benar HANYA kalau
    91	    # `arr` tidak punya leading NaN (kasus TR/+DM/-DM, yang memang mulai
    92	    # dari index 0). TAPI kalau `arr` punya leading NaN (kasus `dx` di
    93	    # calculate_adx: punya period-1 NaN di depan sebelum DI+/DI- pertama
    94	    # kali valid), nanmean(arr[:period]) cuma merata-ratakan SATU nilai
    95	    # real yang kebetulan ada di window itu (nilai NaN diabaikan nanmean),
    96	    # BUKAN rata-rata `period` nilai real pertama seperti metodologi Wilder
    97	    # baku (ADX textbook: "ADX pertama = rata-rata 14 nilai DX pertama").
    98	    # Dibuktikan: dx dgn 13 NaN lalu nilai real -> seed lama muncul di
    99	    # index 13 memakai HANYA 1 nilai (harusnya nunggu sampai index 26,
   100	    # rata-rata 14 nilai real). Dampak nyata ke calculate_adx: ADX di
   101	    # sekitar bar minimum (29 bar) meleset ~2.4 poin bahkan SETELAH fix
   102	    # zero-contamination sebelumnya. Fix: deteksi posisi nilai valid
   103	    # PERTAMA, lalu seed = rata-rata `period` nilai valid pertama mulai
   104	    # dari situ (bukan dari index absolut 0).
   105	    first_valid = 0
   106	    while first_valid < n and np.isnan(arr[first_valid]):
   107	        first_valid += 1
   108	
   109	    seed_idx = first_valid + period - 1
   110	    if seed_idx >= n:
   111	        return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
   112	
   113	    window = arr[first_valid: first_valid + period]
   114	    if np.any(np.isnan(window)):
   115	        # Ada NaN "di tengah" window (bukan cuma leading) -- data tidak
   116	        # bersih, tidak bisa seed dengan aman. Fallback ke perilaku lama
   117	        # (nanmean atas window yang sama) drpd crash/seed sembarangan.
   118	        result[seed_idx] = np.nanmean(window)
   119	    else:
   120	        result[seed_idx] = float(np.mean(window))
   121	
   122	    for i in range(seed_idx + 1, n):
   123	        if np.isnan(result[i - 1]) or np.isnan(arr[i]):
   124	            result[i] = result[i - 1] if not np.isnan(result[i - 1]) else np.nan
   125	        else:
   126	            result[i] = (result[i - 1] * (period - 1) + arr[i]) / period
   127	
   128	    return pd.Series(result, index=series.index)
   129	
   130	def _calc_true_range(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
   131	    # [PERF] numpy vectorized — ~12.5x lebih cepat dari pd.concat approach
   132	    h  = df["high"].values.astype(float)
   133	    l  = df["low"].values.astype(float)
   134	    c  = df["close"].values.astype(float)
   135	    n  = len(c)
   136	    pc = np.empty(n); pc[0] = c[0]; pc[1:] = c[:-1]
   137	    tr = np.maximum(h - l, np.maximum(np.abs(h - pc), np.abs(l - pc)))
   138	    return pd.Series(tr, index=df.index)
   139	
   140	def _calc_directional_movement(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Tuple[pd.Series, pd.Series]:
   141	    # [PERF] numpy vectorized — ~2.6x lebih cepat dari loop Python per-bar
   142	    high = df["high"].values.astype(float)
   143	    low  = df["low"].values.astype(float)
   144	
   145	    up_move   = np.diff(high, prepend=high[0])   # high[i] - high[i-1]
   146	    down_move = -np.diff(low, prepend=low[0])    # low[i-1] - low[i]
   147	
   148	    plus_dm  = np.where((up_move > down_move) & (up_move > 0.0),   up_move,   0.0)
   149	    minus_dm = np.where((down_move > up_move)  & (down_move > 0.0), down_move, 0.0)
   150	
   151	    # Bar pertama tidak punya prev → nol (identik dengan loop lama)
   152	    plus_dm[0]  = 0.0
   153	    minus_dm[0] = 0.0
   154	
   155	    return (
   156	        pd.Series(plus_dm,  index=df.index),
   157	        pd.Series(minus_dm, index=df.index),
   158	    )
   159	
   160	def _score_adx(adx_val: float) -> float:
   161	    if adx_val < ADX_WEAK_TREND:
   162	        t    = adx_val / ADX_WEAK_TREND
   163	        return clamp_score(t * 35.0)
   164	
   165	    if adx_val < ADX_MODERATE_TREND:
   166	        t    = (adx_val - ADX_WEAK_TREND) / (ADX_MODERATE_TREND - ADX_WEAK_TREND)
   167	        return clamp_score(35.0 + t * 20.0)
   168	
   169	    if adx_val < ADX_STRONG_TREND:
   170	        t    = (adx_val - ADX_MODERATE_TREND) / (ADX_STRONG_TREND - ADX_MODERATE_TREND)
   171	        return clamp_score(55.0 + t * 25.0)
   172	
   173	    if adx_val < ADX_VERY_STRONG:
   174	        t    = (adx_val - ADX_STRONG_TREND) / (ADX_VERY_STRONG - ADX_STRONG_TREND)
   175	        return clamp_score(80.0 - t * 10.0)
   176	
   177	    excess = min(adx_val - ADX_VERY_STRONG, 30.0)
   178	    return clamp_score(70.0 - excess * 0.8)
   179	
   180	def _score_di(plus_di: float, minus_di: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   181	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 2] Sebelumnya cuma ukur dominasi +DI (bullish
   182	    # directional movement) -- minus_di dominan (bearish, ideal utk short)
   183	    # selalu diskor RENDAH. side="short": ratio dihitung dari minus_di,
   184	    # bukan komplemen (100-x) -- swap peran plus_di/minus_di langsung di
   185	    # rumus yang sama, formula tidak berubah.
   186	    total = plus_di + minus_di
   187	    if total < 1e-9:
   188	        return SCORE_NEUTRAL
   189	    ratio = (minus_di / total) if side == "short" else (plus_di / total)
   190	    return clamp_score(5.0 + ratio * 90.0)
   191	
   192	def calculate_adx(
   193	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   194	    period: int = _ADX_PERIOD,
   195	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   196	) -> StrengthIndicators:
   197	    if errors is None:
   198	        errors = []
   199	
   200	    for col in ("high", "low", "close"):
   201	        if col not in df.columns:
   202	            errors.append(f"adx: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   203	            return StrengthIndicators(
   204	                adx=None,
   205	                plus_di=None,
   206	                minus_di=None,
   207	                adx_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   208	                di_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   209	                di_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   210	                composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   211	            )
   212	
   213	    min_bars = period * 2 + 1
   214	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   215	        errors.append(
   216	            f"adx: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   217	        )
   218	        return StrengthIndicators(
   219	            adx=None,
   220	            plus_di=None,
   221	            minus_di=None,
   222	            adx_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   223	            di_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   224	            di_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   225	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   226	        )
   227	
   228	    tr       = _calc_true_range(df)
   229	    plus_dm, minus_dm = _calc_directional_movement(df)
   230	    atr_smooth       = _wilder_smooth(tr,       period)
   231	    smooth_plus_dm   = _wilder_smooth(plus_dm,  period)
   232	    smooth_minus_dm  = _wilder_smooth(minus_dm, period)
   233	    atr_safe = atr_smooth.replace(0.0, np.nan)
   234	    # [BUG-FIX — kritis, ditemukan lewat cross-check terhadap implementasi
   235	    # ADX independen] Sebelumnya di_plus/di_minus di-fillna(0.0) DI SINI,
   236	    # padahal untuk indeks 0..period-2 (warm-up, atr_smooth masih NaN
   237	    # karena _wilder_smooth baru mulai menghasilkan nilai di index
   238	    # period-1), fillna(0.0) itu MEMALSUKAN "belum ada data" menjadi
   239	    # "DI+/DI- = 0". Akibatnya dx untuk indeks warm-up itu JUGA ikut jadi
   240	    # 0.0 (bukan NaN), dan saat _wilder_smooth(dx, period) mengambil seed
   241	    # awalnya dari nanmean(dx[:period]), rata-rata itu TERCEMAR oleh
   242	    # (period-1) nilai nol palsu -- membuat seed ADX jauh lebih rendah dari
   243	    # yang seharusnya (rata-rata cuma dx_asli/period, bukan dx_asli murni).
   244	    # Dibuktikan lewat implementasi ADX independen (rumus textbook Wilder
   245	    # ditulis ulang dari nol, tanpa contek kode ini): selisih ADX 0.41 dari
   246	    # basis ~18 (~2.3%), dan bias ini LEBIH BESAR lagi persis di sekitar
   247	    # jumlah bar minimum (period*2+1=29) karena rekursi Wilder belum sempat
   248	    # "melupakan" seed yang tercemar. Fix: biarkan NaN mengalir apa adanya
   249	    # sepanjang pipeline (jangan fillna prematur) -- _wilder_smooth sendiri
   250	    # sudah benar menangani NaN di awal (skip via nanmean), dan dropna() di
   251	    # akhir fungsi ini sudah menangani ekstraksi nilai valid terakhir.
   252	    di_plus  = (smooth_plus_dm  / atr_safe * 100.0)
   253	    di_minus = (smooth_minus_dm / atr_safe * 100.0)
   254	    di_sum  = (di_plus + di_minus).replace(0.0, np.nan)
   255	    dx      = ((di_plus - di_minus).abs() / di_sum * 100.0)
   256	    adx_series = _wilder_smooth(dx, period)
   257	    last_adx      = adx_series.dropna()
   258	    last_di_plus  = di_plus.dropna()
   259	    last_di_minus = di_minus.dropna()
   260	
   261	    if last_adx.empty or last_di_plus.empty:
   262	        errors.append("adx: hasil kalkulasi kosong setelah dropna")
   263	        return StrengthIndicators(
   264	            adx=None,
   265	            plus_di=None,
   266	            minus_di=None,
   267	            adx_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   268	            di_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   269	            di_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   270	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   271	        )
   272	
   273	    adx_val      = float(last_adx.iloc[-1])
   274	    plus_di_val  = float(last_di_plus.iloc[-1])
   275	    minus_di_val = float(last_di_minus.iloc[-1])
   276	
   277	    adx_score = _score_adx(adx_val)
   278	    di_score  = _score_di(plus_di_val, minus_di_val)
   279	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 2] adx_score TIDAK disentuh (genuinely direction-
   280	    # agnostic, dikonfirmasi -- cuma ukur kekuatan trend, bukan arahnya).
   281	    di_score_short = _score_di(plus_di_val, minus_di_val, side="short")
   282	
   283	    log.debug(
   284	        "adx: adx=%.1f DI+=%.1f DI-=%.1f → adx_score=%.1f di_score=%.1f/%.1f(short)",
   285	        adx_val, plus_di_val, minus_di_val, adx_score, di_score, di_score_short,
   286	    )
   287	
   288	    return StrengthIndicators(
   289	        adx=adx_val,
   290	        plus_di=plus_di_val,
   291	        minus_di=minus_di_val,
   292	        adx_score=adx_score,
   293	        di_score=di_score,
   294	        di_score_short=di_score_short,
   295	        composite_score=clamp_score((adx_score + di_score) / 2),
   296	    )
   297	
   298	def _calc_obv(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
   299	    # [PERF] numpy vectorized — ~3.4x lebih cepat dari loop Python per-bar
   300	    # np.sign: +1 naik, -1 turun, 0 flat → direction[0]=0 (tidak ada prev bar)
   301	    c         = close.values.astype(float)
   302	    v         = volume.values.astype(float)
   303	    direction = np.sign(np.diff(c, prepend=c[0]))
   304	    direction[0] = 0.0   # bar pertama tidak punya arah
   305	    return pd.Series(np.cumsum(direction * v), index=close.index)
   306	
   307	def _obv_trend(obv: pd.Series, window: int = _OBV_SLOPE_PERIOD) -> str:
   308	    if len(obv) < window + 1:
   309	        return "flat"
   310	
   311	    current = float(obv.iloc[-1])
   312	    past    = float(obv.iloc[-window])
   313	    delta   = current - past
   314	
   315	    mean_abs = float(obv.iloc[-window:].abs().mean())
   316	    threshold = mean_abs * 0.01 if mean_abs > 0 else 1.0
   317	
   318	    if delta > threshold:
   319	        return "rising"
   320	    if delta < -threshold:
   321	        return "falling"
   322	    return "flat"
   323	
   324	def _score_volume(
   325	    ratio: float,
   326	    spike: bool,
   327	    climax: bool,
   328	    obv_trend_str: str,
   329	    side: str = "long",
   330	) -> float:
   331	    if ratio < VOLUME_RATIO_WEAK:
   332	        t    = ratio / VOLUME_RATIO_WEAK
   333	        base = t * 20.0
   334	    elif ratio < VOLUME_RATIO_NORMAL:
   335	        t    = (ratio - VOLUME_RATIO_WEAK) / (VOLUME_RATIO_NORMAL - VOLUME_RATIO_WEAK)
   336	        base = 20.0 + t * 20.0
   337	    elif ratio < VOLUME_RATIO_ELEVATED:
   338	        t    = (ratio - VOLUME_RATIO_NORMAL) / (VOLUME_RATIO_ELEVATED - VOLUME_RATIO_NORMAL)
   339	        base = 40.0 + t * 20.0
   340	    elif ratio < VOLUME_RATIO_STRONG:
   341	        t    = (ratio - VOLUME_RATIO_ELEVATED) / (VOLUME_RATIO_STRONG - VOLUME_RATIO_ELEVATED)
   342	        base = 60.0 + t * 15.0
   343	    elif ratio < VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE:
   344	        t    = (ratio - VOLUME_RATIO_STRONG) / (VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE - VOLUME_RATIO_STRONG)
   345	        base = 75.0 + t * 7.0
   346	    else:
   347	        excess = min(ratio - VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE, VOLUME_RATIO_CLIMAX - VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE)
   348	        t      = excess / (VOLUME_RATIO_CLIMAX - VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE)
   349	        base   = 82.0 - t * 12.0
   350	
   351	    score = base
   352	
   353	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 2] Cuma term OBV-trend ini yang directional (bukan
   354	    # magnitude) -- base (ratio ladder di atas) dan climax penalty di bawah
   355	    # TIDAK disentuh, tetap sama utk kedua sisi (magnitude/kualitas sinyal,
   356	    # bukan arah). side="short": OBV falling (distribusi, bearish) yang
   357	    # dapat bonus, rising yang kena penalti -- swap langsung, bukan 100-x.
   358	    if side == "short":
   359	        if obv_trend_str == "falling":
   360	            score += 8.0
   361	        elif obv_trend_str == "rising":
   362	            score -= 8.0
   363	    else:
   364	        if obv_trend_str == "rising":
   365	            score += 8.0
   366	        elif obv_trend_str == "falling":
   367	            score -= 8.0
   368	
   369	    if climax:
   370	        score -= VOLUME_CLIMAX_PENALTY
   371	
   372	    return clamp_score(score)
   373	
   374	def calculate_volume_analysis(
   375	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   376	    volume_ma_period: int = _VOLUME_MA_PERIOD,
   377	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   378	) -> StrengthIndicators:
   379	    if errors is None:
   380	        errors = []
   381	
   382	    for col in ("close", "volume"):
   383	        if col not in df.columns:
   384	            errors.append(f"volume: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   385	            return StrengthIndicators(
   386	                volume_ratio=None,
   387	                volume_spike=False,
   388	                obv=None,
   389	                obv_trend="flat",
   390	                volume_climax=False,
   391	                volume_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   392	                volume_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   393	                composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   394	            )
   395	
   396	    vol_col = "quote_volume" if "quote_volume" in df.columns else "volume"
   397	    volume  = df[vol_col].replace(0.0, np.nan)
   398	    close   = df["close"]
   399	
   400	    min_bars = volume_ma_period + 2
   401	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   402	        errors.append(
   403	            f"volume: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   404	        )
   405	        return StrengthIndicators(
   406	            volume_ratio=None,
   407	            volume_spike=False,
   408	            obv=None,
   409	            obv_trend="flat",
   410	            volume_climax=False,
   411	            volume_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   412	            volume_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   413	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   414	        )
   415	
   416	    vol_ma     = _sma(volume, volume_ma_period)
   417	    last_vol   = float(volume.iloc[-1]) if not np.isnan(volume.iloc[-1]) else 0.0
   418	    last_ma    = float(vol_ma.iloc[-1]) if pd.notna(vol_ma.iloc[-1]) else 0.0
   419	
   420	    if last_ma < 1e-9:
   421	        errors.append("volume: MA volume mendekati nol — tidak bisa hitung ratio")
   422	        return StrengthIndicators(
   423	            volume_ratio=None,
   424	            volume_spike=False,
   425	            obv=None,
   426	            obv_trend="flat",
   427	            volume_climax=False,
   428	            volume_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   429	            volume_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   430	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   431	        )
   432	
   433	    ratio  = last_vol / last_ma
   434	    spike  = ratio >= VOLUME_RATIO_SPIKE
   435	    climax = ratio >= VOLUME_RATIO_CLIMAX
   436	    # [CLEANUP v2.1] Sebelumnya: df["volume"].replace(0.0, 0.0) — no-op (replace
   437	    # 0.0 dengan 0.0 = tidak melakukan apapun), sisa refactor yang membingungkan.
   438	    # OBV aman terima volume=0.0 mentah karena tidak ada divisi di sini.
   439	    raw_volume = df["volume"]
   440	    obv_series  = _calc_obv(close, raw_volume)
   441	    obv_val     = float(obv_series.iloc[-1])
   442	    obv_trend_str = _obv_trend(obv_series)
   443	    score = _score_volume(ratio, spike, climax, obv_trend_str)
   444	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 2] Cuma term OBV-trend yang di-mirror; base ratio
   445	    # ladder & climax penalty magnitude-only, sama utk kedua sisi.
   446	    score_short = _score_volume(ratio, spike, climax, obv_trend_str, side="short")
   447	
   448	    log.debug(
   449	        "volume: ratio=%.2fx spike=%s climax=%s obv_trend=%s → score=%.1f/%.1f(short)",
   450	        ratio, spike, climax, obv_trend_str, score, score_short,
   451	    )
   452	
   453	    return StrengthIndicators(
   454	        volume_ratio=float(ratio),
   455	        volume_spike=bool(spike),
   456	        obv=obv_val,
   457	        obv_trend=obv_trend_str,
   458	        volume_climax=bool(climax),
   459	        volume_score=score,
   460	        volume_score_short=score_short,
   461	        composite_score=score,
   462	    )
   463	
   464	def _calc_mfi(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int) -> pd.Series:
   465	    high   = df["high"]
   466	    low    = df["low"]
   467	    close  = df["close"]
   468	    # [CLEANUP v2.1] Sebelumnya: df["volume"].replace(0.0, 0.0) — no-op, sama
   469	    # seperti di calculate_volume_analysis(). raw_mf = typical_price * volume
   470	    # aman terima 0.0 mentah (tidak ada divisi pada volume di sini).
   471	    volume = df["volume"]
   472	    typical_price = (high + low + close) / 3.0
   473	    raw_mf        = typical_price * volume
   474	    tp_change    = typical_price.diff()
   475	    positive_mf  = raw_mf.where(tp_change > 0, 0.0)
   476	    negative_mf  = raw_mf.where(tp_change < 0, 0.0).abs()
   477	    sum_pos  = positive_mf.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).sum()
   478	    sum_neg  = negative_mf.rolling(window=period, min_periods=period).sum()
   479	    # [BUG-FIX -- ditemukan lewat verifikasi matematika independen, pola
   480	    # sama seperti bug RSI lama] Sebelumnya:
   481	    #   money_ratio = (sum_pos / sum_neg.replace(0.0, np.nan)).replace([inf,-inf], NaN)
   482	    #   mfi = 100 - 100/(1+money_ratio)  lalu fillna(SCORE_NEUTRAL=50)
   483	    # Ini MENYAMAKAN dua kondisi yang secara matematis BERBEDA saat
   484	    # sum_neg==0:
   485	    #   (a) sum_pos>0, sum_neg==0 -> SEMUA money flow POSITIF (tidak ada
   486	    #       tekanan jual sama sekali dlm window) -> money_ratio -> takhingga
   487	    #       -> MFI seharusnya 100 (extreme overbought) TAPI kode lama
   488	    #       memberi 50 (netral) krn sum_neg.replace(0,NaN) membuat rasio
   489	    #       NaN, lalu fillna(50) di akhir menyamarkan kasus ini.
   490	    #   (b) sum_pos==0, sum_neg==0 -> BENAR-BENAR flat (tidak ada
   491	    #       perubahan typical price sama sekali dlm window) -> MFI=50
   492	    #       (netral) BENAR.
   493	    # Dibuktikan lewat eksperimen: 30 bar harga naik terus (sum_neg=0) ->
   494	    # MFI lama=50.0, seharusnya=100.0. Asimetris dgn kasus turun terus
   495	    # (sum_pos=0) yang SUDAH benar memberi MFI=0.0 (krn 0/sum_neg=0.0
   496	    # valid, tidak kena replace). Fix: MFI=100 HANYA kalau sum_pos>0 DAN
   497	    # sum_neg==0; kalau keduanya 0 (flat total), MFI=50 (netral) --
   498	    # persis pola fix RSI (avg_gain>0 & avg_loss==0 -> 100, keduanya 0 ->
   499	    # 50).
   500	    sum_neg_safe = sum_neg.replace(0.0, np.nan)
   501	    money_ratio = (sum_pos / sum_neg_safe).replace([np.inf, -np.inf], np.nan)
   502	    mfi = 100.0 - (100.0 / (1.0 + money_ratio))
   503	    mfi = mfi.where(sum_neg > 0, np.where(sum_pos > 0, 100.0, 50.0))
   504	    mfi = pd.Series(mfi, index=close.index)
   505	
   506	    return mfi.fillna(SCORE_NEUTRAL)
   507	
   508	def _detect_mfi_rsi_divergence(
   509	    mfi: pd.Series,
   510	    rsi: pd.Series,
   511	    lookback: int = 10,
   512	) -> float:
   513	    if len(mfi) < lookback + 1 or len(rsi) < lookback + 1:
   514	        return 0.0
   515	
   516	    mfi_change = float(mfi.iloc[-1]) - float(mfi.iloc[-lookback])
   517	    rsi_change = float(rsi.iloc[-1]) - float(rsi.iloc[-lookback])
   518	
   519	    diff = mfi_change - rsi_change
   520	
   521	    if abs(diff) < RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   522	        return 0.0
   523	
   524	    return diff
   525	
   526	def _score_mfi(mfi_val: float, mfi_rsi_div: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   527	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 3, input-reflection] Teknik sama persis dgn
   528	    # _score_rsi() -- MFI_OVERSOLD(20)/MFI_OVERBOUGHT(80) persis simetris
   529	    # 100-, mfi_rsi_div ikut pola asymmetric-bonus/penalty yg sama dgn
   530	    # divergence RSI/MACD (>0 favor bullish, <0 favor bearish).
   531	    if side == "short":
   532	        mfi_val     = 100.0 - mfi_val
   533	        mfi_rsi_div = -mfi_rsi_div
   534	
   535	    if mfi_val <= MFI_OVERSOLD:
   536	        if mfi_val <= 20.0:
   537	            base = 50.0
   538	        else:
   539	            t    = (mfi_val - 20.0) / (MFI_OVERSOLD - 20.0)
   540	            base = 50.0 + t * 8.0
   541	    elif mfi_val <= 45.0:
   542	        t    = (mfi_val - MFI_OVERSOLD) / (45.0 - MFI_OVERSOLD)
   543	        base = 58.0 - t * 6.0
   544	    elif mfi_val <= 55.0:
   545	        t    = (mfi_val - 45.0) / 10.0
   546	        base = 52.0 + t * 20.0
   547	    elif mfi_val <= MFI_OVERBOUGHT:
   548	        t    = (mfi_val - 55.0) / (MFI_OVERBOUGHT - 55.0)
   549	        base = 72.0 - t * 34.0
   550	    elif mfi_val <= 90.0:
   551	        t    = (mfi_val - MFI_OVERBOUGHT) / 10.0
   552	        base = 38.0 - t * 16.0
   553	    else:
   554	        base = 22.0
   555	
   556	    score = base
   557	
   558	    if mfi_rsi_div > RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   559	        score += min(10.0, mfi_rsi_div * 0.3)
   560	    elif mfi_rsi_div < -RSI_DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD:
   561	        score += max(-8.0, mfi_rsi_div * 0.2)
   562	
   563	    return clamp_score(score)
   564	
   565	def calculate_money_flow(
   566	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   567	    period: int = _MFI_PERIOD,
   568	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   569	    rsi_series: Optional[pd.Series] = None,
   570	) -> StrengthIndicators:
   571	    """
   572	    [PERF v2.1] Parameter rsi_series opsional — RSI(14) dipakai di sini hanya
   573	    untuk deteksi divergence MFI-vs-RSI, dan period-nya (_MFI_PERIOD=14) sama
   574	    persis dengan RSI default di momentum.py. Sebelumnya _calc_rsi() dihitung
   575	    ulang dari nol di sini meskipun score_momentum() baru saja menghitung RSI
   576	    yang identik dari close yang sama — benchmark menunjukkan ini ~19% dari
   577	    total waktu score_strength(). Kalau observer.py meneruskan rsi_series
   578	    yang sudah dihitung, dipakai langsung. Kalau None/panjang tidak cocok
   579	    (misal dipanggil mandiri dengan period custom), dihitung sendiri seperti
   580	    biasa — tetap backward-compatible.
   581	    """
   582	    if errors is None:
   583	        errors = []
   584	
   585	    for col in ("high", "low", "close", "volume"):
   586	        if col not in df.columns:
   587	            errors.append(f"mfi: kolom '{col}' tidak tersedia")
   588	            return StrengthIndicators(
   589	                mfi=None,
   590	                mfi_divergence=0.0,
   591	                mfi_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   592	                mfi_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   593	                composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   594	            )
   595	
   596	    min_bars = period + 3
   597	    if len(df) < min_bars:
   598	        errors.append(
   599	            f"mfi: data hanya {len(df)} bar, butuh minimal {min_bars}"
   600	        )
   601	        return StrengthIndicators(
   602	            mfi=None,
   603	            mfi_divergence=0.0,
   604	            mfi_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   605	            mfi_score_short=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   606	            composite_score=SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   607	        )
   608	
   609	    from engine.indicators.momentum import _calc_rsi
   610	    mfi_series = _calc_mfi(df, period)
   611	    mfi_val    = float(mfi_series.iloc[-1])
   612	    use_external = rsi_series is not None and len(rsi_series) == len(df)
   613	    rsi_series = rsi_series if use_external else _calc_rsi(df["close"], period)
   614	    mfi_div = _detect_mfi_rsi_divergence(mfi_series, rsi_series)
   615	    score = _score_mfi(mfi_val, mfi_div)
   616	    score_short = _score_mfi(mfi_val, mfi_div, side="short")
   617	
   618	    log.debug(
   619	        "mfi: val=%.1f div=%.2f → score=%.1f/%.1f(short)",
   620	        mfi_val, mfi_div, score, score_short,
   621	    )
   622	
   623	    return StrengthIndicators(
   624	        mfi=mfi_val,
   625	        mfi_divergence=mfi_div,
   626	        mfi_score=score,
   627	        mfi_score_short=score_short,
   628	        composite_score=score,
   629	    )
   630	
   631	def score_strength(
   632	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   633	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   634	    rsi_series: Optional[pd.Series] = None,
   635	) -> StrengthIndicators:
   636	    if errors is None:
   637	        errors = []
   638	
   639	    result = StrengthIndicators()
   640	
   641	    adx_res = calculate_adx(df, errors=errors)
   642	    result.adx       = adx_res.adx
   643	    result.plus_di   = adx_res.plus_di
   644	    result.minus_di  = adx_res.minus_di
   645	    result.adx_score = adx_res.adx_score
   646	    result.di_score  = adx_res.di_score
   647	    # [BUG-FIX KRITIS -- SAMA PERSIS dgn bug momentum.py di Sub-Batch A.2]
   648	    # di_score_short SEBELUMNYA TIDAK PERNAH disalin ke result -- sejak
   649	    # Batch 2, di jalur produksi asli (observer.py -> score_strength()),
   650	    # iset.strength.di_score_short SELALU None. Additive fix, di_score
   651	    # (long) TIDAK disentuh.
   652	    result.di_score_short = adx_res.di_score_short
   653	    adx_ok = result.adx is not None
   654	    di_ok  = result.plus_di is not None
   655	
   656	    vol_res = calculate_volume_analysis(df, errors=errors)
   657	    result.volume_ratio  = vol_res.volume_ratio
   658	    result.volume_spike  = vol_res.volume_spike
   659	    result.obv           = vol_res.obv
   660	    result.obv_trend     = vol_res.obv_trend
   661	    result.volume_climax = vol_res.volume_climax
   662	    result.volume_score  = vol_res.volume_score
   663	    # [BUG-FIX KRITIS -- sama persis]
   664	    result.volume_score_short = vol_res.volume_score_short
   665	    vol_ok = result.volume_ratio is not None
   666	
   667	    mfi_res = calculate_money_flow(df, errors=errors, rsi_series=rsi_series)
   668	    result.mfi           = mfi_res.mfi
   669	    result.mfi_divergence = mfi_res.mfi_divergence
   670	    result.mfi_score     = mfi_res.mfi_score
   671	    # [BUG-FIX KRITIS -- sama persis]
   672	    result.mfi_score_short = mfi_res.mfi_score_short
   673	    mfi_ok = result.mfi is not None
   674	
   675	    sub_indicators = [
   676	        (_ADX_WEIGHT,    adx_ok, result.adx_score),
   677	        (_DI_WEIGHT,     di_ok,  result.di_score),
   678	        (_VOLUME_WEIGHT, vol_ok, result.volume_score),
   679	        (_MFI_WEIGHT,    mfi_ok, result.mfi_score),
   680	    ]
   681	
   682	    total_weight_available = sum(w for w, ok, _ in sub_indicators if ok)
   683	
   684	    if total_weight_available < 1e-6:
   685	        errors.append("strength: tidak ada sub-indikator yang valid, composite = neutral")
   686	        result.composite_score = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   687	        result.composite_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   688	        return result
   689	
   690	    composite = 0.0
   691	    for base_w, ok, score in sub_indicators:
   692	        if not ok:
   693	            continue
   694	        adjusted_w  = base_w / total_weight_available
   695	        composite  += score * adjusted_w
   696	
   697	    result.composite_score = clamp_score(composite)
   698	
   699	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.3, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
   700	    # composite_score_short: reuse ok-flags & bobot yg SAMA dgn long.
   701	    # adx_score TIDAK punya versi _short (ADX cuma ukur MAGNITUDE kekuatan
   702	    # tren, bukan arah -- arah-agnostic, sama seperti spread_score/
   703	    # liquidity_score di orderbook Batch 7) -- dipakai IDENTIK di kedua
   704	    # sisi. di_score/volume_score/mfi_score genuinely directional, pakai
   705	    # versi _short (di_score_short dari Batch 2, volume_score_short &
   706	    # mfi_score_short dari Batch 3 -- semua BARU BENAR terisi setelah
   707	    # bug-fix di atas).
   708	    sub_indicators_short = [
   709	        (_ADX_WEIGHT,    adx_ok, result.adx_score),        # arah-agnostic, sama persis
   710	        (_DI_WEIGHT,     di_ok,  result.di_score_short),
   711	        (_VOLUME_WEIGHT, vol_ok, result.volume_score_short),
   712	        (_MFI_WEIGHT,    mfi_ok, result.mfi_score_short),
   713	    ]
   714	    composite_short = 0.0
   715	    for base_w, ok, score in sub_indicators_short:
   716	        if not ok:
   717	            continue
   718	        adjusted_w = base_w / total_weight_available
   719	        composite_short += score * adjusted_w
   720	
   721	    result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(composite_short)
   722	
   723	    log.debug(
   724	        "strength composite: adx=%.1f di=%.1f vol=%.1f mfi=%.1f → composite=%.1f",
   725	        result.adx_score, result.di_score, result.volume_score, result.mfi_score, result.composite_score,
   726	    )
   727	
   728	    return result
   729	
   730	def calculate_all(
   731	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   732	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   733	) -> StrengthIndicators:
   734	    return score_strength(df, errors=errors)

──────────────────────────────────────────
 FILE: engine/indicators/structure.py
