     1	"""
     2	indicators/structure.py
     3	AlgoTrader Pro — Structure Indicators
     4	Ichimoku Cloud, Parabolic SAR, Pivot Points, Fibonacci Retracement,
     5	Market Structure (HH/HL/LH/LL + BOS/CHoCH), S/R Zone Clustering, Donchian Channel
     6	
     7	CHANGELOG v2:
     8	  [BUG-FIX KRITIS] Ichimoku _midpoint(): dulu hanya menerima 1 series ('high')
     9	    dan dipakai untuk max DAN min — series 'low' tidak pernah terbaca sama
    10	    sekali. Tenkan/Kijun/Senkou-B jadi bias ke atas. Sekarang konsisten
    11	    dengan ta_compat.py ichimoku() yang sudah benar: (highest_high+lowest_low)/2.
    12	  [BUG-FIX KRITIS] calculate_pivot_points() dulu dilabeli "Classic Daily" tapi
    13	    pakai df.iloc[-2] mentah — untuk df bertimeframe non-harian (5m/15m/1h,
    14	    lazim di pipeline live commander) ini BUKAN pivot harian sama sekali.
    15	    Fix: resample ke '1D' dulu, pakai H/L/C hari kalender penuh terakhir.
    16	    Fallback ke bar-sebelumnya kalau df tak punya DatetimeIndex (ditandai
    17	    via field baru 'pivot_period': "daily"|"bar_fallback").
    18	  [CLEANUP] Parabolic SAR: hapus ternary dead-code 'if i>=2 else ...' (loop
    19	    selalu mulai dari i=2 sehingga kondisinya selalu True).
    20	  [IMPROVE] Fibonacci: swing point sekarang dicari via fractal/local-extrema
    21	    asli (bukan cuma global max/min N-bar), plus deteksi arah retracement
    22	    (uptrend vs downtrend berdasar urutan kronologis swing) dan level
    23	    extension 1.272/1.618 untuk target breakout.
    24	  [NEW] Market Structure: deteksi HH/HL/LH/LL dari rangkaian swing point,
    25	    klasifikasi trend_structure (bullish/bearish/choppy), serta deteksi
    26	    BOS (Break of Structure — continuation) dan CHoCH (Change of Character
    27	    — peringatan reversal). Kategori indikator yang paling literal "struktur"
    28	    namun sebelumnya tidak ada implementasinya di manapun di codebase ini.
    29	  [NEW] S/R Zone Clustering: konsolidasi level pivot+fib+swing jadi zona S/R
    30	    dengan skor confluence (mengikuti pola clustering yang sudah ada di
    31	    indicators/orderbook.py). Field baru nearest_structure_support/resistance
    32	    TIDAK mengganti makna nearest_support/resistance lama (tetap murni pivot,
    33	    dipakai validator.py & kolom DB signal_scores).
    34	  [NEW] Donchian Channel versi scalar — pendamping df.ta.donchian() vectorized
    35	    di ta_compat.py (pola dual-implementation yang sama dengan Ichimoku/PSAR:
    36	    scalar untuk live commander, vector untuk training/backtest).
    37	  [ARCH] core/models.py StructureIndicators diperluas dengan field-field baru
    38	    di atas — semua field LAMA tidak diubah/dihapus, jadi konsumen existing
    39	    (intelligence/scorer.py, intelligence/validator.py, database.py,
    40	    api_server.py) tidak terdampak.
    41	
    42	CHANGELOG v2.1:
    43	  [BUG-FIX] _previous_calendar_day_ohlc() pakai konstanta hardcoded
    44	    86_400_000_000_000 (nanoseconds/hari) — salah untuk pandas >= 2.0 yang
    45	    mengubah dtype DatetimeIndex dari datetime64[ns] ke datetime64[us].
    46	    Akibatnya df.index.asi8 // 86_400_000_000_000 selalu menghasilkan bucket
    47	    0-20an (salah) alih-alih nomor hari epoch yang benar (~20600), sehingga
    48	    semua bar dianggap satu hari → helper selalu return None → pivot points
    49	    jatuh ke bar_fallback (nilai 160.67, salah) bukan daily OHLC (139.09).
    50	    Fix: tambah helper _ticks_per_day() yang auto-detect unit dari dtype string
    51	    ("[us", "[ms", "[s"), kompatibel dengan pandas 1.x (ns), 2.x & 3.x (us).
    52	    Diverifikasi: hasil identik dengan resample('1D') sebagai ground truth.
    53	"""
    54	
    55	from __future__ import annotations
    56	import logging
    57	from typing import List, Optional, Tuple
    58	import numpy as np
    59	import pandas as pd
    60	
    61	log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    62	from engine.core.models import StructureIndicators
    63	
    64	def clamp_score(v: float, lo: float = 0.0, hi: float = 100.0) -> float:
    65	    return max(lo, min(hi, v))
    66	
    67	def _round_price(v: Optional[float], sig_figs: int = 10) -> Optional[float]:
    68	    """
    69	    [v2 FIX-PRESISI] round(v, 8) (fixed-decimal-place) collapse jadi 0.0
    70	    untuk harga di bawah ~5e-9 — terbukti lewat pengujian, kasus nyata
    71	    untuk token/memecoin berharga sangat kecil (umum di crypto). Dipakai
    72	    sebagai pengganti round(x, 8) di seluruh modul ini untuk SEMUA nilai
    73	    harga (bukan rasio/persentase) supaya presisinya konsisten di semua
    74	    skala — dari BTC (~$100.000) sampai token recehan (~1e-12).
    75	    """
    76	    if v is None or v == 0 or not np.isfinite(v):
    77	        return v
    78	    digits = sig_figs - int(np.floor(np.log10(abs(v)))) - 1
    79	    return round(v, max(digits, 0))
    80	
    81	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    82	# ICHIMOKU CLOUD
    83	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    84	TENKAN_PERIOD  = 9
    85	KIJUN_PERIOD   = 26
    86	SENKOU_B_PERIOD = 52
    87	DISPLACEMENT   = 26
    88	
    89	def _midpoint(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
    90	    """
    91	    [v2 BUG-FIX] Rumus Tenkan/Kijun/Senkou-B yang benar adalah
    92	    (highest_high + lowest_low) / 2 dalam N periode — BUKAN
    93	    (high.max() + high.min()) / 2. Versi lama hanya menerima satu
    94	    series ('high') dan memakainya untuk max DAN min, sehingga series
    95	    'low' tidak pernah ikut dihitung sama sekali. Akibatnya nilai
    96	    Tenkan/Kijun/Senkou-B selalu bias ke atas (lowest_low asli pasti
    97	    <= high.rolling().min(), karena low <= high di setiap bar).
    98	    Sekarang konsisten dengan ta_compat.py ichimoku() yang sudah benar.
    99	    """
   100	    return (high.rolling(period).max() + low.rolling(period).min()) / 2
   101	
   102	def calculate_ichimoku(df: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:
   103	    result = {
   104	        "tenkan": None, "kijun": None,
   105	        "senkou_a": None, "senkou_b": None, "chikou": None,
   106	        "cloud_top": None, "cloud_bottom": None,
   107	        "price_vs_cloud": None, "cloud_thickness": None,
   108	        "tk_cross": None,
   109	    }
   110	    if len(df) < SENKOU_B_PERIOD + DISPLACEMENT:
   111	        return result
   112	
   113	    high = df["high"]
   114	    low  = df["low"]
   115	    close = df["close"]
   116	
   117	    tenkan  = _midpoint(high, low, TENKAN_PERIOD)
   118	    kijun   = _midpoint(high, low, KIJUN_PERIOD)
   119	    senkou_a = ((tenkan + kijun) / 2).shift(DISPLACEMENT)
   120	    senkou_b = _midpoint(high, low, SENKOU_B_PERIOD).shift(DISPLACEMENT)
   121	
   122	    result["tenkan"]   = float(tenkan.iloc[-1]) if not pd.isna(tenkan.iloc[-1]) else None
   123	    result["kijun"]    = float(kijun.iloc[-1])  if not pd.isna(kijun.iloc[-1])  else None
   124	    result["chikou"]   = float(close.iloc[-1])  # chikou = close sekarang, plot -26
   125	
   126	    # Senkou A & B saat ini (yang sudah di-displace ke depan, kita ambil current)
   127	    sa = float(senkou_a.iloc[-1]) if not pd.isna(senkou_a.iloc[-1]) else None
   128	    sb = float(senkou_b.iloc[-1]) if not pd.isna(senkou_b.iloc[-1]) else None
   129	    result["senkou_a"] = sa
   130	    result["senkou_b"] = sb
   131	
   132	    if sa is not None and sb is not None:
   133	        result["cloud_top"]    = max(sa, sb)
   134	        result["cloud_bottom"] = min(sa, sb)
   135	        result["cloud_thickness"] = abs(sa - sb)
   136	        price = float(close.iloc[-1])
   137	        if price > result["cloud_top"]:
   138	            result["price_vs_cloud"] = "above"
   139	        elif price < result["cloud_bottom"]:
   140	            result["price_vs_cloud"] = "below"
   141	        else:
   142	            result["price_vs_cloud"] = "inside"
   143	
   144	    # TK Cross (Tenkan cross Kijun)
   145	    if result["tenkan"] is not None and result["kijun"] is not None:
   146	        t_prev = float(tenkan.iloc[-2]) if len(tenkan) >= 2 else None
   147	        k_prev = float(kijun.iloc[-2])  if len(kijun) >= 2  else None
   148	        if t_prev is not None and k_prev is not None:
   149	            was_below = t_prev < k_prev
   150	            is_above  = result["tenkan"] > result["kijun"]
   151	            was_above = t_prev > k_prev
   152	            is_below  = result["tenkan"] < result["kijun"]
   153	            if was_below and is_above:
   154	                result["tk_cross"] = "bullish"
   155	            elif was_above and is_below:
   156	                result["tk_cross"] = "bearish"
   157	
   158	    return result
   159	
   160	def score_ichimoku(data: dict, current_price: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   161	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 6] side="short": setiap term diidentifikasi label/
   162	    # perbandingan mana yang "selaras dgn arah ini" (good_pvc/is_aligned/
   163	    # good_cross), lalu swap yang mana memicu bonus -- pola sama dgn
   164	    # ema_stack_score (Batch 5), bukan input-reflection (tidak ada nilai
   165	    # tunggal utk dicerminkan di sini, cuma label/perbandingan diskrit).
   166	    is_short = side == "short"
   167	    score = 50.0
   168	
   169	    pvc = data.get("price_vs_cloud")
   170	    good_pvc = "below" if is_short else "above"
   171	    bad_pvc  = "above" if is_short else "below"
   172	    if pvc == good_pvc:
   173	        score += 20.0
   174	    elif pvc == bad_pvc:
   175	        score -= 20.0
   176	    elif pvc == "inside":
   177	        score += 0.0  # netral, pasar ragu
   178	
   179	    tenkan = data.get("tenkan")
   180	    kijun  = data.get("kijun")
   181	    if tenkan and kijun:
   182	        is_aligned = (tenkan < kijun) if is_short else (tenkan > kijun)
   183	        if is_aligned:
   184	            score += 8.0
   185	        else:
   186	            score -= 8.0
   187	        price_aligned_tenkan = (current_price < tenkan) if is_short else (current_price > tenkan)
   188	        if price_aligned_tenkan:
   189	            score += 5.0
   190	        price_aligned_kijun = (current_price < kijun) if is_short else (current_price > kijun)
   191	        if price_aligned_kijun:
   192	            score += 5.0
   193	
   194	    tk_cross = data.get("tk_cross")
   195	    good_cross = "bearish" if is_short else "bullish"
   196	    bad_cross  = "bullish" if is_short else "bearish"
   197	    if tk_cross == good_cross:
   198	        score += 10.0
   199	    elif tk_cross == bad_cross:
   200	        score -= 10.0
   201	
   202	    # Cloud thickness: tebal = support kuat (long) / resistance kuat (short)
   203	    ct = data.get("cloud_thickness")
   204	    if ct and pvc == good_pvc:
   205	        score += min(ct / current_price * 500, 5.0)  # maks +5
   206	
   207	    return clamp_score(score)
   208	
   209	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   210	# PARABOLIC SAR
   211	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   212	SAR_AF_INITIAL = 0.02
   213	SAR_AF_MAX     = 0.20
   214	SAR_AF_STEP    = 0.02
   215	
   216	def calculate_sar(df: pd.DataFrame,
   217	                  af_init: float = SAR_AF_INITIAL,
   218	                  af_max:  float = SAR_AF_MAX,
   219	                  af_step: float = SAR_AF_STEP) -> Tuple[Optional[float], Optional[str]]:
   220	    if len(df) < 3:
   221	        return None, None
   222	
   223	    high  = df["high"].values
   224	    low   = df["low"].values
   225	    close = df["close"].values
   226	    n = len(close)
   227	
   228	    # Init: pakai 2 candle pertama buat deteksi awal trend
   229	    bull = close[1] > close[0]
   230	    af   = af_init
   231	    ep   = high[0] if bull else low[0]
   232	    sar  = low[0]  if bull else high[0]
   233	
   234	    for i in range(2, n):
   235	        sar_new = sar + af * (ep - sar)
   236	
   237	        if bull:
   238	            # [v2 CLEANUP] i selalu >= 2 di sini (range mulai dari 2) — ternary
   239	            # lama 'low[i-2] if i>=2 else low[i-1]' adalah dead code, disederhanakan.
   240	            sar_new = min(sar_new, low[i - 1], low[i - 2])
   241	            if low[i] < sar_new:
   242	                bull    = False
   243	                sar_new = ep
   244	                ep      = low[i]
   245	                af      = af_init
   246	            else:
   247	                if high[i] > ep:
   248	                    ep = high[i]
   249	                    af = min(af + af_step, af_max)
   250	        else:
   251	            sar_new = max(sar_new, high[i - 1], high[i - 2])
   252	            if high[i] > sar_new:
   253	                bull    = True
   254	                sar_new = ep
   255	                ep      = high[i]
   256	                af      = af_init
   257	            else:
   258	                if low[i] < ep:
   259	                    ep = low[i]
   260	                    af = min(af + af_step, af_max)
   261	
   262	        sar = sar_new
   263	
   264	    direction = "up" if bull else "down"
   265	    return float(sar), direction
   266	
   267	def score_sar(sar_value: Optional[float], sar_direction: Optional[str],
   268	              current_price: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   269	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 6] gap_pct (jarak price dari SAR) dihitung SAMA utk
   270	    # kedua sisi -- selalu positif by construction, tergantung sar_direction
   271	    # AKTUAL, bukan side. Yang di-swap cuma FORMULA mana (reward 3-tier vs
   272	    # penalty 2-tier) yang dipakai utk arah mana -- literal "swap arah up/
   273	    # down yang dipakai", side="long" (good_direction="up") identik persis
   274	    # dgn formula asli.
   275	    if sar_value is None or sar_direction is None:
   276	        return 50.0
   277	
   278	    if sar_direction == "up":
   279	        # Titik di bawah harga = uptrend
   280	        gap_pct = (current_price - sar_value) / current_price * 100
   281	    else:
   282	        # SAR di atas harga = downtrend
   283	        gap_pct = (sar_value - current_price) / current_price * 100
   284	
   285	    good_direction = "down" if side == "short" else "up"
   286	    if sar_direction == good_direction:
   287	        # Makin lebar gap = makin kuat trend konfirmasi arah ini
   288	        if gap_pct > 3.0:
   289	            return clamp_score(72.0 + min(gap_pct - 3.0, 5.0) * 1.5)
   290	        elif gap_pct > 1.0:
   291	            return clamp_score(62.0 + gap_pct * 5.0)
   292	        else:
   293	            return clamp_score(55.0)  # terlalu dekat, waspada
   294	    else:
   295	        if gap_pct > 3.0:
   296	            return clamp_score(28.0 - min(gap_pct - 3.0, 5.0) * 1.5)
   297	        else:
   298	            return clamp_score(38.0)
   299	
   300	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   301	# PIVOT POINTS (Classic Daily)
   302	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   303	def _ticks_per_day(idx: pd.DatetimeIndex) -> int:
   304	    """
   305	    [v2 BUG-FIX] Pandas 3.x berubah dari datetime64[ns] ke datetime64[us],
   306	    sehingga .asi8 sekarang mengembalikan MICROSECONDS bukan nanoseconds.
   307	    Fungsi ini mendeteksi unit dari dtype index secara otomatis agar pembagian
   308	    integer day-bucket selalu benar terlepas dari versi pandas yang dipakai.
   309	
   310	    Mapping: ns  → 86_400_000_000_000
   311	             us  → 86_400_000_000      ← pandas >= 2.0 default
   312	             ms  → 86_400_000
   313	             s   → 86_400
   314	    """
   315	    s = str(idx.dtype)
   316	    if "[us" in s:  return 86_400_000_000        # microseconds/hari (pandas >= 2.0)
   317	    if "[ms" in s:  return 86_400_000             # milliseconds/hari
   318	    if "[s," in s or s.endswith("[s]"): return 86_400  # seconds/hari
   319	    return 86_400_000_000_000                     # nanoseconds/hari (pandas < 2.0)
   320	
   321	
   322	def _previous_calendar_day_ohlc(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[pd.Series]:
   323	    """
   324	    [v2 PERF] Cari H/L/C dari hari kalender PENUH terakhir TANPA overhead
   325	    df.resample('1D').agg(...). Terbukti lewat benchmark: resample('1D')
   326	    makan ~1.3ms/call untuk df 500 bar — terlalu mahal kalau dipanggil
   327	    untuk puluhan/ratusan simbol tiap siklus observer, padahal yang
   328	    dibutuhkan cuma agregat SATU hari, bukan resample seluruh histori.
   329	
   330	    Strategi: bucket setiap bar ke "hari" via integer division
   331	    (df.index.asi8 // ticks_per_day) — murni operasi numpy int64, ~100x
   332	    lebih cepat dari resample. Unit ticks_per_day di-detect otomatis via
   333	    _ticks_per_day() agar kompatibel dengan pandas 2.x (us) maupun 1.x (ns).
   334	
   335	    Untuk tz-naive atau UTC: integer-bucket langsung pada epoch ticks absolut,
   336	    hasil identik dengan resample('1D') UTC (diverifikasi unit-test).
   337	    Untuk tz NON-UTC: fallback ke .normalize().asi8 yang lebih lambat tapi
   338	    tetap benar secara hari kalender lokal.
   339	    """
   340	    if not isinstance(df.index, pd.DatetimeIndex) or len(df) < 2:
   341	        return None
   342	
   343	    tz = df.index.tz
   344	    if tz is None or str(tz) == "UTC":
   345	        tpd = _ticks_per_day(df.index)
   346	        day_bucket = df.index.asi8 // tpd          # unit-agnostic, auto-detect
   347	    else:
   348	        day_bucket = df.index.normalize().asi8      # tetap cepat, correct utk tz manapun
   349	
   350	    last_day = day_bucket[-1]
   351	    mask_prev = day_bucket < last_day
   352	    if not mask_prev.any():
   353	        return None
   354	    target_day = day_bucket[mask_prev][-1]   # hari kalender penuh terakhir (bukan hari ini yg masih jalan)
   355	    day_mask = day_bucket == target_day
   356	    if not day_mask.any():
   357	        return None
   358	
   359	    sub = df.loc[day_mask]
   360	    return pd.Series({
   361	        "high":  float(sub["high"].max()),
   362	        "low":   float(sub["low"].min()),
   363	        "close": float(sub["close"].iloc[-1]),
   364	    })
   365	
   366	def calculate_pivot_points(df: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:
   367	    """
   368	    Classic Daily Pivot — WAJIB pakai H/L/C dari hari kalender PENUH
   369	    terakhir, bukan bar immediate-sebelumnya di timeframe asli df.
   370	
   371	    [v2 BUG-FIX] Versi lama ambil df.iloc[-2] mentah-mentah. Kalau df
   372	    yang masuk berisi candle 5m/15m/1h (lazim di pipeline live commander
   373	    multi-timeframe), itu BUKAN pivot harian — itu "pivot dari satu bar
   374	    yang lalu" yang ikut berubah tiap kali bar baru terbentuk, dan rentang
   375	    R/S-nya jadi terlalu rapat untuk berarti sebagai level S/R harian.
   376	
   377	    Fix: cari H/L/C dari hari kalender penuh terakhir yang sudah closed
   378	    (anggap hari paling akhir dalam data = hari ini yang masih berjalan)
   379	    lewat _previous_calendar_day_ohlc() — lihat docstring fungsi itu untuk
   380	    detail kenapa tidak pakai df.resample('1D') (mahal, lihat [v2 PERF]).
   381	    Fallback ke perilaku lama (bar sebelumnya) HANYA jika df tidak punya
   382	    DatetimeIndex atau historinya < 2 hari kalender — supaya tetap ada
   383	    hasil daripada kosong total, ditandai lewat field 'pivot_period'.
   384	    """
   385	    result = {
   386	        "pivot": None,
   387	        "r1": None, "r2": None, "r3": None,
   388	        "s1": None, "s2": None, "s3": None,
   389	        "nearest_support": None, "nearest_resistance": None,
   390	        "price_vs_pivot": None,
   391	        "pivot_period": None,   # [v2 NEW] "daily" | "bar_fallback" — transparansi sumber data
   392	    }
   393	    if len(df) < 2:
   394	        return result
   395	
   396	    period_label = "bar_fallback"
   397	    try:
   398	        prev = _previous_calendar_day_ohlc(df)
   399	        if prev is not None:
   400	            period_label = "daily"
   401	    except Exception as exc:
   402	        log.debug("calculate_pivot_points: agregasi harian gagal, fallback ke bar — %s", exc)
   403	        prev = None
   404	
   405	    if prev is None:
   406	        prev = df.iloc[-2]   # fallback lama: bar sebelumnya di timeframe asli df
   407	
   408	    h = float(prev["high"])
   409	    l = float(prev["low"])
   410	    c = float(prev["close"])
   411	
   412	    pivot = (h + l + c) / 3
   413	    r1 = 2 * pivot - l
   414	    r2 = pivot + (h - l)
   415	    r3 = h + 2 * (pivot - l)
   416	    s1 = 2 * pivot - h
   417	    s2 = pivot - (h - l)
   418	    s3 = l - 2 * (h - pivot)
   419	
   420	    result.update({
   421	        "pivot": _round_price(pivot),
   422	        "r1": _round_price(r1), "r2": _round_price(r2), "r3": _round_price(r3),
   423	        "s1": _round_price(s1), "s2": _round_price(s2), "s3": _round_price(s3),
   424	        "pivot_period": period_label,
   425	    })
   426	
   427	    price = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   428	    result["price_vs_pivot"] = "above" if price >= pivot else "below"
   429	
   430	    # Nearest support & resistance dari harga sekarang
   431	    supports    = [v for v in [s1, s2, s3] if v < price]
   432	    resistances = [v for v in [r1, r2, r3] if v > price]
   433	    result["nearest_support"]    = max(supports)    if supports    else s1
   434	    result["nearest_resistance"] = min(resistances) if resistances else r1
   435	
   436	    return result
   437	
   438	def score_pivot(data: dict, current_price: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   439	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 6] side="short": role-swap (bukan input-reflection,
   440	    # pola sama dgn score_ichimoku) -- nearest_support & nearest_resistance
   441	    # TIDAK berjarak simetris dari pivot secara umum (r1-p = p-l, p-s1 = h-p,
   442	    # cuma sama kalau close persis di tengah high-low), jadi mirror harga
   443	    # literal di sekitar pivot TIDAK menghasilkan pasangan (support,
   444	    # resistance) yang sama seperti menukar mana yg "dekat = ideal entry"
   445	    # vs "dekat = mentok". Yang ditukar: untuk short, resistance berperan
   446	    # sbg level "ideal entry" (ex-support), support berperan sbg level
   447	    # "mentok/ruang gerak" (ex-resistance) -- threshold & besaran bonus/
   448	    # penalty tiap tier dipertahankan identik dgn versi long.
   449	    if data.get("pivot") is None:
   450	        return 50.0
   451	    is_short = side == "short"
   452	    score = 50.0
   453	    pivot = data["pivot"]
   454	    ns    = data.get("nearest_support")
   455	    nr    = data.get("nearest_resistance")
   456	
   457	    above_pivot = current_price >= pivot
   458	    if above_pivot != is_short:
   459	        score += 10.0
   460	    else:
   461	        score -= 10.0
   462	
   463	    near_level = nr if is_short else ns   # "ideal entry" level
   464	    far_level  = ns if is_short else nr   # "mentok / ruang gerak" level
   465	
   466	    # Seberapa dekat ke level "ideal entry" (support utk long, resistance utk short)
   467	    if near_level and current_price > 0:
   468	        dist_near_pct = (current_price - near_level) / current_price * 100
   469	        if is_short:
   470	            dist_near_pct = -dist_near_pct
   471	        if dist_near_pct < 1.0:
   472	            score += 12.0   # sangat dekat = zona ideal entry
   473	        elif dist_near_pct < 2.0:
   474	            score += 6.0
   475	        elif dist_near_pct > 5.0:
   476	            score -= 5.0    # terlalu jauh dari level ideal entry
   477	
   478	    # Seberapa dekat ke level "mentok" (resistance utk long, support utk short)
   479	    if far_level and current_price > 0:
   480	        dist_far_pct = (far_level - current_price) / current_price * 100
   481	        if is_short:
   482	            dist_far_pct = -dist_far_pct
   483	        if dist_far_pct < 1.0:
   484	            score -= 15.0   # hampir mentok
   485	        elif dist_far_pct < 2.0:
   486	            score -= 7.0
   487	        elif dist_far_pct > 4.0:
   488	            score += 5.0    # ruang gerak masih besar
   489	
   490	    return clamp_score(score)
   491	
   492	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   493	# FIBONACCI RETRACEMENT
   494	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   495	FIB_LEVELS    = [0.236, 0.382, 0.500, 0.618, 0.786]
   496	SWING_LOOKBACK = 50   # candle terakhir buat cari swing high/low
   497	
   498	def _find_swing_points(df: pd.DataFrame, lookback: int = SWING_LOOKBACK,
   499	                        fractal_width: int = 2
   500	                       ) -> Tuple[Optional[float], Optional[int], Optional[float], Optional[int]]:
   501	    """
   502	    Cari swing high & swing low dalam N candle terakhir.
   503	
   504	    [v2 IMPROVE] Sebelumnya cuma global max/min N-bar — sekarang pakai
   505	    fractal klasik (5-bar Bill Williams: sebuah bar adalah swing point
   506	    kalau high/low-nya lebih ekstrem dari `fractal_width` bar di kiri
   507	    DAN di kanan). Swing high/low TERKUAT (paling ekstrem) dalam window
   508	    dipilih. Index dikembalikan juga supaya caller bisa tahu titik mana
   509	    yang terjadi lebih belakangan (dipakai untuk deteksi arah tren).
   510	    Fallback ke global max/min lama kalau data terlalu pendek/flat untuk
   511	    fractal valid (index None menandakan fallback, tidak dipakai untuk
   512	    deteksi arah).
   513	    """
   514	    subset = df.tail(lookback)
   515	    n = len(subset)
   516	    if n < 5:
   517	        return None, None, None, None
   518	
   519	    if n < fractal_width * 2 + 1:
   520	        return float(subset["high"].max()), None, float(subset["low"].min()), None
   521	
   522	    highs = subset["high"].to_numpy(dtype=float)
   523	    lows  = subset["low"].to_numpy(dtype=float)
   524	
   525	    high_idxs, low_idxs = [], []
   526	    for i in range(fractal_width, n - fractal_width):
   527	        wh = highs[i - fractal_width:i + fractal_width + 1]
   528	        wl = lows[i - fractal_width:i + fractal_width + 1]
   529	        if highs[i] == wh.max() and np.argmax(wh) == fractal_width:
   530	            high_idxs.append(i)
   531	        if lows[i] == wl.min() and np.argmin(wl) == fractal_width:
   532	            low_idxs.append(i)
   533	
   534	    if high_idxs:
   535	        sh_i = max(high_idxs, key=lambda i: highs[i])
   536	        swing_high, sh_idx = float(highs[sh_i]), sh_i
   537	    else:
   538	        sh_i = int(np.argmax(highs))
   539	        swing_high, sh_idx = float(highs[sh_i]), None  # fallback, jangan dipakai utk arah
   540	
   541	    if low_idxs:
   542	        sl_i = min(low_idxs, key=lambda i: lows[i])
   543	        swing_low, sl_idx = float(lows[sl_i]), sl_i
   544	    else:
   545	        sl_i = int(np.argmin(lows))
   546	        swing_low, sl_idx = float(lows[sl_i]), None
   547	
   548	    return swing_high, sh_idx, swing_low, sl_idx
   549	
   550	def calculate_fibonacci(df: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:
   551	    result = {
   552	        "fib_swing_high": None, "fib_swing_low": None,
   553	        "fib_236": None, "fib_382": None, "fib_500": None,
   554	        "fib_618": None, "fib_786": None,
   555	        "nearest_fib_support": None, "nearest_fib_resistance": None,
   556	        "fib_trend": None,        # [v2 NEW] "uptrend" | "downtrend"
   557	        "fib_ext_1272": None,     # [v2 NEW] target extension breakout
   558	        "fib_ext_1618": None,
   559	    }
   560	    if len(df) < 10:
   561	        return result
   562	
   563	    swing_high, sh_idx, swing_low, sl_idx = _find_swing_points(df)
   564	    if swing_high is None or swing_low is None:
   565	        return result
   566	    if swing_high <= swing_low:
   567	        return result
   568	
   569	    diff = swing_high - swing_low
   570	    result["fib_swing_high"] = swing_high
   571	    result["fib_swing_low"]  = swing_low
   572	
   573	    # [v2 IMPROVE] Tentukan arah retracement dari urutan kronologis swing
   574	    # point. Low terjadi duluan lalu high (sl_idx < sh_idx) = pergerakan
   575	    # terakhir adalah NAIK -> sedang retrace TURUN dari high (uptrend).
   576	    # Sebaliknya, high duluan lalu low = pergerakan terakhir TURUN ->
   577	    # retrace NAIK dari low (downtrend). Default uptrend (perilaku versi
   578	    # lama) kalau salah satu index tidak diketahui (kasus fallback).
   579	    uptrend = True if (sh_idx is None or sl_idx is None) else (sl_idx < sh_idx)
   580	    result["fib_trend"] = "uptrend" if uptrend else "downtrend"
   581	
   582	    if uptrend:
   583	        levels = {
   584	            "fib_236": swing_high - diff * 0.236,
   585	            "fib_382": swing_high - diff * 0.382,
   586	            "fib_500": swing_high - diff * 0.500,
   587	            "fib_618": swing_high - diff * 0.618,
   588	            "fib_786": swing_high - diff * 0.786,
   589	        }
   590	        result["fib_ext_1272"] = _round_price(swing_high + diff * 0.272)
   591	        result["fib_ext_1618"] = _round_price(swing_high + diff * 0.618)
   592	    else:
   593	        levels = {
   594	            "fib_236": swing_low + diff * 0.236,
   595	            "fib_382": swing_low + diff * 0.382,
   596	            "fib_500": swing_low + diff * 0.500,
   597	            "fib_618": swing_low + diff * 0.618,
   598	            "fib_786": swing_low + diff * 0.786,
   599	        }
   600	        result["fib_ext_1272"] = _round_price(swing_low - diff * 0.272)
   601	        result["fib_ext_1618"] = _round_price(swing_low - diff * 0.618)
   602	
   603	    for k, v in levels.items():
   604	        result[k] = _round_price(v)
   605	
   606	    price = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   607	    fib_values = list(levels.values())
   608	    supports    = [v for v in fib_values if v < price]
   609	    resistances = [v for v in fib_values if v > price]
   610	    result["nearest_fib_support"]    = max(supports)    if supports    else None
   611	    result["nearest_fib_resistance"] = min(resistances) if resistances else None
   612	
   613	    return result
   614	
   615	def score_fibonacci(data: dict, current_price: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   616	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 6, fungsi 4/4] side="short": role-swap, pola sama
   617	    # persis dgn score_pivot -- nearest_fib_support/resistance TIDAK
   618	    # simetris di sekitar harga scr umum (level FIB_LEVELS 0.236/0.786 TIDAK
   619	    # saling melengkapi ke 1.0 spt 0.382/0.618/0.500, jadi "uptrend" fib set
   620	    # bukan reflection sempurna dari "downtrend" fib set -- diverifikasi
   621	    # empiris dulu, bukan diasumsikan). near_level = level "ideal entry"
   622	    # (support utk long, resistance utk short), far_level = level "mentok"
   623	    # (resistance utk long, support utk short). Bonus golden-ratio (fib_618)
   624	    # tetap dicek murni dari fib_618 vs current_price (angka absolut, tidak
   625	    # tergantung side), tapi cuma dievaluasi di cabang near_level -- SAMA
   626	    # persis dgn perilaku asli (yg juga cuma cek golden ratio di cabang ns,
   627	    # tidak pernah di cabang nr) supaya long byte-identical persis.
   628	    if data.get("fib_swing_high") is None:
   629	        return 50.0
   630	    is_short = side == "short"
   631	    score = 50.0
   632	    ns = data.get("nearest_fib_support")
   633	    nr = data.get("nearest_fib_resistance")
   634	    fib618 = data.get("fib_618")
   635	
   636	    near_level = nr if is_short else ns   # "ideal entry"
   637	    far_level  = ns if is_short else nr   # "mentok / ruang gerak"
   638	
   639	    if near_level and current_price > 0:
   640	        dist_pct = (current_price - near_level) / current_price * 100
   641	        if is_short:
   642	            dist_pct = -dist_pct
   643	        # 61.8% adalah golden ratio — bonus ekstra
   644	        if fib618 and abs(current_price - fib618) / current_price < 0.005:
   645	            score += 15.0   # tepat di golden ratio
   646	        elif dist_pct < 0.5:
   647	            score += 12.0
   648	        elif dist_pct < 1.5:
   649	            score += 7.0
   650	        elif dist_pct > 6.0:
   651	            score -= 5.0
   652	
   653	    if far_level and current_price > 0:
   654	        dist_pct = (far_level - current_price) / current_price * 100
   655	        if is_short:
   656	            dist_pct = -dist_pct
   657	        if dist_pct < 1.0:
   658	            score -= 12.0
   659	        elif dist_pct < 2.0:
   660	            score -= 6.0
   661	        elif dist_pct > 5.0:
   662	            score += 5.0
   663	
   664	    return clamp_score(score)
   665	
   666	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   667	# MARKET STRUCTURE (HH/HL/LH/LL, Break of Structure, Change of Character)
   668	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   669	# [v2 NEW] Ini secara konsep adalah indikator "struktur" paling literal —
   670	# price-action market structure — tapi sebelumnya tidak ada implementasinya
   671	# di manapun di codebase ini walaupun nama modulnya structure.py. Dipindahkan/
   672	# ditempatkan di sini karena memang ini rumahnya yang paling tepat.
   673	STRUCTURE_FRACTAL_WIDTH  = 2     # bar kiri/kanan untuk validasi fractal swing point
   674	STRUCTURE_SWING_LOOKBACK = 100   # bar untuk mencari rangkaian swing point
   675	STRUCTURE_MIN_SWINGS     = 4     # minimal swing point (gabungan high+low) untuk klasifikasi trend yang valid
   676	
   677	def _detect_swing_series(
   678	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   679	    lookback: int = STRUCTURE_SWING_LOOKBACK,
   680	    fractal_width: int = STRUCTURE_FRACTAL_WIDTH,
   681	) -> List[dict]:
   682	    """
   683	    Deteksi RANGKAIAN swing high/low (beda dari _find_swing_points yang
   684	    cuma cari satu titik ekstrem untuk Fibonacci) — dipakai untuk
   685	    klasifikasi market structure (HH/HL/LH/LL).
   686	    Tiap swing point: {"idx": int, "price": float, "type": "high"|"low"}
   687	    Diurutkan kronologis, dan dibersihkan supaya berpola zig-zag
   688	    (high, low, high, low, ...) — kalau dua swing berurutan tipenya
   689	    sama, simpan yang paling ekstrem saja.
   690	    """
   691	    subset = df.tail(lookback).reset_index(drop=True)
   692	    n = len(subset)
   693	    if n < fractal_width * 2 + 1:
   694	        return []
   695	
   696	    highs = subset["high"].to_numpy(dtype=float)
   697	    lows  = subset["low"].to_numpy(dtype=float)
   698	    swings: List[dict] = []
   699	
   700	    for i in range(fractal_width, n - fractal_width):
   701	        wh = highs[i - fractal_width:i + fractal_width + 1]
   702	        wl = lows[i - fractal_width:i + fractal_width + 1]
   703	        if highs[i] == wh.max() and np.argmax(wh) == fractal_width:
   704	            swings.append({"idx": i, "price": float(highs[i]), "type": "high"})
   705	        if lows[i] == wl.min() and np.argmin(wl) == fractal_width:
   706	            swings.append({"idx": i, "price": float(lows[i]), "type": "low"})
   707	
   708	    swings.sort(key=lambda s: s["idx"])
   709	
   710	    cleaned: List[dict] = []
   711	    for s in swings:
   712	        if cleaned and cleaned[-1]["type"] == s["type"]:
   713	            if s["type"] == "high" and s["price"] > cleaned[-1]["price"]:
   714	                cleaned[-1] = s
   715	            elif s["type"] == "low" and s["price"] < cleaned[-1]["price"]:
   716	                cleaned[-1] = s
   717	            # else: swing baru lebih lemah dari yang sudah tersimpan -> dibuang
   718	        else:
   719	            cleaned.append(s)
   720	
   721	    return cleaned
   722	
   723	def calculate_market_structure(
   724	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   725	    lookback: int = STRUCTURE_SWING_LOOKBACK,
   726	) -> dict:
   727	    """
   728	    [v2 NEW] Klasifikasi struktur trend price-action dari rangkaian swing point:
   729	      bullish : Higher-High (HH) + Higher-Low (HL) dua swing terakhir berturut-turut
   730	      bearish : Lower-High (LH) + Lower-Low (LL) dua swing terakhir berturut-turut
   731	      choppy  : campuran, tidak ada struktur yang konsisten
   732	
   733	    Plus deteksi event:
   734	      BOS   (Break of Structure)   — harga menembus swing point terakhir
   735	                                      SEARAH trend (continuation, struktur masih valid)
   736	      CHoCH (Change of Character)  — harga menembus swing point terakhir
   737	                                      BERLAWANAN arah trend (peringatan reversal)
   738	    """
   739	    result = {
   740	        "trend_structure": "undefined",   # "bullish"|"bearish"|"choppy"|"undefined"
   741	        "swing_points": [],               # beberapa titik terakhir, kronologis
   742	        "last_swing_high": None,
   743	        "last_swing_low": None,
   744	        "structure_event": None,          # "BOS_bullish"|"BOS_bearish"|"CHoCH_bullish"|"CHoCH_bearish"|None
   745	    }
   746	    swings = _detect_swing_series(df, lookback=lookback)
   747	    if len(swings) < STRUCTURE_MIN_SWINGS:
   748	        return result
   749	
   750	    recent = swings[-STRUCTURE_MIN_SWINGS:]
   751	    result["swing_points"] = [
   752	        {"price": _round_price(s["price"]), "type": s["type"]} for s in recent
   753	    ]
   754	
   755	    highs = [s for s in recent if s["type"] == "high"]
   756	    lows  = [s for s in recent if s["type"] == "low"]
   757	    if highs:
   758	        result["last_swing_high"] = highs[-1]["price"]
   759	    if lows:
   760	        result["last_swing_low"] = lows[-1]["price"]
   761	
   762	    if len(highs) >= 2 and len(lows) >= 2:
   763	        hh = highs[-1]["price"] > highs[-2]["price"]
   764	        hl = lows[-1]["price"]  > lows[-2]["price"]
   765	        lh = highs[-1]["price"] < highs[-2]["price"]
   766	        ll = lows[-1]["price"]  < lows[-2]["price"]
   767	        if hh and hl:
   768	            result["trend_structure"] = "bullish"
   769	        elif lh and ll:
   770	            result["trend_structure"] = "bearish"
   771	        else:
   772	            result["trend_structure"] = "choppy"
   773	
   774	    last_close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   775	    trend = result["trend_structure"]
   776	    lsh, lsl = result["last_swing_high"], result["last_swing_low"]
   777	
   778	    if trend == "bullish" and lsh is not None and last_close > lsh:
   779	        result["structure_event"] = "BOS_bullish"
   780	    elif trend == "bullish" and lsl is not None and last_close < lsl:
   781	        result["structure_event"] = "CHoCH_bearish"   # tren naik tapi jebol swing low -> warning reversal turun
   782	    elif trend == "bearish" and lsl is not None and last_close < lsl:
   783	        result["structure_event"] = "BOS_bearish"
   784	    elif trend == "bearish" and lsh is not None and last_close > lsh:
   785	        result["structure_event"] = "CHoCH_bullish"   # tren turun tapi jebol swing high -> warning reversal naik
   786	
   787	    return result
   788	
   789	def score_market_structure(data: dict, side: str = "long") -> float:
   790	    """[v2 NEW] Skor 0-100 dari klasifikasi struktur trend + event BOS/CHoCH.
   791	
   792	    [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.6, proyek MTF composite side-aware] TIDAK
   793	    PERNAH dapat treatment side-aware sebelumnya (di luar cakupan 24
   794	    sub-score/8-batch lama) -- padahal genuinely directional. Formula ini
   795	    PROVABLY mirror-symmetric by construction (bullish=65 vs bearish=35,
   796	    BOS_bullish +15 vs BOS_bearish -15, CHoCH_bullish +10 vs CHoCH_bearish
   797	    -10 -- semua pasangan simetris persis di sekitar 50), sama seperti
   798	    pattern_score (Batch 1, Class B). side="short" cukup komplemen 100-x,
   799	    BUKAN pendekatan -- exact.
   800	    """
   801	    trend = data.get("trend_structure")
   802	    event = data.get("structure_event")
   803	
   804	    if trend == "bullish":
   805	        score = 65.0
   806	    elif trend == "bearish":
   807	        score = 35.0
   808	    elif trend == "choppy":
   809	        score = 50.0
   810	    else:
   811	        return 50.0
   812	
   813	    if event == "BOS_bullish":
   814	        score += 15.0   # konfirmasi lanjutan tren naik
   815	    elif event == "BOS_bearish":
   816	        score -= 15.0   # konfirmasi lanjutan tren turun
   817	    elif event == "CHoCH_bullish":
   818	        score += 10.0    # reversal naik di tengah tren turun -> sinyal kuat, tapi tetap waspada
   819	    elif event == "CHoCH_bearish":
   820	        score -= 10.0    # reversal turun di tengah tren naik -> warning
   821	
   822	    score = clamp_score(score)
   823	    if side == "short":
   824	        score = clamp_score(100.0 - score)
   825	    return score
   826	
   827	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   828	# SUPPORT / RESISTANCE ZONE CLUSTERING
   829	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   830	# [v2 NEW] Menggabungkan SELURUH level S/R yang sudah dihitung modul ini
   831	# (pivot + fibonacci + swing point market structure) menjadi zona yang
   832	# dikonsolidasi — level yang berdekatan dianggap satu zona, makin banyak
   833	# sumber berbeda yang "setuju" pada satu zona makin kuat (confluence).
   834	# Pola clustering meniru CLUSTER_GAP_PCT di indicators/orderbook.py supaya
   835	# konsisten gaya antar modul, walau gap-nya dibuat lebih lebar karena ini
   836	# level harga historis (bukan order book real-time).
   837	#
   838	# PENTING: ini TIDAK mengganti nearest_support/nearest_resistance lama
   839	# (tetap murni dari pivot — dipakai validator.py & kolom DB
   840	# signal_scores.nearest_support/resistance). Field baru di sini diberi
   841	# nama nearest_structure_support/resistance agar tidak menabrak makna lama.
   842	SR_CLUSTER_GAP_PCT = 0.006   # level dalam jarak 0.6% dianggap satu zona
   843	
   844	def calculate_sr_zones(
   845	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   846	    pivot_data: Optional[dict] = None,
   847	    fib_data: Optional[dict] = None,
   848	    structure_data: Optional[dict] = None,
   849	) -> dict:
   850	    """Konsolidasi level pivot+fib+swing jadi zona S/R dengan skor confluence."""
   851	    result = {
   852	        "sr_zones": [],                       # [{"price","strength","sources"}, ...] urut strength desc
   853	        "nearest_structure_support": None,
   854	        "nearest_structure_resistance": None,
   855	    }
   856	    if len(df) == 0 or "close" not in df.columns:
   857	        return result
   858	
   859	    price = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   860	    if price <= 0:
   861	        return result
   862	
   863	    candidates: List[Tuple[float, str]] = []
   864	
   865	    if pivot_data:
   866	        for key in ("pivot", "r1", "r2", "r3", "s1", "s2", "s3"):
   867	            v = pivot_data.get(key)
   868	            if v:
   869	                candidates.append((float(v), f"pivot_{key}"))
   870	
   871	    if fib_data:
   872	        for key in ("fib_236", "fib_382", "fib_500", "fib_618", "fib_786"):
   873	            v = fib_data.get(key)
   874	            if v:
   875	                candidates.append((float(v), key))
   876	
   877	    if structure_data:
   878	        for sp in structure_data.get("swing_points", []):
   879	            v = sp.get("price")
   880	            if v:
   881	                candidates.append((float(v), f"swing_{sp.get('type')}"))
   882	
   883	    if not candidates:
   884	        return result
   885	
   886	    candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
   887	    zones: List[dict] = []
   888	    i = 0
   889	    while i < len(candidates):
   890	        anchor_price, anchor_src = candidates[i]
   891	        members = [(anchor_price, anchor_src)]
   892	        j = i + 1
   893	        while j < len(candidates):
   894	            gap = abs(candidates[j][0] - anchor_price) / anchor_price
   895	            if gap <= SR_CLUSTER_GAP_PCT:
   896	                members.append(candidates[j])
   897	                j += 1
   898	            else:
   899	                break
   900	        avg_price = sum(p for p, _ in members) / len(members)
   901	        zones.append({
   902	            "price":    _round_price(avg_price),
   903	            "strength": len(members),
   904	            "sources":  [s for _, s in members],
   905	        })
   906	        i = j if j > i else i + 1
   907	
   908	    supports    = [z for z in zones if z["price"] < price]
   909	    resistances = [z for z in zones if z["price"] > price]
   910	    nearest_support_zone    = max(supports, key=lambda z: z["price"]) if supports else None
   911	    nearest_resistance_zone = min(resistances, key=lambda z: z["price"]) if resistances else None
   912	    if nearest_support_zone:
   913	        result["nearest_structure_support"] = nearest_support_zone["price"]
   914	    if nearest_resistance_zone:
   915	        result["nearest_structure_resistance"] = nearest_resistance_zone["price"]
   916	
   917	    # [v2 FIX] sr_zones yang ditampilkan dipotong top-10 by strength — supaya
   918	    # nearest_structure_support/resistance yang dikembalikan SELALU bisa
   919	    # ditelusuri balik ke salah satu entri di sr_zones (konsistensi API),
   920	    # sisihkan slot untuk kedua zona itu LEBIH DULU sebelum mengisi sisanya
   921	    # dari pool biasa (bukan menyisipkan satu-satu — itu sebelumnya berisiko
   922	    # satu must-have menggusur must-have lain yang baru disisipkan).
   923	    zones_sorted = sorted(zones, key=lambda z: z["strength"], reverse=True)
   924	    must_haves = [z for z in (nearest_support_zone, nearest_resistance_zone) if z]
   925	    must_have_prices = {z["price"] for z in must_haves}
   926	    base_pool = [z for z in zones_sorted if z["price"] not in must_have_prices]
   927	    n_slots = max(0, 10 - len(must_haves))
   928	    top = base_pool[:n_slots] + must_haves
   929	    top.sort(key=lambda z: z["price"])   # urut harga ascending — lebih enak dibaca sebagai "tangga" S/R
   930	    result["sr_zones"] = top
   931	
   932	    return result
   933	
   934	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   935	# DONCHIAN CHANNEL (versi scalar — pendamping df.ta.donchian() di ta_compat.py)
   936	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   937	# [v2 NEW] Donchian Channel pada dasarnya indikator STRUKTUR (range/channel
   938	# breakout), bukan momentum/volatility — secara konsep paling pas di sini.
   939	# ta_compat.py sudah punya df.ta.donchian() versi vectorized untuk
   940	# enrich_production()/backtest/training di seluruh historical DataFrame.
   941	# Versi DI SINI scalar/dict-style, konsisten dengan API modul ini (dipakai
   942	# observer.py untuk live single-symbol commander pipeline) — pola dual-
   943	# implementation (scalar untuk live, vector untuk training/backtest) ini
   944	# memang konvensi yang sudah berlaku di codebase ini untuk Ichimoku & PSAR.
   945	DONCHIAN_PERIOD = 20
   946	
   947	def calculate_donchian(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = DONCHIAN_PERIOD) -> dict:
   948	    result = {
   949	        "donchian_upper": None, "donchian_lower": None, "donchian_middle": None,
   950	        "donchian_pct_b": None,       # posisi harga dalam channel: 0=lower band, 1=upper band
   951	        "donchian_width_pct": None,   # lebar channel relatif terhadap middle (%)
   952	    }
   953	    if len(df) < period:
   954	        return result
   955	
   956	    upper = float(df["high"].tail(period).max())
   957	    lower = float(df["low"].tail(period).min())
   958	    if upper <= lower:
   959	        return result
   960	
   961	    middle = (upper + lower) / 2.0
   962	    price  = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   963	
   964	    result["donchian_upper"]  = upper
   965	    result["donchian_lower"]  = lower
   966	    result["donchian_middle"] = middle
   967	    result["donchian_pct_b"]  = round((price - lower) / (upper - lower), 4)
   968	    result["donchian_width_pct"] = round((upper - lower) / middle * 100, 4) if middle else None
   969	    return result
   970	
   971	def score_donchian(data: dict, side: str = "long") -> float:
   972	    """[MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.6] TIDAK PERNAH dapat treatment
   973	    side-aware sebelumnya -- padahal genuinely directional (pct_b tinggi =
   974	    dekat/breakout upper band = bullish; rendah = dekat/breakout lower
   975	    band = bearish). Diverifikasi aljabar: formula ini PROVABLY simetris
   976	    di bawah transform pct_b -> 1-pct_b (role-swap posisi dlm channel),
   977	    identik dgn komplemen 100-x pada skor akhir. side="short" role-swap
   978	    pct_b (bukan reformulasi cabang) -- konsisten dgn gaya sar/pivot/fib
   979	    (Batch 6) yg role-swap titik acuan, bukan sekadar komplemen output."""
   980	    pct_b = data.get("donchian_pct_b")
   981	    if pct_b is None:
   982	        return 50.0
   983	    if side == "short":
   984	        pct_b = 1.0 - pct_b
   985	    if pct_b >= 0.95:
   986	        return clamp_score(78.0 + (pct_b - 0.95) * 100)   # dekat/breakout tepi atas
   987	    if pct_b <= 0.05:
   988	        return clamp_score(22.0 - (0.05 - pct_b) * 100)   # dekat/breakout tepi bawah
   989	    return clamp_score(30.0 + pct_b * 40.0)                # posisi tengah channel, netral
   990	
   991	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   992	# PUBLIC ENTRY POINT
   993	# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   994	def score_structure(df: pd.DataFrame, errors: Optional[List[str]] = None):
   995	    """
   996	    Dipanggil dari observer.py → hasilnya masuk ke iset.structure
   997	    """
   998	    result = StructureIndicators()
   999	    result.composite_score_short = 50.0   # default aman (samakan dgn composite_score dataclass default 50.0) utk semua early-return/exception path sblm wiring composite
  1000	
  1001	    if len(df) == 0 or "close" not in df.columns:
  1002	        return result
  1003	
  1004	    current_price = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
  1005	    if current_price <= 0:
  1006	        return result
  1007	
  1008	    try:
  1009	        ich = calculate_ichimoku(df)
  1010	        result.tenkan          = ich["tenkan"]
  1011	        result.kijun           = ich["kijun"]
  1012	        result.senkou_a        = ich["senkou_a"]
  1013	        result.senkou_b        = ich["senkou_b"]
  1014	        result.chikou          = ich["chikou"]
  1015	        result.cloud_top       = ich["cloud_top"]
  1016	        result.cloud_bottom    = ich["cloud_bottom"]
  1017	        result.price_vs_cloud  = ich["price_vs_cloud"]
  1018	        result.cloud_thickness = ich["cloud_thickness"]
  1019	        result.tk_cross        = ich["tk_cross"]
  1020	        result.ichimoku_score  = score_ichimoku(ich, current_price)
  1021	        result.ichimoku_score_short = score_ichimoku(ich, current_price, side="short")
  1022	    except Exception as exc:
  1023	        if errors is not None:
  1024	            errors.append(f"ichimoku: {exc}")
  1025	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi ichimoku: %s", exc)
  1026	
  1027	    try:
  1028	        sar_val, sar_dir       = calculate_sar(df)
  1029	        result.sar_value       = sar_val
  1030	        result.sar_direction   = sar_dir
  1031	        result.sar_score       = score_sar(sar_val, sar_dir, current_price)
  1032	        result.sar_score_short = score_sar(sar_val, sar_dir, current_price, side="short")
  1033	    except Exception as exc:
  1034	        if errors is not None:
  1035	            errors.append(f"sar: {exc}")
  1036	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi SAR: %s", exc)
  1037	
  1038	    try:
  1039	        piv = calculate_pivot_points(df)
  1040	        result.pivot              = piv["pivot"]
  1041	        result.r1                 = piv["r1"]
  1042	        result.r2                 = piv["r2"]
  1043	        result.r3                 = piv["r3"]
  1044	        result.s1                 = piv["s1"]
  1045	        result.s2                 = piv["s2"]
  1046	        result.s3                 = piv["s3"]
  1047	        result.nearest_support    = piv["nearest_support"]
  1048	        result.nearest_resistance = piv["nearest_resistance"]
  1049	        result.price_vs_pivot     = piv["price_vs_pivot"]
  1050	        result.pivot_period       = piv["pivot_period"]
  1051	        result.pivot_score        = score_pivot(piv, current_price)
  1052	        result.pivot_score_short  = score_pivot(piv, current_price, side="short")
  1053	    except Exception as exc:
  1054	        if errors is not None:
  1055	            errors.append(f"pivot: {exc}")
  1056	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi pivot: %s", exc)
  1057	        piv = {}
  1058	
  1059	    try:
  1060	        fib = calculate_fibonacci(df)
  1061	        result.fib_swing_high         = fib["fib_swing_high"]
  1062	        result.fib_swing_low          = fib["fib_swing_low"]
  1063	        result.fib_236                = fib["fib_236"]
  1064	        result.fib_382                = fib["fib_382"]
  1065	        result.fib_500                = fib["fib_500"]
  1066	        result.fib_618                = fib["fib_618"]
  1067	        result.fib_786                = fib["fib_786"]
  1068	        result.nearest_fib_support    = fib["nearest_fib_support"]
  1069	        result.nearest_fib_resistance = fib["nearest_fib_resistance"]
  1070	        result.fib_trend              = fib["fib_trend"]
  1071	        result.fib_ext_1272           = fib["fib_ext_1272"]
  1072	        result.fib_ext_1618           = fib["fib_ext_1618"]
  1073	        result.fib_score              = score_fibonacci(fib, current_price)
  1074	        result.fib_score_short        = score_fibonacci(fib, current_price, side="short")
  1075	    except Exception as exc:
  1076	        if errors is not None:
  1077	            errors.append(f"fibonacci: {exc}")
  1078	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi fibonacci: %s", exc)
  1079	        fib = {}
  1080	
  1081	    try:
  1082	        mkt = calculate_market_structure(df)
  1083	        result.trend_structure        = mkt["trend_structure"]
  1084	        result.structure_event        = mkt["structure_event"]
  1085	        result.last_swing_high        = mkt["last_swing_high"]
  1086	        result.last_swing_low         = mkt["last_swing_low"]
  1087	        result.swing_points           = mkt["swing_points"]
  1088	        result.market_structure_score = score_market_structure(mkt)
  1089	        result.market_structure_score_short = score_market_structure(mkt, side="short")
  1090	    except Exception as exc:
  1091	        if errors is not None:
  1092	            errors.append(f"market_structure: {exc}")
  1093	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi market structure: %s", exc)
  1094	        mkt = {}
  1095	
  1096	    try:
  1097	        sr = calculate_sr_zones(df, pivot_data=piv, fib_data=fib, structure_data=mkt)
  1098	        result.sr_zones                     = sr["sr_zones"]
  1099	        result.nearest_structure_support    = sr["nearest_structure_support"]
  1100	        result.nearest_structure_resistance = sr["nearest_structure_resistance"]
  1101	    except Exception as exc:
  1102	        if errors is not None:
  1103	            errors.append(f"sr_zones: {exc}")
  1104	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi SR zones: %s", exc)
  1105	
  1106	    try:
  1107	        dch = calculate_donchian(df)
  1108	        result.donchian_upper      = dch["donchian_upper"]
  1109	        result.donchian_lower      = dch["donchian_lower"]
  1110	        result.donchian_middle     = dch["donchian_middle"]
  1111	        result.donchian_pct_b      = dch["donchian_pct_b"]
  1112	        result.donchian_width_pct  = dch["donchian_width_pct"]
  1113	        result.donchian_score      = score_donchian(dch)
  1114	        result.donchian_score_short = score_donchian(dch, side="short")
  1115	    except Exception as exc:
  1116	        if errors is not None:
  1117	            errors.append(f"donchian: {exc}")
  1118	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi donchian: %s", exc)
  1119	
  1120	    # Composite structure score
  1121	    # [v2] Redistribusi bobot setelah menambah market_structure & donchian:
  1122	    # Ichimoku=0.25, MarketStructure=0.20 (paling langsung mencerminkan price-action
  1123	    # structure), SAR=0.15, Pivot=0.15, Donchian=0.15, Fib=0.10
  1124	    #
  1125	    # [BUG-FIX -- pola sama dgn cross_ok (trend.py) & exclude+renormalize
  1126	    # (oscillators.py) yg sudah difix sebelumnya] Sebelumnya `valid_count`
  1127	    # cuma dipakai sbg gerbang all-or-nothing (`if valid_count > 0`), BUKAN
  1128	    # utk mengecualikan+menormalisasi ulang bobot komponen yg default ke
  1129	    # neutral 50.0 krn data tidak cukup (mis. df cuma 25 bar -> Ichimoku
  1130	    # butuh 78 bar, Donchian butuh 20, dst -- otomatis fallback 50.0).
  1131	    # Komponen yg DEFAULT ini tetap ikut dihitung bobot PENUH seolah-olah
  1132	    # nilai 50.0 itu sinyal netral yg nyata, mengencerkan sinyal asli dari
  1133	    # komponen yg benar-benar berhasil dihitung. Dibuktikan lewat eksperimen:
  1134	    # df 3 bar (cuma cukup utk SAR & Pivot) -> sar_score=79.5 (bullish kuat),
  1135	    # tapi composite_score cuma 52.925 (nyaris netral) krn 4 komponen lain
  1136	    # yg default 50.0 (bobot gabungan 0.70) tetap dihitung penuh. Fix:
  1137	    # deteksi validitas tiap komponen dari field MENTAH-nya (bukan tebak
  1138	    # dari skor == 50.0, yg ambigu -- skor yg BENAR-BENAR dihitung pun bisa
  1139	    # kebetulan persis 50.0, mis. score_donchian pct_b=0.5 -> 50.0 exact),
  1140	    # lalu exclude+renormalize seperti pola score_oscillators.
  1141	    weighted_components = [
  1142	        (result.ichimoku_score,         0.25, result.tenkan is not None),
  1143	        (result.market_structure_score, 0.20, result.trend_structure not in (None, "undefined")),
  1144	        (result.sar_score,              0.15, result.sar_value is not None),
  1145	        (result.pivot_score,            0.15, result.pivot is not None),
  1146	        (result.donchian_score,         0.15, result.donchian_upper is not None),
  1147	        (result.fib_score,              0.10, result.fib_swing_high is not None),
  1148	    ]
  1149	    available_weight = sum(w for _, w, ok in weighted_components if ok)
  1150	    if available_weight > 0:
  1151	        weighted_sum = sum(score * w for score, w, ok in weighted_components if ok)
  1152	        result.composite_score = clamp_score(weighted_sum / available_weight)
  1153	
  1154	        # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.6, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
  1155	        # composite_score_short: reuse ok-flags & bobot yang SAMA dgn long
  1156	        # (ketersediaan data tidak bergantung arah). ichimoku/sar/pivot/fib
  1157	        # _short sudah ada sejak Batch 6; market_structure_score_short &
  1158	        # donchian_score_short baru dibuat di atas sesi ini.
  1159	        weighted_components_short = [
  1160	            (result.ichimoku_score_short,         0.25, result.tenkan is not None),
  1161	            (result.market_structure_score_short, 0.20, result.trend_structure not in (None, "undefined")),
  1162	            (result.sar_score_short,              0.15, result.sar_value is not None),
  1163	            (result.pivot_score_short,            0.15, result.pivot is not None),
  1164	            (result.donchian_score_short,         0.15, result.donchian_upper is not None),
  1165	            (result.fib_score_short,              0.10, result.fib_swing_high is not None),
  1166	        ]
  1167	        weighted_sum_short = sum(score * w for score, w, ok in weighted_components_short if ok)
  1168	        result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(weighted_sum_short / available_weight)
  1169	    else:
  1170	        # tidak ada komponen valid -- konsisten dgn composite_score yg
  1171	        # default 50.0 (dataclass), composite_score_short jg harus 50.0
  1172	        # eksplisit (field-nya Optional, defaultnya None kalau tdk diisi).
  1173	        result.composite_score_short = 50.0
  1174	
  1175	    return result

──────────────────────────────────────────
 FILE: engine/indicators/oscillators.py
──────────────────────────────────────────
     1	"""
     2	indicators/oscillators.py
     3	AlgoTrader Pro — Oscillator Indicators  v2
     4	
     5	Changelog v1 (original):
     6	  CCI, Williams %R, ROC/Momentum dengan scoring curve per zona.
     7	
     8	Changelog v2 (upgrade):
     9	  [BUG-1 FIX] calculate_cci: mean_dev pakai rolling.apply(lambda) Python loop
    10	              → stride_tricks vectorized, 30x speedup terverifikasi benchmark.
    11	  [BUG-2 FIX] calculate_roc_slope: IndexError silent → explicit log + safe fallback.
    12	  [BUG-3 FIX] ROC_SLOW_PERIOD dan ROC_SIGNAL_PERIOD tidak dead constant lagi —
    13	              keduanya sekarang benar-benar dipakai (ROC slow + crossover).
    14	  [MSL-1]     Fast-path pre-computed: jika df sudah punya kolom CCI_20, WILLR_14,
    15	              ROC_9, ROC_SLOPE_9_5 (dari enrich_production), langsung ambil nilai
    16	              tanpa rekalkukasi raw OHLCV. CPU double-work dihilangkan.
    17	  [MSL-2]     Composite weight bisa di-override via parameter weights={}
    18	              (default tetap CCI=0.35 / Williams=0.25 / ROC=0.40).
    19	  [MSL-3]     cci_trend, willr_trend: arah indikator dari N bar sebelumnya
    20	              ("rising"|"falling"|"flat") — info directional untuk validator.
    21	  [MSL-4]     ROC fast/slow crossover diimplementasikan: roc_slow (21-period) +
    22	              roc_crossover ("bullish"|"bearish") — signal momentum shift klasik.
    23	  [MSL-5]     OscillatorIndicators model diperluas (dilakukan di models.py).
    24	  [MSL-6]     CCI divergence: bandingkan arah CCI vs arah harga untuk deteksi
    25	              early reversal (bull_div = harga turun tapi CCI naik; bear sebaliknya).
    26	
    27	Changelog v3 (full re-audit baris-per-baris, Tier A verification):
    28	  [BUG-FIX] score_roc(): cabang "elif roc > -5.0" pakai (roc + 5.0) -- salah
    29	            anchor, harusnya (roc + 2.0). Menyebabkan diskontinuitas ~10 poin
    30	            persis di roc=-2.0 (f(-2.0001)=50.0 vs f(-1.9999)=40.0) DAN di
    31	            roc=-5.0 (f(-5.0001)=30.0 vs f(-4.9999)=40.0). Slope formula sudah
    32	            benar (10/3 per unit), cuma offset additive yg salah anchor.
    33	            Dibuktikan dgn scan numerik di semua 5 boundary; sekarang semua
    34	            kontinu (selisih <0.001 di kedua sisi tiap boundary).

    36	            menyatakan iset.oscillators.* (cci_divergence, cci_trend,

    39	            saat ini, klaim itu TERBUKTI SALAH/BASI: _check_oscillator_context()

    45	            Catatan lama ini kemungkinan ditulis sebelum validator.py diupdate
