    50	from __future__ import annotations
    51	
    52	import logging
    53	from typing import Dict, List, Optional
    54	
    55	import numpy as np
    56	import pandas as pd
    57	from numpy.lib.stride_tricks import sliding_window_view
    58	
    59	log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    60	from engine.core.models import OscillatorIndicators
    61	
    62	# ── Constants ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    63	CCI_PERIOD          = 20
    64	CCI_OVERBOUGHT      = 100.0
    65	CCI_OVERSOLD        = -100.0
    66	CCI_EXTREME_OB      = 200.0
    67	CCI_EXTREME_OS      = -200.0
    68	CCI_TREND_LOOKBACK  = 3      # bar lookback untuk deteksi cci_trend / willr_trend
    69	
    70	WILLIAMS_PERIOD     = 14
    71	WILLIAMS_OB         = -20.0
    72	WILLIAMS_OS         = -80.0
    73	
    74	ROC_FAST_PERIOD     = 9
    75	ROC_SLOW_PERIOD     = 21     # [BUG-3 FIX] sekarang benar-benar dipakai
    76	ROC_SIGNAL_PERIOD   = 5      # [BUG-3 FIX] sekarang benar-benar dipakai
    77	
    78	# Divergence lookback — bar untuk bandingkan puncak/lembah harga vs CCI
    79	CCI_DIV_LOOKBACK    = 10
    80	
    81	# Default composite weights
    82	_DEFAULT_WEIGHTS = {"cci": 0.35, "williams": 0.25, "roc": 0.40}
    83	
    84	
    85	def clamp_score(v: float, lo: float = 0.0, hi: float = 100.0) -> float:
    86	    return max(lo, min(hi, v))
    87	
    88	
    89	# ── CCI ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    90	def calculate_cci(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = CCI_PERIOD) -> Optional[float]:
    91	    """
    92	    [BUG-1 FIX] mean_dev vectorized via stride_tricks — 30x lebih cepat dari
    93	    rolling.apply(lambda). Hasil identik secara numerik.
    94	    """
    95	    if len(df) < period:
    96	        return None
    97	    tp = (df["high"] + df["low"] + df["close"]) / 3
    98	
    99	    # [BUG-1 FIX] stride_tricks menggantikan rolling.apply(lambda x: mean(abs(x-x.mean())))
   100	    arr  = tp.to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   101	    wins = sliding_window_view(arr, period)          # (n-period+1, period)
   102	    mu   = wins.mean(axis=1)
   103	    mad  = np.abs(wins - mu[:, None]).mean(axis=1)  # mean absolute deviation
   104	
   105	    denom = 0.015 * mad[-1]
   106	    if denom == 0:
   107	        return None
   108	    sma_last = mu[-1]
   109	    return float((arr[-1] - sma_last) / denom)
   110	
   111	
   112	def _cci_series(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = CCI_PERIOD, n: int = CCI_TREND_LOOKBACK + 1) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
   113	    """Hitung N nilai CCI terakhir untuk trend & divergence detection."""
   114	    needed = period + n - 1
   115	    if len(df) < needed:
   116	        return None
   117	    tp   = (df["high"] + df["low"] + df["close"]) / 3
   118	    arr  = tp.to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   119	    wins = sliding_window_view(arr, period)
   120	    mu   = wins.mean(axis=1)
   121	    mad  = np.abs(wins - mu[:, None]).mean(axis=1)
   122	    with np.errstate(divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
   123	        cci_arr = np.where(mad > 0, (arr[period - 1:] - mu) / (0.015 * mad), np.nan)
   124	    return cci_arr[-n:]   # N nilai terbaru
   125	
   126	
   127	def calculate_cci_trend(df: pd.DataFrame, lookback: int = CCI_TREND_LOOKBACK) -> Optional[str]:
   128	    """[MSL-3] Deteksi arah CCI: rising/falling/flat berdasarkan lookback bar."""
   129	    series = _cci_series(df, n=lookback + 1)
   130	    if series is None or np.any(np.isnan(series)):
   131	        return None
   132	    delta = series[-1] - series[0]
   133	    if delta > 5:
   134	        return "rising"
   135	    if delta < -5:
   136	        return "falling"
   137	    return "flat"
   138	
   139	
   140	def calculate_cci_divergence(df: pd.DataFrame, lookback: int = CCI_DIV_LOOKBACK) -> Optional[float]:
   141	    """
   142	    [MSL-6] CCI divergence score.
   143	    Bull divergence: harga buat lower-low tapi CCI buat higher-low → early reversal up.
   144	    Bear divergence: harga buat higher-high tapi CCI buat lower-high → early reversal down.
   145	
   146	    Returns:
   147	        +nilai  = bullish divergence (kuat makin besar)
   148	        -nilai  = bearish divergence
   149	        None    = tidak ada divergence terdeteksi
   150	    """
   151	    needed = CCI_PERIOD + lookback
   152	    if len(df) < needed:
   153	        return None
   154	
   155	    cci_arr  = _cci_series(df, n=lookback + 1)
   156	    if cci_arr is None or np.any(np.isnan(cci_arr)):
   157	        return None
   158	
   159	    close_arr = df["close"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)[-(lookback + 1):]
   160	    price_mid = (close_arr[-1] + close_arr[0]) / 2
   161	
   162	    # Bandingkan first half vs second half
   163	    half = lookback // 2
   164	    price_early = close_arr[:half].min()
   165	    price_late  = close_arr[half:].min()
   166	    cci_early   = cci_arr[:half].min()
   167	    cci_late    = cci_arr[half:].min()
   168	
   169	    price_early_h = close_arr[:half].max()
   170	    price_late_h  = close_arr[half:].max()
   171	    cci_early_h   = cci_arr[:half].max()
   172	    cci_late_h    = cci_arr[half:].max()
   173	
   174	    # Bull divergence: price lower-low + CCI higher-low
   175	    bull_div = 0.0
   176	    if price_late < price_early and cci_late > cci_early:
   177	        price_drop_pct = (price_early - price_late) / max(abs(price_mid), 1e-9) * 100
   178	        cci_recovery   = cci_late - cci_early
   179	        bull_div = min(price_drop_pct * 0.5 + cci_recovery * 0.1, 30.0)
   180	
   181	    # Bear divergence: price higher-high + CCI lower-high
   182	    bear_div = 0.0
   183	    if price_late_h > price_early_h and cci_late_h < cci_early_h:
   184	        price_rise_pct = (price_late_h - price_early_h) / max(abs(price_mid), 1e-9) * 100
   185	        cci_weakness   = cci_early_h - cci_late_h
   186	        bear_div = min(price_rise_pct * 0.5 + cci_weakness * 0.1, 30.0)
   187	
   188	    if bull_div > 2.0 and bull_div >= bear_div:
   189	        return round(bull_div, 2)
   190	    if bear_div > 2.0 and bear_div > bull_div:
   191	        return round(-bear_div, 2)
   192	    return None
   193	
   194	
   195	def score_cci(cci: Optional[float], side: str = "long") -> float:
   196	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 4, input-reflection] CCI simetris di sekitar 0 by
   197	    # construction (mean-deviation oscillator) -- mirror(cci) = -cci.
   198	    if cci is None:
   199	        return 50.0
   200	    if side == "short":
   201	        cci = -cci
   202	    if cci >= CCI_EXTREME_OB:
   203	        return 20.0
   204	    if cci >= CCI_OVERBOUGHT:
   205	        t = (cci - CCI_OVERBOUGHT) / (CCI_EXTREME_OB - CCI_OVERBOUGHT)
   206	        return clamp_score(65.0 - t * 45.0)
   207	    if cci >= 0:
   208	        t = cci / CCI_OVERBOUGHT
   209	        return clamp_score(50.0 + t * 15.0)
   210	    if cci >= CCI_OVERSOLD:
   211	        t = cci / CCI_OVERSOLD
   212	        return clamp_score(50.0 - t * 15.0)
   213	    if cci >= CCI_EXTREME_OS:
   214	        t = (cci - CCI_OVERSOLD) / (CCI_EXTREME_OS - CCI_OVERSOLD)
   215	        return clamp_score(35.0 + t * 45.0)
   216	    return 80.0   # extreme oversold = strong buy candidate
   217	
   218	
   219	# ── Williams %R ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   220	def calculate_williams_r(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = WILLIAMS_PERIOD) -> Optional[float]:
   221	    if len(df) < period:
   222	        return None
   223	    hh    = df["high"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)[-period:].max()
   224	    ll    = df["low"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)[-period:].min()
   225	    close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   226	    denom = hh - ll
   227	    if denom == 0:
   228	        return None
   229	    return float(((hh - close) / denom) * -100)
   230	
   231	
   232	def calculate_willr_trend(df: pd.DataFrame,
   233	                           period: int   = WILLIAMS_PERIOD,
   234	                           lookback: int = CCI_TREND_LOOKBACK) -> Optional[str]:
   235	    """[MSL-3] Arah Williams %R dari lookback bar terakhir."""
   236	    needed = period + lookback
   237	    if len(df) < needed:
   238	        return None
   239	    arr_h = df["high"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   240	    arr_l = df["low"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   241	    arr_c = df["close"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   242	    vals  = []
   243	    for i in range(lookback + 1):
   244	        offset = lookback - i          # 0 = oldest, lookback = newest
   245	        sl_h   = arr_h[-(period + offset): len(arr_h) - offset if offset else None]
   246	        sl_l   = arr_l[-(period + offset): len(arr_l) - offset if offset else None]
   247	        c      = arr_c[-(offset + 1)]
   248	        hh     = sl_h.max()
   249	        ll     = sl_l.min()
   250	        d      = hh - ll
   251	        if d == 0:
   252	            return None
   253	        vals.append(((hh - c) / d) * -100)
   254	    delta = vals[-1] - vals[0]
   255	    # Williams %R naik (ke arah 0) = overbought; turun (ke arah -100) = oversold
   256	    if delta > 3:
   257	        return "rising"   # bergerak ke arah overbought
   258	    if delta < -3:
   259	        return "falling"  # bergerak ke arah oversold
   260	    return "flat"
   261	
   262	
   263	def score_williams_r(wr: Optional[float], side: str = "long") -> float:
   264	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 4, input-reflection] Williams %R range [-100,0],
   265	    # midpoint -50 -- mirror(wr) = -100-wr (verified: mirror(0)=-100,
   266	    # mirror(-100)=0, mirror(-50)=-50 fixed point).
   267	    if wr is None:
   268	        return 50.0
   269	    if side == "short":
   270	        wr = -100.0 - wr
   271	    if wr >= -20:
   272	        t = (wr - (-20)) / (0 - (-20))
   273	        return clamp_score(30.0 - t * 10.0)
   274	    if wr >= -50:
   275	        t = (wr - (-50)) / (-20 - (-50))
   276	        return clamp_score(50.0 - t * 20.0)
   277	    if wr >= -80:
   278	        t = (wr - (-80)) / (-50 - (-80))
   279	        return clamp_score(70.0 - t * 20.0)
   280	    t = (wr - (-100)) / (-80 - (-100))
   281	    return clamp_score(85.0 - t * 15.0)
   282	
   283	
   284	# ── ROC / Momentum ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   285	def calculate_roc(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = ROC_FAST_PERIOD) -> Optional[float]:
   286	    if len(df) < period + 1:
   287	        return None
   288	    close = df["close"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   289	    prev  = close[-(period + 1)]
   290	    if prev == 0:
   291	        return None
   292	    return float(((close[-1] - prev) / prev) * 100)
   293	
   294	
   295	def calculate_roc_slow(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = ROC_SLOW_PERIOD) -> Optional[float]:
   296	    """[MSL-4] ROC slow (21-period default) untuk crossover dengan ROC fast."""
   297	    return calculate_roc(df, period=period)
   298	
   299	
   300	def calculate_roc_crossover(roc_fast: Optional[float],
   301	                             roc_slow: Optional[float]) -> Optional[str]:
   302	    """
   303	    [MSL-4] ROC fast/slow crossover.
   304	    Bullish: roc_fast > roc_slow (momentum cepat melampaui lambat).
   305	    Bearish: roc_fast < roc_slow.
   306	    """
   307	    if roc_fast is None or roc_slow is None:
   308	        return None
   309	    if roc_fast > roc_slow + 0.1:   # buffer 0.1% hindari noise
   310	        return "bullish"
   311	    if roc_fast < roc_slow - 0.1:
   312	        return "bearish"
   313	    return None
   314	
   315	
   316	def calculate_roc_slope(df: pd.DataFrame,
   317	                         fast: int   = ROC_FAST_PERIOD,
   318	                         signal: int = ROC_SIGNAL_PERIOD) -> Optional[float]:
   319	    """
   320	    Slope of ROC — positif = momentum akselerasi, negatif = deselerasi.
   321	    [BUG-2 FIX] IndexError di-log secara eksplisit, tidak hilang diam-diam.
   322	    Loop 5-iterasi ini dipertahankan — overhead negligible vs pct_change full-series.
   323	    """
   324	    needed = fast + signal + 1
   325	    if len(df) < needed:
   326	        return None
   327	    close     = df["close"].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
   328	    roc_vals: list[float] = []
   329	    try:
   330	        for i in range(signal):
   331	            idx      = -(signal - i)
   332	            prev_idx = idx - fast
   333	            p = close[len(close) + prev_idx]
   334	            c = close[len(close) + idx]
   335	            if p == 0:
   336	                log.debug("calculate_roc_slope: prev price=0 di iterasi %d, return None", i)
   337	                return None
   338	            roc_vals.append(((c - p) / p) * 100)
   339	    except IndexError as exc:
   340	        log.debug("calculate_roc_slope: IndexError — df mungkin terlalu pendek: %s", exc)
   341	        return None
   342	    if len(roc_vals) < 2:
   343	        return None
   344	    return float(roc_vals[-1] - roc_vals[0])
   345	
   346	
   347	_ROC_CROSSOVER_MIRROR = {"bullish": "bearish", "bearish": "bullish"}
   348	
   349	
   350	def score_roc(roc: Optional[float], roc_slope: Optional[float] = None,
   351	              roc_crossover: Optional[str] = None, side: str = "long") -> float:
   352	    """[MSL-4] Score ROC dengan crossover sebagai modifier tambahan.
   353	
   354	    [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 4, input-reflection] mirror(roc)=-roc,
   355	    mirror(roc_slope)=-roc_slope (turunan seri yg dicerminkan, sama pola
   356	    dgn slope RSI di Batch 3), roc_crossover di-swap bullish<->bearish.
   357	    """
   358	    if roc is None:
   359	        return 50.0
   360	
   361	    if side == "short":
   362	        roc = -roc
   363	        roc_slope = -roc_slope if roc_slope is not None else None
   364	        roc_crossover = _ROC_CROSSOVER_MIRROR.get(roc_crossover, roc_crossover)
   365	
   366	    if roc > 5.0:
   367	        base = clamp_score(70.0 + min(roc - 5.0, 10.0) * 2.0)
   368	    elif roc > 2.0:
   369	        base = clamp_score(60.0 + (roc - 2.0) * (10.0 / 3.0))
   370	    elif roc > 0:
   371	        base = clamp_score(50.0 + roc * (10.0 / 2.0))
   372	    elif roc > -2.0:
   373	        base = clamp_score(50.0 + roc * (10.0 / 2.0))
   374	    elif roc > -5.0:
   375	        # [BUG-FIX] Sebelumnya (roc + 5.0) -- salah anchor, menyebabkan
   376	        # diskontinuitas ~10 poin persis di roc=-2.0 DAN roc=-5.0 (terbukti:
   377	        # f(-2.0001)=50.0 vs f(-1.9999)=40.0, lompat 10 poin di titik yg
   378	        # SAMA). Formula ini harus anchor ke titik -2.0 (di mana branch
   379	        # tetangga "roc > -2.0" berakhir di nilai 40.0), bukan ke -5.0.
   380	        # (roc + 2.0) menjaga slope sama (10/3 per unit) tapi anchor benar:
   381	        # f(-2)=40 (match branch atasnya), f(-5)=30 (match branch bawahnya).
   382	        base = clamp_score(40.0 + (roc + 2.0) * (10.0 / 3.0))
   383	    else:
   384	        base = clamp_score(30.0 - min(abs(roc) - 5.0, 10.0) * 2.0)
   385	
   386	    # Slope modifier — early warning kalau momentum melambat/akselerasi
   387	    if roc_slope is not None:
   388	        if roc > 0 and roc_slope < -1.0:
   389	            base -= 8.0
   390	        elif roc > 0 and roc_slope > 1.0:
   391	            base += 5.0
   392	        elif roc < 0 and roc_slope > 1.0:
   393	            base += 5.0
   394	
   395	    # [MSL-4] Crossover modifier
   396	    if roc_crossover == "bullish":
   397	        base += 6.0   # fast > slow = momentum shift positif
   398	    elif roc_crossover == "bearish":
   399	        base -= 6.0
   400	
   401	    return clamp_score(base)
   402	
   403	
   404	# ── Public entry point ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   405	def score_oscillators(
   406	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   407	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   408	    weights: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None,
   409	) -> OscillatorIndicators:
   410	    """
   411	    Hitung semua oscillator indicators dan return OscillatorIndicators.
   412	
   413	    [MSL-1] Fast-path: jika df sudah punya kolom pre-computed dari enrich_production()
   414	            (CCI_20, WILLR_14, ROC_9, ROC_SLOPE_9_5), langsung ambil nilainya —
   415	            tidak perlu rekalkukasi dari raw OHLCV. Hemat CPU signifikan per tick.
   416	
   417	    [MSL-2] weights: override bobot composite (default CCI=0.35/Williams=0.25/ROC=0.40).
   418	            Contoh: weights={"cci": 0.20, "williams": 0.20, "roc": 0.60}
   419	    """
   420	    w = {**_DEFAULT_WEIGHTS, **(weights or {})}
   421	    result = OscillatorIndicators()
   422	    result.composite_score_short = 50.0   # default aman jika exception terjadi sblm wiring composite
   423	    try:
   424	        # ── CCI ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   425	        # [MSL-1] Fast-path: pakai kolom pre-computed jika tersedia
   426	        if "CCI_20" in df.columns:
   427	            v = df["CCI_20"].iloc[-1]
   428	            result.cci = float(v) if pd.notna(v) else None
   429	        else:
   430	            result.cci = calculate_cci(df)
   431	
   432	        result.cci_score     = score_cci(result.cci)
   433	        result.cci_score_short = score_cci(result.cci, side="short")
   434	        result.cci_trend     = calculate_cci_trend(df)        # [MSL-3]
   435	        result.cci_divergence = calculate_cci_divergence(df)  # [MSL-6]
   436	
   437	        # ── Williams %R ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   438	        if "WILLR_14" in df.columns:
   439	            v = df["WILLR_14"].iloc[-1]
   440	            result.williams_r = float(v) if pd.notna(v) else None
   441	        else:
   442	            result.williams_r = calculate_williams_r(df)
   443	
   444	        result.williams_r_score = score_williams_r(result.williams_r)
   445	        result.williams_r_score_short = score_williams_r(result.williams_r, side="short")
   446	        result.willr_trend      = calculate_willr_trend(df)   # [MSL-3]
   447	
   448	        # ── ROC ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   449	        if "ROC_9" in df.columns:
   450	            v = df["ROC_9"].iloc[-1]
   451	            result.roc = float(v) if pd.notna(v) else None
   452	        else:
   453	            result.roc = calculate_roc(df)
   454	
   455	        if "ROC_SLOPE_9_5" in df.columns:
   456	            v = df["ROC_SLOPE_9_5"].iloc[-1]
   457	            result.roc_slope = float(v) if pd.notna(v) else None
   458	        else:
   459	            result.roc_slope = calculate_roc_slope(df)
   460	
   461	        # [MSL-4] ROC slow + crossover — selalu hitung karena tidak ada pre-computed
   462	        result.roc_slow     = calculate_roc_slow(df)
   463	        result.roc_crossover = calculate_roc_crossover(result.roc, result.roc_slow)
   464	        result.roc_score    = score_roc(result.roc, result.roc_slope, result.roc_crossover)
   465	        result.roc_score_short = score_roc(
   466	            result.roc, result.roc_slope, result.roc_crossover, side="short"
   467	        )
   468	
   469	        # ── Composite ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   470	        # [BUG-FIX] Sebelumnya composite SELALU memakai bobot tetap
   471	        # (cci=0.35/williams=0.25/roc=0.40) walau salah satu sub-indikator
   472	        # None (data kurang) -- score_cci(None)/score_williams_r(None)/
   473	        # score_roc(None) semua fallback ke 50.0 (netral), dan nilai fallback
   474	        # itu tetap DIHITUNG BERBOBOT PENUH seolah sinyal nyata, alih-alih
   475	        # dikecualikan & bobot dinormalisasi ulang di antara yang tersedia
   476	        # saja (pola yang SUDAH BENAR dipakai score_trend & score_momentum).
   477	        # Dibuktikan lewat eksperimen: 15 bar data (CCI butuh >=20 -> None,
   478	        # Williams & ROC valid) -> composite lama=51.28, seharusnya=51.96
   479	        # (kalau CCI dikecualikan). Selisih membesar kalau skor yang valid
   480	        # makin ekstrem/menjauh dari 50. Fix: exclude None + renormalize.
   481	        available_w   = {}
   482	        available_val = {}
   483	        if result.cci is not None:
   484	            available_w["cci"] = w["cci"]; available_val["cci"] = result.cci_score
   485	        if result.williams_r is not None:
   486	            available_w["williams"] = w["williams"]; available_val["williams"] = result.williams_r_score
   487	        if result.roc is not None:
   488	            available_w["roc"] = w["roc"]; available_val["roc"] = result.roc_score
   489	
   490	        total_w = sum(available_w.values())
   491	        if total_w <= 0:
   492	            result.composite_score = 50.0
   493	            result.composite_score_short = 50.0
   494	        else:
   495	            result.composite_score = clamp_score(
   496	                sum(available_val[k] * available_w[k] for k in available_w) / total_w
   497	            )
   498	            # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.5, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
   499	            # composite_score_short: reuse available_w (ok-flags/bobot) yang
   500	            # SAMA persis dgn long -- ketersediaan data (cci/williams_r/roc
   501	            # is not None) tidak bergantung arah. cci_score_short/
   502	            # williams_r_score_short/roc_score_short SUDAH dihitung inline di
   503	            # atas sejak Batch 4 (bukan lewat sub-object copy spt momentum/
   504	            # strength, jadi tidak ada risiko bug copy-omission di sini).
   505	            available_val_short = {}
   506	            if "cci" in available_w:
   507	                available_val_short["cci"] = result.cci_score_short
   508	            if "williams" in available_w:
   509	                available_val_short["williams"] = result.williams_r_score_short
   510	            if "roc" in available_w:
   511	                available_val_short["roc"] = result.roc_score_short
   512	            result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(
   513	                sum(available_val_short[k] * available_w[k] for k in available_w) / total_w
   514	            )
   515	
   516	    except Exception as exc:
   517	        if errors is not None:
   518	            errors.append(f"oscillators: {exc}")
   519	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi oscillators: %s", exc)
   520	
   521	    return result

──────────────────────────────────────────
 FILE: engine/indicators/patterns.py
──────────────────────────────────────────
     1	"""
     2	indicators/patterns.py
     3	AlgoTrader Pro v7.0 — "The Intelligence Pipeline"
     4	
     5	CHANGELOG v2 (audit kualitas internal + field utilization):
     6	  [BUG-FIX] _is_volume_confirmed(): sebelumnya cek df[vol_col].iloc[-1] —
     7	           candle LIVE/belum closed. Semua fungsi detect_* di file ini
     8	           (engulfing, hammer, doji, marubozu) pakai iloc[-2] sebagai candle
     9	           pattern (konsisten dgn main.py: confirmed_ts = bars[-2][0]).
    10	           Dibuktikan dgn skenario: candle -2 volume 2.8x MA (harusnya
    11	           confirmed) tapi candle -1 baru 0.14x MA (live, wajar kecil) —
    12	           hasil lama False, seharusnya True. Diganti ke iloc[-2].
    13	  [CLEANUP] Hapus parameter require_volume_confirmation dari
    14	           _detect_engulfing_raw()/detect_engulfing() — diterima tapi tidak
    15	           pernah dipakai di body manapun, tidak ada caller yang pass False.
    16	  [UPGRADE] intelligence/validator.py: primary_pattern (field paling
    17	           informatif, sebelumnya 100% idle di luar file ini) dan
    18	           distance_to_support (asimetris dgn distance_to_resistance yg
    19	           sudah aktif) sekarang diaktifkan lewat _check_pattern_type_context()
    20	           dan _check_support_resistance_context().
    21	"""
    22	
    23	from __future__ import annotations
    24	
    25	import logging
    26	from typing import List, Optional, Tuple
    27	
    28	import numpy as np
    29	import pandas as pd
    30	
    31	from engine.constants import (
    32	    ENGULFING_MIN_BODY_RATIO,
    33	    ENGULFING_COVERAGE_RATIO,
    34	    HAMMER_LOWER_SHADOW_MULT,
    35	    HAMMER_UPPER_SHADOW_MAX_MULT,
    36	    HAMMER_MIN_BODY_PCT,
    37	    DOJI_MAX_BODY_PCT,
    38	    DOJI_BALANCED_SHADOW_RATIO,
    39	    MARUBOZU_MIN_BODY_PCT,
    40	    PATTERN_NEAR_SUPPORT_PCT,
    41	    PATTERN_NEAR_RESISTANCE_PCT,
    42	    PATTERN_VOLUME_CONFIRM_RATIO,
    43	    PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_ENGULFING,
    44	    PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_HAMMER,
    45	    PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_DOJI,
    46	    PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_MARUBOZU,
    47	    PATTERN_VOLUME_CONFIRM_BONUS,
    48	    PATTERN_CONTEXT_SUPPORT_BONUS,
    49	    PATTERN_HIGHER_TF_ALIGN_BONUS,
    50	    PATTERN_NO_CONFIRM_PENALTY,
    51	    SCORE_NEUTRAL,
    52	)
    53	from engine.core.models import PatternIndicators, PatternType, PatternContext, clamp_score
    54	
    55	log = logging.getLogger("indicators.patterns")
    56	_VOLUME_MA_WINDOW = 20
    57	_SWING_LOOKBACK = 20
    58	_DOJI_BODY_THRESHOLD = DOJI_MAX_BODY_PCT
    59	
    60	def _candle_components(
    61	    o: float, h: float, l: float, c: float
    62	) -> Tuple[float, float, float, float, bool]:
    63	    total_range  = h - l
    64	    if total_range < 1e-10:
    65	        return 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, True
    66	
    67	    body_size    = abs(c - o)
    68	    upper_shadow = h - max(o, c)
    69	    lower_shadow = min(o, c) - l
    70	    is_bullish   = c >= o
    71	
    72	    return total_range, body_size, upper_shadow, lower_shadow, is_bullish
    73	
    74	def _body_pct(total_range: float, body_size: float) -> float:
    75	    if total_range < 1e-10:
    76	        return 0.0
    77	    return body_size / total_range
    78	
    79	def _get_volume_ma(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[float]:
    80	    vol_col = "quote_volume" if "quote_volume" in df.columns else "volume"
    81	    if vol_col not in df.columns:
    82	        return None
    83	
    84	    volume = df[vol_col]
    85	    if len(volume) < _VOLUME_MA_WINDOW + 1:
    86	        lookback = volume.iloc[:-1]
    87	    else:
    88	        lookback = volume.iloc[-_VOLUME_MA_WINDOW-1:-1]
    89	
    90	    if lookback.empty or lookback.sum() < 1e-9:
    91	        return None
    92	
    93	    return float(lookback.mean())
    94	
    95	def _is_volume_confirmed(df: pd.DataFrame) -> bool:
    96	    """
    97	    [BUG-FIX v2] Sebelumnya cek df[vol_col].iloc[-1] — itu candle LIVE/belum
    98	    closed (main.py pakai konvensi confirmed_ts = bars[-2][0], dan SEMUA
    99	    fungsi detect_* di file ini — engulfing, hammer, doji, marubozu — pakai
   100	    iloc[-2] sebagai candle pattern). Cek volume harus di candle YANG SAMA
   101	    dengan candle tempat pattern terdeteksi (-2), bukan candle selanjutnya
   102	    yang masih berjalan. Sebelumnya pattern dgn volume tinggi di candle -2
   103	    bisa salah dapat PATTERN_NO_CONFIRM_PENALTY karena candle -1 (baru
   104	    sebagian waktu berlalu) volumenya wajar kecil.
   105	    """
   106	    vol_col = "quote_volume" if "quote_volume" in df.columns else "volume"
   107	    if vol_col not in df.columns:
   108	        return False
   109	
   110	    current_vol = float(df[vol_col].iloc[-2])
   111	    vol_ma      = _get_volume_ma(df)
   112	
   113	    if vol_ma is None or vol_ma < 1e-9:
   114	        return False
   115	
   116	    return current_vol >= vol_ma * PATTERN_VOLUME_CONFIRM_RATIO
   117	
   118	def get_pattern_context(
   119	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   120	    bb_position: Optional[float] = None,
   121	    bb_lower: Optional[float] = None,
   122	    bb_upper: Optional[float] = None,
   123	    ema_values: Optional[dict] = None,
   124	) -> PatternContext:
   125	    if len(df) < 2:
   126	        return PatternContext.UNKNOWN
   127	
   128	    if bb_position is not None:
   129	        try:
   130	            pos = float(bb_position)
   131	            if pos <= 0.10:
   132	                return PatternContext.NEAR_SUPPORT
   133	            if pos >= 0.90:
   134	                return PatternContext.NEAR_RESISTANCE
   135	            return PatternContext.MID_RANGE
   136	        except Exception:
   137	            pass
   138	
   139	    close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   140	    if close <= 0:
   141	        return PatternContext.UNKNOWN
   142	
   143	    low_arr  = df["low"].values
   144	    high_arr = df["high"].values
   145	    support_levels: List[float] = []
   146	
   147	    if bb_lower is not None and bb_lower > 0:
   148	        support_levels.append(bb_lower)
   149	
   150	    if ema_values and ema_values.get("ema50"):
   151	        ema50 = float(ema_values["ema50"])
   152	        if ema50 > 0 and ema50 < close:
   153	            support_levels.append(ema50)
   154	
   155	    lookback_lows  = low_arr[-_SWING_LOOKBACK-1:-1]
   156	    if len(lookback_lows) > 0:
   157	        swing_low = float(np.min(lookback_lows))
   158	        if swing_low > 0:
   159	            support_levels.append(swing_low)
   160	
   161	    resistance_levels: List[float] = []
   162	
   163	    if bb_upper is not None and bb_upper > 0:
   164	        resistance_levels.append(bb_upper)
   165	
   166	    lookback_highs = high_arr[-_SWING_LOOKBACK-1:-1]
   167	    if len(lookback_highs) > 0:
   168	        swing_high = float(np.max(lookback_highs))
   169	        if swing_high > 0 and swing_high > close:
   170	            resistance_levels.append(swing_high)
   171	
   172	    support_threshold    = close * PATTERN_NEAR_SUPPORT_PCT
   173	    resistance_threshold = close * PATTERN_NEAR_RESISTANCE_PCT
   174	
   175	    for level in support_levels:
   176	        if abs(close - level) <= support_threshold:
   177	            log.debug("pattern context: NEAR_SUPPORT (close=%.5f level=%.5f)", close, level)
   178	            return PatternContext.NEAR_SUPPORT
   179	
   180	    for level in resistance_levels:
   181	        if abs(close - level) <= resistance_threshold:
   182	            log.debug("pattern context: NEAR_RESISTANCE (close=%.5f level=%.5f)", close, level)
   183	            return PatternContext.NEAR_RESISTANCE
   184	
   185	    return PatternContext.MID_RANGE
   186	
   187	def _detect_engulfing_raw(
   188	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   189	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   190	) -> Tuple[PatternType, float]:
   191	    # [CLEANUP v2] Parameter require_volume_confirmation dihapus — sebelumnya
   192	    # diterima tapi tidak pernah dipakai di body fungsi ini (volume confirmation
   193	    # yang sesungguhnya sudah ditangani terpisah lewat _is_volume_confirmed()
   194	    # yang dipanggil score_pattern(), bukan di sini), dan tidak ada caller yang
   195	    # pernah pass False — parameter ini 100% kosmetik/dead.
   196	    if errors is None:
   197	        errors = []
   198	
   199	    if len(df) < 3:
   200	        errors.append("engulfing: butuh minimal 3 bar (2 konfirmasi + 1 buffer)")
   201	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   202	
   203	    bar_curr = df.iloc[-2]
   204	    bar_prev = df.iloc[-3]
   205	
   206	    o_curr = float(bar_curr["open"])
   207	    h_curr = float(bar_curr["high"])
   208	    l_curr = float(bar_curr["low"])
   209	    c_curr = float(bar_curr["close"])
   210	
   211	    o_prev = float(bar_prev["open"])
   212	    h_prev = float(bar_prev["high"])
   213	    l_prev = float(bar_prev["low"])
   214	    c_prev = float(bar_prev["close"])
   215	
   216	    range_curr, body_curr, upper_curr, lower_curr, is_bull_curr = _candle_components(
   217	        o_curr, h_curr, l_curr, c_curr
   218	    )
   219	    range_prev, body_prev, _, _, is_bull_prev = _candle_components(
   220	        o_prev, h_prev, l_prev, c_prev
   221	    )
   222	
   223	    if range_curr < 1e-10 or range_prev < 1e-10:
   224	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   225	
   226	    body_pct_curr = _body_pct(range_curr, body_curr)
   227	
   228	    if body_pct_curr < ENGULFING_MIN_BODY_RATIO:
   229	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   230	
   231	    if not is_bull_prev and is_bull_curr:
   232	        if (o_curr <= c_prev and
   233	                c_curr >= o_prev and
   234	                body_curr >= body_prev * ENGULFING_COVERAGE_RATIO):
   235	
   236	            quality = min(1.0, body_curr / (range_prev + 1e-10))
   237	
   238	            log.debug(
   239	                "BULLISH_ENGULFING detected: quality=%.3f vol_ok=%s",
   240	                quality, _is_volume_confirmed(df),
   241	            )
   242	            return PatternType.BULLISH_ENGULFING, quality
   243	
   244	    if is_bull_prev and not is_bull_curr:
   245	        if (o_curr >= c_prev and
   246	                c_curr <= o_prev and
   247	                body_curr >= body_prev * ENGULFING_COVERAGE_RATIO):
   248	
   249	            quality = min(1.0, body_curr / (range_prev + 1e-10))
   250	
   251	            log.debug(
   252	                "BEARISH_ENGULFING detected: quality=%.3f",
   253	                quality,
   254	            )
   255	            return PatternType.BEARISH_ENGULFING, quality
   256	
   257	    return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   258	
   259	def detect_engulfing(
   260	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   261	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   262	) -> PatternIndicators:
   263	    p, q = _detect_engulfing_raw(
   264	        df,
   265	        errors=errors,
   266	    )
   267	    out = PatternIndicators()
   268	    out.primary_pattern = p
   269	    out.pattern_score = _score_single_pattern(
   270	        pattern_type=p,
   271	        quality=q,
   272	        context=PatternContext.UNKNOWN,
   273	        volume_confirmed=_is_volume_confirmed(df),
   274	        higher_tf_aligned=None,
   275	    )
   276	    out.composite_score = out.pattern_score
   277	    return out
   278	
   279	def _detect_hammer_shooting_star_raw(
   280	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   281	    context: PatternContext = PatternContext.UNKNOWN,
   282	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   283	) -> Tuple[PatternType, float]:
   284	    if errors is None:
   285	        errors = []
   286	
   287	    if len(df) < 2:
   288	        errors.append("hammer: butuh minimal 2 bar")
   289	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   290	
   291	    bar = df.iloc[-2]
   292	    o   = float(bar["open"])
   293	    h   = float(bar["high"])
   294	    l   = float(bar["low"])
   295	    c   = float(bar["close"])
   296	
   297	    total_range, body_size, upper_shadow, lower_shadow, is_bullish = \
   298	        _candle_components(o, h, l, c)
   299	
   300	    if total_range < 1e-10:
   301	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   302	
   303	    body_pct = _body_pct(total_range, body_size)
   304	
   305	    if body_pct < HAMMER_MIN_BODY_PCT:
   306	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   307	
   308	    if body_pct > 0.50:
   309	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   310	
   311	    if body_size < 1e-10:
   312	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   313	
   314	    is_hammer = (
   315	        lower_shadow >= HAMMER_LOWER_SHADOW_MULT * body_size and
   316	        upper_shadow <= HAMMER_UPPER_SHADOW_MAX_MULT * body_size
   317	    )
   318	
   319	    is_shooting_star = (
   320	        upper_shadow >= HAMMER_LOWER_SHADOW_MULT * body_size and
   321	        lower_shadow <= HAMMER_UPPER_SHADOW_MAX_MULT * body_size
   322	    )
   323	
   324	    if not is_hammer and not is_shooting_star:
   325	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   326	
   327	    if is_hammer:
   328	        if context not in (PatternContext.NEAR_SUPPORT,):
   329	            log.debug("hammer detected tapi context bukan support (%s) — return NONE", context)
   330	            return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   331	
   332	        quality = min(1.0, lower_shadow / (body_size * 4 + 1e-10))
   333	
   334	        log.debug("HAMMER detected: quality=%.3f context=%s", quality, context)
   335	        return PatternType.HAMMER, quality
   336	
   337	    if is_shooting_star:
   338	        if context not in (PatternContext.NEAR_RESISTANCE,):
   339	            log.debug(
   340	                "shooting_star detected tapi context bukan resistance (%s) — return NONE",
   341	                context,
   342	            )
   343	            return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   344	
   345	        quality = min(1.0, upper_shadow / (body_size * 4 + 1e-10))
   346	        log.debug("SHOOTING_STAR detected: quality=%.3f context=%s", quality, context)
   347	        return PatternType.SHOOTING_STAR, quality
   348	
   349	    return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   350	
   351	def detect_hammer_shooting_star(
   352	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   353	    context: PatternContext = PatternContext.UNKNOWN,
   354	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   355	) -> PatternIndicators:
   356	    p, q = _detect_hammer_shooting_star_raw(df, context=context, errors=errors)
   357	    out = PatternIndicators()
   358	    out.primary_pattern = p
   359	    out.pattern_context = context
   360	    out.pattern_score = _score_single_pattern(
   361	        pattern_type=p,
   362	        quality=q,
   363	        context=context,
   364	        volume_confirmed=_is_volume_confirmed(df),
   365	        higher_tf_aligned=None,
   366	    )
   367	    out.composite_score = out.pattern_score
   368	    return out
   369	
   370	def _detect_doji_raw(
   371	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   372	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   373	) -> Tuple[PatternType, float]:
   374	    if errors is None:
   375	        errors = []
   376	
   377	    if len(df) < 2:
   378	        errors.append("doji: butuh minimal 2 bar")
   379	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   380	
   381	    bar = df.iloc[-2]
   382	    o   = float(bar["open"])
   383	    h   = float(bar["high"])
   384	    l   = float(bar["low"])
   385	    c   = float(bar["close"])
   386	
   387	    total_range, body_size, upper_shadow, lower_shadow, _ = _candle_components(
   388	        o, h, l, c
   389	    )
   390	
   391	    if total_range < 1e-10:
   392	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   393	
   394	    body_pct = _body_pct(total_range, body_size)
   395	
   396	    if body_pct > DOJI_MAX_BODY_PCT:
   397	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   398	
   399	    body_quality = max(0.0, 1.0 - (body_pct / DOJI_MAX_BODY_PCT))
   400	
   401	    if (
   402	        (lower_shadow > 0 and upper_shadow < 1e-10)
   403	        or (
   404	            (upper_shadow > 0 and lower_shadow / upper_shadow >= 3.0)
   405	            and lower_shadow / total_range >= 0.65
   406	        )
   407	    ):
   408	        quality = body_quality * 0.6 + min(1.0, lower_shadow / total_range) * 0.4
   409	        log.debug("DRAGONFLY_DOJI detected: quality=%.3f", quality)
   410	        return PatternType.DRAGONFLY_DOJI, quality
   411	
   412	    if (
   413	        (upper_shadow > 0 and lower_shadow < 1e-10)
   414	        or (
   415	            (lower_shadow > 0 and upper_shadow / lower_shadow >= 3.0)
   416	            and upper_shadow / total_range >= 0.65
   417	        )
   418	    ):
   419	        quality = body_quality * 0.6 + min(1.0, upper_shadow / total_range) * 0.4
   420	        log.debug("GRAVESTONE_DOJI detected: quality=%.3f", quality)
   421	        return PatternType.GRAVESTONE_DOJI, quality
   422	
   423	    if upper_shadow > 0 and lower_shadow > 0:
   424	        shadow_ratio = max(upper_shadow, lower_shadow) / min(upper_shadow, lower_shadow)
   425	        if shadow_ratio <= DOJI_BALANCED_SHADOW_RATIO:
   426	            log.debug("STANDARD_DOJI detected: quality=%.3f", body_quality)
   427	            return PatternType.STANDARD_DOJI, body_quality
   428	
   429	    log.debug("SPINNING_TOP detected (kuasi-doji)")
   430	    return PatternType.SPINNING_TOP, body_quality * 0.6
   431	
   432	def detect_doji(
   433	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   434	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   435	) -> PatternIndicators:
   436	    p, q = _detect_doji_raw(df, errors=errors)
   437	    out = PatternIndicators()
   438	    out.primary_pattern = p
   439	    out.pattern_score = _score_single_pattern(
   440	        pattern_type=p,
   441	        quality=q,
   442	        context=PatternContext.UNKNOWN,
   443	        volume_confirmed=_is_volume_confirmed(df),
   444	        higher_tf_aligned=None,
   445	    )
   446	    out.composite_score = out.pattern_score
   447	    return out
   448	
   449	def detect_all(
   450	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   451	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   452	    context: PatternContext = PatternContext.UNKNOWN,
   453	    higher_tf_aligned: Optional[bool] = None,
   454	    bb_lower: Optional[float] = None,
   455	    bb_upper: Optional[float] = None,
   456	    ema_values: Optional[dict] = None,
   457	) -> PatternIndicators:
   458	    return score_pattern(
   459	        df=df,
   460	        context=context,
   461	        higher_tf_aligned=higher_tf_aligned,
   462	        bb_lower=bb_lower,
   463	        bb_upper=bb_upper,
   464	        ema_values=ema_values,
   465	        errors=errors,
   466	    )
   467	
   468	def detect_marubozu(
   469	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   470	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   471	) -> Tuple[PatternType, float]:
   472	    if errors is None:
   473	        errors = []
   474	
   475	    if len(df) < 2:
   476	        errors.append("marubozu: butuh minimal 2 bar")
   477	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   478	
   479	    bar = df.iloc[-2]
   480	    o   = float(bar["open"])
   481	    h   = float(bar["high"])
   482	    l   = float(bar["low"])
   483	    c   = float(bar["close"])
   484	
   485	    total_range, body_size, _, _, is_bullish = _candle_components(o, h, l, c)
   486	
   487	    if total_range < 1e-10:
   488	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   489	
   490	    body_pct = _body_pct(total_range, body_size)
   491	
   492	    if body_pct < MARUBOZU_MIN_BODY_PCT:
   493	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   494	
   495	    quality = min(1.0, (body_pct - MARUBOZU_MIN_BODY_PCT) / (1.0 - MARUBOZU_MIN_BODY_PCT) + 0.5)
   496	
   497	    if is_bullish:
   498	        log.debug("BULLISH_MARUBOZU detected: quality=%.3f", quality)
   499	        return PatternType.BULLISH_MARUBOZU, quality
   500	    else:
   501	        log.debug("BEARISH_MARUBOZU detected: quality=%.3f", quality)
   502	        return PatternType.BEARISH_MARUBOZU, quality
   503	
   504	def detect_volume_climax(
   505	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   506	    climax_ratio: float = 5.0,
   507	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   508	) -> Tuple[PatternType, float]:
   509	    if errors is None:
   510	        errors = []
   511	
   512	    vol_col = "quote_volume" if "quote_volume" in df.columns else "volume"
   513	    if vol_col not in df.columns:
   514	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   515	
   516	    if len(df) < _VOLUME_MA_WINDOW + 2:
   517	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   518	
   519	    volume  = df[vol_col]
   520	    vol_ma  = _get_volume_ma(df)
   521	
   522	    if vol_ma is None or vol_ma < 1e-9:
   523	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   524	
   525	    current_vol = float(volume.iloc[-2])
   526	    ratio       = current_vol / vol_ma
   527	
   528	    if ratio < climax_ratio:
   529	        return PatternType.NONE, 0.0
   530	
   531	    quality = min(1.0, (ratio - climax_ratio) / climax_ratio)
   532	    quality = max(0.3, quality)
   533	
   534	    log.debug("VOLUME_CLIMAX detected: ratio=%.1fx quality=%.3f", ratio, quality)
   535	    return PatternType.VOLUME_CLIMAX, quality
   536	
   537	def _score_single_pattern(
   538	    pattern_type: PatternType,
   539	    quality: float,
   540	    context: PatternContext,
   541	    volume_confirmed: bool,
   542	    higher_tf_aligned: Optional[bool],
   543	) -> float:
   544	    if pattern_type == PatternType.NONE:
   545	        return SCORE_NEUTRAL
   546	
   547	    if pattern_type == PatternType.VOLUME_CLIMAX:
   548	        climax_penalty = 15.0 + quality * 10.0
   549	        return clamp_score(SCORE_NEUTRAL - climax_penalty)
   550	
   551	    _BASE_SCORES = {
   552	        PatternType.BULLISH_ENGULFING: PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_ENGULFING,
   553	        PatternType.HAMMER:            PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_HAMMER,
   554	        PatternType.DRAGONFLY_DOJI:    PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_DOJI + 5.0,
   555	        PatternType.MORNING_STAR:      PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_ENGULFING + 5.0,
   556	        PatternType.BULLISH_MARUBOZU:  PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_MARUBOZU,
   557	        PatternType.BEARISH_ENGULFING: -(PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_ENGULFING - 50.0),
   558	        PatternType.SHOOTING_STAR:     -(PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_HAMMER - 50.0),
   559	        PatternType.GRAVESTONE_DOJI:   -(PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_DOJI + 5.0 - 50.0),
   560	        PatternType.EVENING_STAR:      -(PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_ENGULFING + 5.0 - 50.0),
   561	        PatternType.BEARISH_MARUBOZU:  -(PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_MARUBOZU - 50.0),
   562	        PatternType.STANDARD_DOJI:     PATTERN_BASE_SCORE_DOJI,
   563	        PatternType.SPINNING_TOP:      SCORE_NEUTRAL - 3.0,
   564	        PatternType.BB_KC_SQUEEZE:     65.0,
   565	    }
   566	
   567	    base = _BASE_SCORES.get(pattern_type, SCORE_NEUTRAL)
   568	
   569	    is_bearish_penalty = pattern_type in (
   570	        PatternType.BEARISH_ENGULFING,
   571	        PatternType.SHOOTING_STAR,
   572	        PatternType.GRAVESTONE_DOJI,
   573	        PatternType.EVENING_STAR,
   574	        PatternType.BEARISH_MARUBOZU,
   575	    )
   576	
   577	    if is_bearish_penalty:
   578	        raw_penalty = abs(base)
   579	        adjusted    = SCORE_NEUTRAL - raw_penalty * quality
   580	    else:
   581	        excess    = base - SCORE_NEUTRAL
   582	        adjusted  = SCORE_NEUTRAL + excess * quality
   583	
   584	    score = adjusted
   585	
   586	    # [BUG-FIX -- ditemukan lewat audit menyeluruh, didiskusikan & disetujui
   587	    # user] Sebelumnya SEMUA penyesuaian di bawah ini (volume_confirmed,
   588	    # context, higher_tf_aligned=True) di-gate `if not is_bearish_penalty`,
   589	    # artinya pattern BEARISH tidak pernah mendapat penyesuaian volume/
   590	    # context sama sekali (skor bearish engulfing selalu identik terlepas
   591	    # dari volume tinggi/rendah atau posisi context) -- kehilangan sinyal
   592	    # yang berarti, padahal bullish mendapat penyesuaian penuh (dibuktikan:
   593	    # volume_confirmed mengubah skor bullish 35 poin, bearish 0 poin).
   594	    # LEBIH PARAH: `elif higher_tf_aligned is False: score -= 8.0` berlaku
   595	    # ke KEDUA arah tanpa disadari arahnya salah untuk bearish -- karena
   596	    # skor bearish sudah di bawah 50, -8 mendorongnya MAKIN JAUH dari 50
   597	    # (makin ekstrem), padahal "tidak align dengan HTF" seharusnya berarti
   598	    # SEMAKIN TIDAK RELIABLE (mendorong ke arah netral 50), bukan sebaliknya.
   599	    # Fix root-cause: simetriskan explicit per arah. Konfirmasi (volume
   600	    # tinggi / context selaras arah / HTF align) mendorong skor MENJAUH
   601	    # dari 50 sesuai arah pattern (bullish naik, bearish turun). Tidak-
   602	    # konfirmasi mendorong skor MENDEKATI 50 (kurang reliable) untuk KEDUA
   603	    # arah. Context "selaras" utk bearish adalah NEAR_RESISTANCE (resistance
   604	    # tertahan menguatkan reversal turun) -- mirror dari NEAR_SUPPORT utk
   605	    # bullish; NEAR_SUPPORT justru melemahkan bearish (support berpotensi
   606	    # bertahan) -- mirror dari NEAR_RESISTANCE utk bullish.
   607	    if is_bearish_penalty:
   608	        if volume_confirmed:
   609	            score -= PATTERN_VOLUME_CONFIRM_BONUS
   610	        else:
   611	            score -= PATTERN_NO_CONFIRM_PENALTY   # PATTERN_NO_CONFIRM_PENALTY sudah negatif -> score += 20 (menuju netral)
   612	
   613	        if context == PatternContext.NEAR_RESISTANCE:
   614	            score -= PATTERN_CONTEXT_SUPPORT_BONUS
   615	        elif context == PatternContext.NEAR_SUPPORT:
   616	            score += 10.0
   617	
   618	        if higher_tf_aligned is True:
   619	            score -= PATTERN_HIGHER_TF_ALIGN_BONUS
   620	        elif higher_tf_aligned is False:
   621	            score += 8.0
   622	    else:
   623	        if volume_confirmed:
   624	            score += PATTERN_VOLUME_CONFIRM_BONUS
   625	        else:
   626	            score += PATTERN_NO_CONFIRM_PENALTY
   627	
   628	        if context == PatternContext.NEAR_SUPPORT:
   629	            score += PATTERN_CONTEXT_SUPPORT_BONUS
   630	        elif context == PatternContext.NEAR_RESISTANCE:
   631	            score -= 10.0
   632	
   633	        if higher_tf_aligned is True:
   634	            score += PATTERN_HIGHER_TF_ALIGN_BONUS
   635	        elif higher_tf_aligned is False:
   636	            score -= 8.0
   637	
   638	    return clamp_score(score)
   639	
   640	def score_pattern(
   641	    df: pd.DataFrame,
   642	    context: PatternContext = PatternContext.UNKNOWN,
   643	    higher_tf_aligned: Optional[bool] = None,
   644	    bb_lower: Optional[float] = None,
   645	    bb_upper: Optional[float] = None,
   646	    ema_values: Optional[dict] = None,
   647	    errors: Optional[List[str]] = None,
   648	) -> PatternIndicators:
   649	    if errors is None:
   650	        errors = []
   651	
   652	    result = PatternIndicators()
   653	
   654	    if context == PatternContext.UNKNOWN and len(df) >= 3:
   655	        context = get_pattern_context(
   656	            df,
   657	            bb_lower=bb_lower,
   658	            bb_upper=bb_upper,
   659	            ema_values=ema_values,
   660	        )
   661	
   662	    result.pattern_context    = context
   663	    result.higher_tf_aligned  = higher_tf_aligned
   664	
   665	    if len(df) < 3:
   666	        errors.append("score_pattern: butuh minimal 3 bar untuk deteksi pattern")
   667	        result.pattern_score       = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   668	        result.pattern_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   669	        result.context_score       = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   670	        result.context_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   671	        result.composite_score     = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   672	        result.composite_score_short = SCORE_NEUTRAL
   673	        return result
   674	
   675	    vol_confirmed = _is_volume_confirmed(df)
   676	    result.pattern_volume_confirmed = vol_confirmed
   677	
   678	    bar = df.iloc[-2]
   679	    o, h, l, c = float(bar["open"]), float(bar["high"]), float(bar["low"]), float(bar["close"])
   680	    total_range, body_size, _, _, _ = _candle_components(o, h, l, c)
   681	    result.pattern_body_pct = _body_pct(total_range, body_size)
   682	
   683	    close = float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
   684	    if bb_lower is not None and bb_lower > 0 and close > 0:
   685	        result.distance_to_support = abs(close - bb_lower) / close * 100.0
   686	    if bb_upper is not None and bb_upper > 0 and close > 0:
   687	        result.distance_to_resistance = abs(close - bb_upper) / close * 100.0
   688	
   689	    primary_pattern   = PatternType.NONE
   690	    primary_quality   = 0.0
   691	    secondary_pattern = PatternType.NONE
   692	
   693	    climax_pattern, climax_quality = detect_volume_climax(df, errors=errors)
   694	    if climax_pattern == PatternType.VOLUME_CLIMAX:
   695	        secondary_pattern = climax_pattern
   696	        log.debug("Volume climax terdeteksi, lanjut cari candlestick pattern")
   697	
   698	    if primary_pattern == PatternType.NONE:
   699	        eng_type, eng_quality = _detect_engulfing_raw(df, errors=errors)
   700	        if eng_type != PatternType.NONE:
   701	            primary_pattern = eng_type
   702	            primary_quality = eng_quality
   703	
   704	    if primary_pattern == PatternType.NONE:
   705	        hs_type, hs_quality = _detect_hammer_shooting_star_raw(
   706	            df, context=context, errors=errors
   707	        )
   708	        if hs_type != PatternType.NONE:
   709	            primary_pattern = hs_type
   710	            primary_quality = hs_quality
   711	
   712	    if primary_pattern == PatternType.NONE:
   713	        mrz_type, mrz_quality = detect_marubozu(df, errors=errors)
   714	        if mrz_type != PatternType.NONE:
   715	            primary_pattern = mrz_type
   716	            primary_quality = mrz_quality
   717	
   718	    if primary_pattern == PatternType.NONE:
   719	        doji_type, doji_quality = _detect_doji_raw(df, errors=errors)
   720	        if doji_type != PatternType.NONE:
   721	            primary_pattern = doji_type
   722	            primary_quality = doji_quality
   723	
   724	    if secondary_pattern == PatternType.VOLUME_CLIMAX and primary_pattern == PatternType.NONE:
   725	        primary_pattern = climax_pattern
   726	        primary_quality = climax_quality
   727	        secondary_pattern = PatternType.NONE
   728	
   729	    result.primary_pattern   = primary_pattern
   730	    result.secondary_pattern = secondary_pattern
   731	
   732	    pattern_score = _score_single_pattern(
   733	        pattern_type      = primary_pattern,
   734	        quality           = primary_quality,
   735	        context           = context,
   736	        volume_confirmed  = vol_confirmed,
   737	        higher_tf_aligned = higher_tf_aligned,
   738	    )
   739	
   740	    if secondary_pattern == PatternType.VOLUME_CLIMAX:
   741	        climax_penalty = 12.0 * climax_quality
   742	        pattern_score  = clamp_score(pattern_score - climax_penalty)
   743	        log.debug(
   744	            "Climax penalty diterapkan pada bullish pattern: -%.1f",
   745	            climax_penalty,
   746	        )
   747	
   748	    result.pattern_score = pattern_score
   749	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 1, Class B] _score_single_pattern() SUDAH mirror-
   750	    # symmetric (bearish pattern = 50-magnitude, bullish = 50+magnitude
   751	    # dgn magnitude yang SAMA persis, dikonfirmasi dari konstruksi
   752	    # _BASE_SCORES: tiap entry bearish = -(entry_bullish_pasangannya - 50)).
   753	    # Karena itu 100-x adalah mirror yang PERSIS BENAR di sini -- bukan
   754	    # sekadar pendekatan -- beda dgn kategori lain (trend/oscillator/dst)
   755	    # yang butuh reformulasi cabang, bukan komplemen sederhana.
   756	    result.pattern_score_short = clamp_score(100.0 - pattern_score)
   757	
   758	    context_score_map = {
   759	        PatternContext.NEAR_SUPPORT:    70.0,
   760	        PatternContext.NEAR_RESISTANCE: 32.0,
   761	        PatternContext.MID_RANGE:       52.0,
   762	        PatternContext.UNKNOWN:         SCORE_NEUTRAL,
   763	    }
   764	    context_score = context_score_map.get(context, SCORE_NEUTRAL)
   765	    result.context_score = context_score
   766	    # [MTF-BIAS-FIX -- Sub-Batch A.4, proyek MTF composite side-aware]
   767	    # context_score TIDAK PERNAH dapat treatment side-aware di Batch 1 (yg
   768	    # cuma cakup pattern_score) -- padahal genuinely directional: NEAR_SUPPORT
   769	    # (dekat support = ekspektasi bounce naik) bagus utk long, NEAR_RESISTANCE
   770	    # (dekat resistance = ekspektasi rejection turun) bagus utk short. Pola
   771	    # input-reflection (100-x) sama persis dgn pattern_score_short di atas --
   772	    # NEAR_SUPPORT 70->30, NEAR_RESISTANCE 32->68, MID_RANGE 52->48,
   773	    # UNKNOWN 50->50 (netral tetap netral).
   774	    result.context_score_short = clamp_score(100.0 - context_score)
   775	
   776	    if primary_pattern == PatternType.NONE:
   777	        result.composite_score = clamp_score(
   778	            SCORE_NEUTRAL * 0.7 + context_score * 0.3
   779	        )
   780	        result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(
   781	            SCORE_NEUTRAL * 0.7 + result.context_score_short * 0.3
   782	        )
   783	    else:
   784	        result.composite_score = clamp_score(
   785	            pattern_score * 0.70 + context_score * 0.30
   786	        )
   787	        result.composite_score_short = clamp_score(
   788	            result.pattern_score_short * 0.70 + result.context_score_short * 0.30
   789	        )
   790	
   791	    log.debug(
   792	        "pattern composite: primary=%s quality=%.3f vol_ok=%s context=%s "
   793	        "→ pattern_score=%.1f context_score=%.1f composite=%.1f",
   794	        primary_pattern.value, primary_quality, vol_confirmed, context.value,
   795	        pattern_score, context_score, result.composite_score,
   796	    )
   797	
   798	    return result

──────────────────────────────────────────
 FILE: engine/indicators/orderbook.py
──────────────────────────────────────────
     1	"""
     2	indicators/orderbook.py

    10	  [MSL-3] _find_cluster_wall() — deteksi cluster wall (beberapa level berdekatan).
    11	  [MSL-5] Price context: wall distance dari mid-price menentukan relevansi wall.

    16	
    17	Changelog v3.1:
    18	  [BUG-FIX] imbalance_score — diskontinuitas 10.2 poin di kedua boundary:
    19	            bull branch (imb>=0.62) mulai dari 65.0, tapi neutral branch berakhir
    20	            di 54.8 → lompatan 10.2 yang tidak wajar. Begitu pula di sisi bear.
    21	            Fix: anchor bull/bear branch ke nilai neutral branch di boundary-nya
    22	            (54.8 dan 45.2) sehingga scoring kontinu di seluruh range [0,1].
    23	            Range baru: 10→45.2→50→54.8→90 (monoton, tidak ada lompatan).
    24	
    25	Changelog v3:
    26	  [BUG-A FIX] Spoofing penalty sebelumnya membandingkan current vs current karena
    27	              state.prev_bid_walls sudah di-overwrite sebelum _spoofing_penalty
    28	              dipanggil → selalu return 1.0, spoof tidak pernah terdeteksi.
    29	              Fix: simpan prev_bid/ask_snapshot SEBELUM state.prev di-update.
    30	  [BUG-B FIX] _walls_to_dict menyimpan semua 20 level termasuk micro-order kecil.
    31	              Micro-order yang menghilang bisa trigger absorbed=True secara salah.
    32	              Fix: tambah filter level >= WHALE_WALL_PCT * total_usdt (whale-only).
    33	  [MSL-A FIX] _state_registry tumbuh selamanya jika coin dirotasi keluar universe.
    34	              Fix: tambah reset_state(symbol) + cleanup_stale_states(ttl_secs=3600).
    35	              _SnapshotState.last_active di-update setiap akses via _get_state().
    36	  [MSL-B FIX] _SnapshotState.wall_first_seen adalah dead field — didefinisikan tapi

    38	              Field dihapus agar tidak menyesatkan.

    40	from __future__ import annotations
    41	
    42	import logging
    43	import statistics
    44	import threading
    45	import time
    46	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    47	from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple

    49	log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
