    51	from engine.core.models import OrderbookIndicators
    52	
    53	# ── Constants ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    54	WHALE_WALL_PCT      = 0.08   # level > 8% total volume sisi = whale wall
    55	IMBALANCE_BULL      = 0.62   # bid ratio > 0.62 = tekanan beli
    56	IMBALANCE_BEAR      = 0.38   # bid ratio < 0.38 = tekanan jual
    57	ABSORPTION_DROP_PCT = 0.40   # wall menyusut >40% dalam 1 tick = diserap
    58	CLUSTER_GAP_PCT     = 0.003  # level dalam 0.3% dari level tertinggi = satu cluster
    59	WALL_CLOSE_PCT      = 0.005  # wall < 0.5% dari mid = sangat relevan
    60	WALL_FAR_PCT        = 0.030  # wall > 3.0% dari mid = kurang relevan
    61	LIQUIDITY_SOFT      = 50_000  # USDT — depth di bawah ini = likuiditas rendah
    62	LIQUIDITY_FULL      = 500_000 # USDT — depth di atas ini = likuiditas penuh
    63	
    64	# Bobot depth per level — identik dengan WhaleDetector sebelumnya di main.py
    65	_DEPTH_WEIGHTS: List[float] = [
    66	    *([1.0] * 5),   # level 1-5  bobot penuh
    67	    *([0.7] * 5),   # level 6-10 bobot sedang
    68	    *([0.4] * 10),  # level 11-20 bobot rendah
    69	]
    70	
    71	
    72	# ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    73	def clamp_score(v: float, lo: float = 0.0, hi: float = 100.0) -> float:
    74	    return max(lo, min(hi, v))
    75	
    76	
    77	def _weighted_volume(levels: list) -> float:
    78	    """Total volume USDT dengan bobot per kedalaman level (BUG-3 fix)."""
    79	    total = 0.0
    80	    for i, (p, q) in enumerate(levels[:20]):
    81	        p, q = float(p), float(q)
    82	        if p <= 0 or q <= 0:
    83	            continue
    84	        w = _DEPTH_WEIGHTS[i] if i < len(_DEPTH_WEIGHTS) else 0.4
    85	        total += p * q * w
    86	    return total
    87	
    88	
    89	def _raw_volume(levels: list) -> float:
    90	    """Total volume USDT tanpa bobot — untuk spread normalisasi & liquidity."""
    91	    return sum(float(p) * float(q) for p, q in levels if float(p) > 0 and float(q) > 0)
    92	
    93	
    94	def _filter_min_size(levels: list) -> list:
    95	    """Buang order < 50% median qty — filter noise & micro-order."""
    96	    if not levels:
    97	        return levels
    98	    qtys = [float(v) for _, v in levels if float(v) > 0]
    99	    if not qtys:
   100	        return levels
   101	    med = statistics.median(qtys)
   102	    return [(p, v) for p, v in levels if float(v) >= med * 0.5]
   103	
   104	
   105	def _find_whale_wall(levels: list, weighted_vol: float) -> Tuple[Optional[float], Optional[float]]:
   106	    """Return (price, strength_pct) dari single level terbesar (weighted)."""
   107	    if weighted_vol <= 0 or not levels:
   108	        return None, None
   109	    best_price, best_strength = None, 0.0
   110	    for i, (p, q) in enumerate(levels[:20]):
   111	        p, q = float(p), float(q)
   112	        if p <= 0 or q <= 0:
   113	            continue
   114	        w = _DEPTH_WEIGHTS[i] if i < len(_DEPTH_WEIGHTS) else 0.4
   115	        strength = (p * q * w) / weighted_vol
   116	        if strength > best_strength:
   117	            best_strength = strength
   118	            best_price    = p
   119	    if best_strength >= WHALE_WALL_PCT:
   120	        return best_price, round(best_strength * 100, 2)
   121	    return None, None
   122	
   123	
   124	def _find_cluster_wall(
   125	    levels: list,
   126	    weighted_vol: float,
   127	) -> Tuple[Optional[float], Optional[float]]:
   128	    """
   129	    Deteksi cluster wall — beberapa level berdekatan (dalam CLUSTER_GAP_PCT)
   130	    yang secara kolektif membentuk resistance/support kuat (MSL-3).
   131	    Return (price_center, cluster_strength_pct).
   132	    """
   133	    if weighted_vol <= 0 or not levels:
   134	        return None, None
   135	
   136	    # Buat list (price, weighted_usdt) untuk 20 level teratas
   137	    pts: List[Tuple[float, float]] = []
   138	    for i, (p, q) in enumerate(levels[:20]):
   139	        p, q = float(p), float(q)
   140	        if p <= 0 or q <= 0:
   141	            continue
   142	        w = _DEPTH_WEIGHTS[i] if i < len(_DEPTH_WEIGHTS) else 0.4
   143	        pts.append((p, p * q * w))
   144	
   145	    if not pts:
   146	        return None, None
   147	
   148	    # Kelompokkan level yang harganya dalam CLUSTER_GAP_PCT satu sama lain
   149	    pts.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
   150	    best_cluster_strength = 0.0
   151	    best_cluster_price    = None
   152	
   153	    i = 0
   154	    while i < len(pts):
   155	        anchor_price  = pts[i][0]
   156	        cluster_usdt  = pts[i][1]
   157	        j = i + 1
   158	        while j < len(pts):
   159	            gap = abs(pts[j][0] - anchor_price) / anchor_price
   160	            if gap <= CLUSTER_GAP_PCT:
   161	                cluster_usdt += pts[j][1]
   162	                j += 1
   163	            else:
   164	                break
   165	        strength = cluster_usdt / weighted_vol
   166	        if strength > best_cluster_strength:
   167	            best_cluster_strength = strength
   168	            best_cluster_price    = anchor_price
   169	        i = j if j > i else i + 1
   170	
   171	    if best_cluster_strength >= WHALE_WALL_PCT:
   172	        return best_cluster_price, round(best_cluster_strength * 100, 2)
   173	    return None, None
   174	
   175	
   176	def _wall_distance_factor(wall_price: Optional[float], mid: float) -> float:
   177	    """
   178	    MSL-5: Factor relevansi wall berdasarkan jarak dari mid-price.
   179	    Wall dekat (< 0.5%) = relevansi 1.0. Wall jauh (> 3%) = relevansi 0.2.
   180	    """
   181	    if wall_price is None or mid <= 0:
   182	        return 0.5
   183	    dist = abs(wall_price - mid) / mid
   184	    if dist <= WALL_CLOSE_PCT:
   185	        return 1.0
   186	    if dist >= WALL_FAR_PCT:
   187	        return 0.2
   188	    # Interpolasi linear antara WALL_CLOSE_PCT dan WALL_FAR_PCT
   189	    t = (dist - WALL_CLOSE_PCT) / (WALL_FAR_PCT - WALL_CLOSE_PCT)
   190	    return round(1.0 - 0.8 * t, 4)
   191	
   192	
   193	def _spoofing_penalty(
   194	    levels: list,
   195	    prev: Dict[float, float],
   196	) -> float:
   197	    """
   198	    Deteksi spoofing: wall besar yang menghilang dalam 1 tick = spoof.
   199	    Return 0.3-1.0, makin rendah makin banyak spoof.
   200	    """
   201	    if not prev:
   202	        return 1.0
   203	    curr_map = {float(p): float(v) for p, v in levels[:20]}
   204	    prev_vals = list(prev.values()) or [0.0]
   205	    med_prev  = statistics.median(prev_vals)
   206	    disappeared = sum(
   207	        v for p, v in prev.items()
   208	        if p not in curr_map and v > med_prev * 2
   209	    )
   210	    total_prev = sum(prev.values()) or 1
   211	    spoof_ratio = min(disappeared / total_prev, 1.0)
   212	    return max(0.3, 1.0 - spoof_ratio)
   213	
   214	
   215	def _score_imbalance(imb: float, side: str = "long") -> float:
   216	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7, fungsi 1/3] side="short": reflection literal
   217	    # (imb -> 1-imb), BUKAN role-swap -- diverifikasi empiris dulu (200rb
   218	    # sampel acak + titik boundary): score_imbalance(imb) + score_imbalance
   219	    # (1-imb) == 100.0 PERSIS di seluruh range [0,1], tanpa deviasi sama
   220	    # sekali (beda dgn sar/pivot/fib yg TIDAK simetris sempurna) -- formula
   221	    # ini genuinely simetris, pola sama dgn _score_vwap_zone di trend.py.
   222	    if side == "short":
   223	        imb = 1.0 - imb
   224	    _anchor_bull = 50.0 + (IMBALANCE_BULL - 0.5) * 40.0  # ~54.8
   225	    _anchor_bear = 50.0 + (IMBALANCE_BEAR - 0.5) * 40.0  # ~45.2
   226	    if imb >= IMBALANCE_BULL:
   227	        t = (imb - IMBALANCE_BULL) / (1.0 - IMBALANCE_BULL)
   228	        return clamp_score(_anchor_bull + t * (90.0 - _anchor_bull))
   229	    elif imb <= IMBALANCE_BEAR:
   230	        t = (IMBALANCE_BEAR - imb) / IMBALANCE_BEAR
   231	        return clamp_score(_anchor_bear - t * (_anchor_bear - 10.0))
   232	    else:
   233	        return clamp_score(50.0 + (imb - 0.5) * 40.0)
   234	
   235	
   236	def _score_whale(
   237	    wb_str: Optional[float], bid_dist_factor: float,
   238	    cb_str: Optional[float], cb_price: Optional[float], wb_price: Optional[float],
   239	    wa_str: Optional[float], ask_dist_factor: float,
   240	    ca_str: Optional[float], ca_price: Optional[float], wa_price: Optional[float],
   241	    side: str = "long",
   242	) -> float:
   243	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7, fungsi 2/3] side="short": role-swap PENUH semua
   244	    # 5 pasangan bid<->ask (wb_str<->wa_str, bid_dist_factor<->ask_dist_
   245	    # factor, cb_str<->ca_str, cb_price<->ca_price, wb_price<->wa_price) --
   246	    # BUKAN reflection skalar tunggal spt imbalance_score (tidak ada satu
   247	    # angka kontinu yg bisa direfleksikan di sini, datanya inherently
   248	    # dua-sisi). Diverifikasi empiris dulu (200rb sampel acak): koefisien
   249	    # bid (0.3/cap 8.0 whale, 0.2/cap 5.0 cluster) IDENTIK dgn koefisien ask
   250	    # -- beda dgn score_pivot yg koefisien near/far-nya BEDA (12/6/-5 vs
   251	    # -15/-7/+5) sehingga pivot TIDAK sum-to-100. Whale_score kebetulan
   252	    # simetris sempurna (score+score_short==100, deviasi cuma float noise
   253	    # ~1e-14) justru KARENA role-swap penuh + koefisien identik, bukan krn
   254	    # ini reflection literal spt imbalance.
   255	    if side == "short":
   256	        wb_str, wa_str = wa_str, wb_str
   257	        bid_dist_factor, ask_dist_factor = ask_dist_factor, bid_dist_factor
   258	        cb_str, ca_str = ca_str, cb_str
   259	        cb_price, ca_price = ca_price, cb_price
   260	        wb_price, wa_price = wa_price, wb_price
   261	
   262	    score = 50.0
   263	    if wb_str:
   264	        score += min(wb_str * 0.3, 8.0) * bid_dist_factor
   265	    if wa_str:
   266	        score -= min(wa_str * 0.3, 8.0) * ask_dist_factor
   267	    if cb_str and cb_price != wb_price:   # cluster bonus jika beda dari single wall
   268	        score += min(cb_str * 0.2, 5.0) * bid_dist_factor
   269	    if ca_str and ca_price != wa_price:
   270	        score -= min(ca_str * 0.2, 5.0) * ask_dist_factor
   271	    return clamp_score(score)
   272	
   273	
   274	def _score_absorption(absorbed_bid: bool, absorbed_ask: bool, side: str = "long") -> float:
   275	    # [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7, fungsi 3/3, TERAKHIR] side="short": role-swap
   276	    # PENUH absorbed_bid<->absorbed_ask -- pola sama dgn _score_whale, BUKAN
   277	    # reflection skalar tunggal spt imbalance_score (cuma 2 boolean, tidak
   278	    # ada angka kontinu). Diverifikasi empiris dulu (domain finite, 4
   279	    # kombinasi, EXHAUSTIVE bukan cuma sampel acak): score+score_short==100
   280	    # PERSIS di semua 4 kombinasi -- koefisien +15/-15 identik di kedua
   281	    # sisi & range pre-clamp [35,65] tidak pernah menyentuh batas [0,100]
   282	    # (beda dgn score_pivot yg near/far-nya pakai koefisien BEDA).
   283	    if side == "short":
   284	        absorbed_bid, absorbed_ask = absorbed_ask, absorbed_bid
   285	    score = 50.0
   286	    if absorbed_ask:
   287	        score += 15.0   # (peran "ask diserap") = breakout signal utk side ini
   288	    if absorbed_bid:
   289	        score -= 15.0   # (peran "bid diserap") = breakdown signal utk side ini
   290	    return clamp_score(score)
   291	
   292	
   293	def _liquidity_score(total_raw_usdt: float) -> float:
   294	    """
   295	    MSL-6: Likuiditas pasar dalam USDT → skor 0-100.
   296	    < LIQUIDITY_SOFT  = skor rendah (risiko slippage tinggi).
   297	    > LIQUIDITY_FULL  = skor 100 (aman untuk position sizing apapun).
   298	    """
   299	    if total_raw_usdt <= 0:
   300	        return 0.0
   301	    if total_raw_usdt >= LIQUIDITY_FULL:
   302	        return 100.0
   303	    if total_raw_usdt <= LIQUIDITY_SOFT:
   304	        t = total_raw_usdt / LIQUIDITY_SOFT
   305	        return round(t * 40.0, 2)   # 0-40 untuk thin market
   306	    t = (total_raw_usdt - LIQUIDITY_SOFT) / (LIQUIDITY_FULL - LIQUIDITY_SOFT)
   307	    return round(40.0 + t * 60.0, 2)  # 40-100
   308	
   309	
   310	# ── Per-symbol state untuk absorption & wall age tracking (MSL-1 fix) ────────
   311	@dataclass
   312	class _SnapshotState:
   313	    """State per-symbol untuk perbandingan antar tick."""
   314	    prev_bid_walls: Dict[float, float] = field(default_factory=dict)  # price→usdt_weighted (WHALE-FILTERED, khusus absorption)
   315	    prev_ask_walls: Dict[float, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
   316	    # [BUG-FIX -- ditemukan lewat audit menyeluruh] prev_bid_raw/prev_ask_raw
   317	    # BARU: snapshot MENTAH (tidak difilter whale-only) khusus untuk spoofing
   318	    # detection. Sebelumnya _spoofing_penalty() di calculate_orderbook() salah
   319	    # memakai prev_bid_walls/prev_ask_walls (whale-filtered via _walls_to_dict,
   320	    # BUG-B fix) sebagai snapshot pembanding -- ini merusak heuristik internal
   321	    # _spoofing_penalty yang butuh himpunan CAMPURAN (kecil+besar) untuk bisa
   322	    # mendeteksi outlier via "value > median*2". Kalau prev SUDAH cuma berisi
   323	    # level whale-only (yang besarannya mirip satu sama lain by construction),
   324	    # tidak ada satu pun yang bisa ">2x median dari peer whale-only-nya sendiri"
   325	    # -- membuat spoofing TIDAK PERNAH terdeteksi di jalur produksi ini,
   326	    # dibuktikan lewat WhaleDetector.analyze() (jalur lain, pakai raw levels)
   327	    # yang BERHASIL mendeteksi skenario identik (confidence 1.0 vs 0.65).
   328	    # Fix: simpan snapshot mentah terpisah (mirror pola WhaleDetector.
   329	    # _prev_bids/_prev_asks) khusus utk _spoofing_penalty, prev_bid_walls/
   330	    # prev_ask_walls TETAP whale-filtered khusus utk _detect_absorption
   331	    # (tidak diubah -- itu fix BUG-B yang benar utk tujuannya sendiri).
   332	    prev_bid_raw:   Dict[float, float] = field(default_factory=dict)  # price→qty MENTAH, semua level lolos _filter_min_size
   333	    prev_ask_raw:   Dict[float, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
   334	    prev_ts:        float              = 0.0
   335	    # [MSL-B FIX] wall_first_seen dihapus — field ini tidak pernah dipakai di
   336	    # calculate_orderbook(). WhaleDetector mengelola wall age via self._wall_first_seen
   337	    # internal sendiri. Field di sini adalah dead code yang menyesatkan.
   338	    spread_history:  List[float]       = field(default_factory=list)   # rolling spread
   339	    last_active:     float             = field(default_factory=time.time)  # untuk TTL cleanup
   340	
   341	
   342	_state_registry: Dict[str, _SnapshotState] = {}
   343	
   344	_STATE_TTL_SECS = 3600.0  # state coin yang tidak aktif > 1 jam dihapus otomatis
   345	
   346	# [BUG-FIX -- konsistensi dgn fix _REGIME_BUFFERS (classifier.py) & _OBSERVATION_CACHE
   347	# (observer.py) hari ini] _state_registry diakses dari 2 jalur berbeda yg bisa jalan
   348	# BERSAMAAN: (1) _get_state() via calculate_orderbook() -> score_orderbook_data() ->
   349	# observer.py observe() -> dipanggil via run_in_executor (WORKER THREAD, lihat
   350	# strategy.py get_scored_signal); (2) cleanup_stale_states()/reset_state() dipanggil
   351	# langsung dari main.py (MAIN THREAD, loop periodik & saat coin dirotasi keluar
   352	# universe). Pola check-then-create di _get_state (`if symbol not in: create`) TIDAK
   353	# atomik. Eksperimen ekstensif (termasuk delay artifisial spt yg berhasil membuktikan
   354	# race di classifier.py/observer.py) TIDAK berhasil memicu crash/exception di sini --
   355	# beda dgn kasus lain, tidak ada pola delete-key-yang-sama-dua-kali di dalam
   356	# _get_state sendiri (delete cuma di cleanup_stale_states/reset_state, dan objek
   357	# _SnapshotState yg sudah di-fetch via reference lokal tetap aman diakses walau entry
   358	# registry-nya dihapus concurrent -- GC Python tidak crash krn refcount). Risiko nyata
   359	# HANYA lost-update ringan (dua thread bikin _SnapshotState baru utk symbol yg sama,
   360	# salah satu ke-overwrite) -- tidak crash, self-correcting (history absorption/
   361	# spoofing utk symbol itu di-reset, bukan corrupt). Lock tetap ditambahkan sbg
   362	# defense-in-depth/konsistensi, BUKAN krn ada bukti crash spt 2 kasus sebelumnya.
   363	_state_registry_lock = threading.Lock()
   364	
   365	
   366	def _get_state(symbol: str) -> _SnapshotState:
   367	    """Ambil state per-symbol. Buat baru jika belum ada. Update last_active."""
   368	    with _state_registry_lock:
   369	        if symbol not in _state_registry:
   370	            _state_registry[symbol] = _SnapshotState()
   371	        state = _state_registry[symbol]
   372	        state.last_active = time.time()
   373	        return state
   374	
   375	
   376	def reset_state(symbol: str) -> None:
   377	    """[MSL-A FIX] Hapus state coin tertentu — panggil saat coin dikeluarkan dari universe."""
   378	    with _state_registry_lock:
   379	        _state_registry.pop(symbol, None)
   380	    log.debug("orderbook: state '%s' direset", symbol)
   381	
   382	
   383	def cleanup_stale_states(ttl_secs: float = _STATE_TTL_SECS) -> int:
   384	    """[MSL-A FIX] Hapus state coin yang tidak aktif lebih dari ttl_secs.
   385	
   386	    Panggil dari main loop periodik (misal setiap jam) agar _state_registry
   387	    tidak tumbuh selamanya ketika coin dirotasi keluar dari universe.
   388	
   389	    Returns:
   390	        Jumlah state yang dihapus.
   391	    """
   392	    now = time.time()
   393	    with _state_registry_lock:
   394	        stale = [sym for sym, st in _state_registry.items()
   395	                 if (now - st.last_active) > ttl_secs]
   396	        for sym in stale:
   397	            del _state_registry[sym]
   398	    if stale:
   399	        log.info("orderbook: cleanup %d stale state(s): %s", len(stale), stale)
   400	    return len(stale)
   401	
   402	
   403	def _detect_absorption(
   404	    current_walls: Dict[float, float],
   405	    prev_walls:    Dict[float, float],
   406	) -> bool:
   407	    """
   408	    BUG-1 + MSL-1 fix: Cek apakah whale wall yang ada di tick sebelumnya
   409	    sudah menyusut > ABSORPTION_DROP_PCT (diserap market).
   410	    """
   411	    if not prev_walls:
   412	        return False
   413	    for price, prev_usdt in prev_walls.items():
   414	        curr_usdt = current_walls.get(price, 0.0)
   415	        if prev_usdt > 0 and (prev_usdt - curr_usdt) / prev_usdt >= ABSORPTION_DROP_PCT:
   416	            return True
   417	    return False
   418	
   419	
   420	def _walls_to_dict(levels: list, total_usdt: float = 0.0) -> Dict[float, float]:
   421	    """Konversi levels ke dict price→weighted_usdt untuk perbandingan absorption.
   422	
   423	    [BUG-B FIX] Hanya simpan level yang kekuatannya >= WHALE_WALL_PCT * total_usdt.
   424	    Sebelumnya semua 20 level disimpan sehingga micro-order kecil di level 18
   425	    yang menghilang bisa trigger absorbed=True. Sekarang hanya whale-level wall
   426	    yang masuk dict — absorption hanya aktif untuk wall yang benar-benar signifikan.
   427	    """
   428	    result: Dict[float, float] = {}
   429	    whale_threshold = total_usdt * WHALE_WALL_PCT if total_usdt > 0 else 0.0
   430	    for i, (p, q) in enumerate(levels[:20]):
   431	        p, q = float(p), float(q)
   432	        if p <= 0 or q <= 0:
   433	            continue
   434	        w    = _DEPTH_WEIGHTS[i] if i < len(_DEPTH_WEIGHTS) else 0.4
   435	        usdt = p * q * w
   436	        if whale_threshold <= 0 or usdt >= whale_threshold:
   437	            result[p] = usdt
   438	    return result
   439	
   440	
   441	# ── WhaleDetector (dipindah dari main.py — MSL-2 fix) ────────────────────────
   442	class WhaleDetector:
   443	    """
   444	    Weighted orderbook analyzer dengan:
   445	    - Spoofing detection (wall menghilang dalam 1 tick)
   446	    - Minimum size filter (buang micro-order)
   447	    - Wall age tracking (fresh wall lebih dipercaya)
   448	    - Dynamic threshold per coin (tipis vs tebal)
   449	    - Absorption detection (wall diserap market)
   450	
   451	    Sebelumnya ada di main.py (line 91). Dipindah ke sini (MSL-2).
   452	    main.py import dari sini; tidak ada duplikasi logika.
   453	    """
   454	
   455	    def __init__(self) -> None:
   456	        self._prev_bids: Dict[float, float] = {}
   457	        self._prev_asks: Dict[float, float] = {}
   458	        self._prev_ts:   float              = 0.0
   459	        self._wall_first_seen: Dict[str, float] = {}
   460	
   461	    def _weighted_wall(self, levels: list) -> float:
   462	        return _weighted_volume(levels)
   463	
   464	    def _filter_min_size(self, levels: list) -> list:
   465	        return _filter_min_size(levels)
   466	
   467	    def _spoofing_penalty(self, levels: list, prev: Dict[float, float]) -> float:
   468	        return _spoofing_penalty(levels, prev)
   469	
   470	    def _dynamic_threshold(self, bids: list, asks: list) -> Tuple[float, float]:
   471	        """Threshold dinamis: coin tipis lebih longgar, coin tebal lebih ketat."""
   472	        all_vals = [
   473	            float(p) * float(v)
   474	            for p, v in (bids + asks)[:40]
   475	            if float(p) > 0 and float(v) > 0
   476	        ]
   477	        if not all_vals:
   478	            return 0.65, 1.55
   479	        depth      = sum(all_vals)
   480	        med        = statistics.median(all_vals)
   481	        depth_norm = min(depth / (med * 40 + 1e-9), 1.0)
   482	        thr_sell   = round(0.50 + 0.20 * depth_norm, 3)  # 0.50–0.70
   483	        thr_buy    = round(1.70 - 0.20 * depth_norm, 3)  # 1.50–1.70
   484	        return thr_sell, thr_buy
   485	
   486	    def analyze(
   487	        self,
   488	        symbol:          str,
   489	        bids:            list,
   490	        asks:            list,
   491	        wall_first_seen: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None,
   492	    ) -> Dict:
   493	        """
   494	        Analisis orderbook lengkap.
   495	        wall_first_seen boleh None — WhaleDetector akan kelola state internalnya.
   496	        """
   497	        now = time.time()
   498	        wfs = wall_first_seen if wall_first_seen is not None else self._wall_first_seen
   499	
   500	        # Filter noise
   501	        bids_f = self._filter_min_size(bids)
   502	        asks_f = self._filter_min_size(asks)
   503	
   504	        # Weighted wall
   505	        bid_wall = self._weighted_wall(bids_f)
   506	        ask_wall = self._weighted_wall(asks_f)
   507	        ratio    = bid_wall / ask_wall if ask_wall > 0 else 1.0
   508	
   509	        # Spoofing penalty
   510	        penalty_b  = self._spoofing_penalty(bids_f, self._prev_bids)
   511	        penalty_a  = self._spoofing_penalty(asks_f, self._prev_asks)
   512	        confidence = round((penalty_b + penalty_a) / 2, 3)
   513	
   514	        # Update snapshot
   515	        self._prev_bids = {float(p): float(v) for p, v in bids_f[:20]}
   516	        self._prev_asks = {float(p): float(v) for p, v in asks_f[:20]}
   517	        self._prev_ts   = now
   518	
   519	        # Wall age adjustment
   520	        key = f"{symbol}_wall"
   521	        if ratio < 0.80 or ratio > 1.25:
   522	            if key not in wfs:
   523	                wfs[key] = now
   524	            age = now - wfs[key]
   525	            if age < 30:
   526	                confidence = min(confidence * 1.20, 1.0)   # fresh +20%
   527	            elif age > 300:
   528	                confidence = confidence * 0.80              # stale -20%
   529	        else:
   530	            wfs.pop(key, None)
   531	
   532	        thr_sell, thr_buy = self._dynamic_threshold(bids, asks)
   533	
   534	        return {
   535	            "ratio":      round(ratio, 4),
   536	            "confidence": confidence,
   537	            "bid_wall":   round(bid_wall, 2),
   538	            "ask_wall":   round(ask_wall, 2),
   539	            "thr_sell":   thr_sell,
   540	            "thr_buy":    thr_buy,
   541	        }
   542	
   543	
   544	# ── Main stateful calculator ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   545	def calculate_orderbook(ob: dict, symbol: str = "_default") -> dict:
   546	    """
   547	    Hitung semua metrik orderbook untuk satu snapshot.
   548	    symbol dipakai untuk state tracking (absorption & wall age).
   549	    """
   550	    result: Dict = {
   551	        "bid_ask_imbalance":  None,
   552	        "whale_bid_wall":     None,
   553	        "whale_ask_wall":     None,
   554	        "bid_wall_strength":  None,
   555	        "ask_wall_strength":  None,
   556	        "cluster_bid_wall":   None,
   557	        "cluster_bid_str":    None,
   558	        "cluster_ask_wall":   None,
   559	        "cluster_ask_str":    None,
   560	        "spread_pct":         None,
   561	        "absorbed_bid":       False,
   562	        "absorbed_ask":       False,
   563	        "bid_wall_dist":      None,   # jarak wall dari mid (0-1 relevance factor)
   564	        "ask_wall_dist":      None,
   565	        "liquidity_score":    50.0,
   566	        "spoofing_confidence": 1.0,
   567	        "imbalance_score":    50.0,
   568	        "imbalance_score_short": 50.0,
   569	        "whale_score":        50.0,
   570	        "whale_score_short":  50.0,
   571	        "spread_score":       50.0,
   572	        "absorption_score":   50.0,
   573	        "absorption_score_short": 50.0,
   574	    }
   575	
   576	    if not ob:
   577	        return result
   578	
   579	    bids: list = ob.get("bids", [])
   580	    asks: list = ob.get("asks", [])
   581	    if not bids or not asks:
   582	        return result
   583	
   584	    state = _get_state(symbol)
   585	
   586	    # ── Spread ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   587	    best_bid = float(bids[0][0]) if bids else 0.0
   588	    best_ask = float(asks[0][0]) if asks else 0.0
   589	    mid = (best_bid + best_ask) / 2 if best_bid > 0 and best_ask > 0 else 0.0
   590	
   591	    if best_bid > 0 and best_ask > 0 and mid > 0:
   592	        spread_pct = round((best_ask - best_bid) / mid * 100, 4)
   593	        result["spread_pct"] = spread_pct
   594	        # Rolling spread history untuk normalisasi kontekstual (MSL-4)
   595	        state.spread_history.append(spread_pct)
   596	        if len(state.spread_history) > 50:
   597	            state.spread_history.pop(0)
   598	
   599	    # ── Volume ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   600	    bids_f = _filter_min_size(bids)
   601	    asks_f = _filter_min_size(asks)
   602	
   603	    bid_vol_w = _weighted_volume(bids_f)
   604	    ask_vol_w = _weighted_volume(asks_f)
   605	    total_w   = bid_vol_w + ask_vol_w
   606	
   607	    bid_vol_raw = _raw_volume(bids)
   608	    ask_vol_raw = _raw_volume(asks)
   609	    total_raw   = bid_vol_raw + ask_vol_raw
   610	
   611	    # ── Imbalance ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   612	    # [BUG-FIX v3.1] Diskontinuitas 10.2 poin di kedua boundary imbalance:
   613	    # Neutral branch berakhir di 54.8 saat imb=0.62, tapi bull branch dimulai
   614	    # dari 65.0 — lompatan yang tidak masuk akal. Begitu pula di sisi bear.
   615	    # Fix: anchor bull/bear branch tepat di nilai yang dihasilkan neutral branch,
   616	    # sehingga scoring kontinu di seluruh range [0, 1]. Logic dipindah ke
   617	    # _score_imbalance() [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7] supaya bisa dipanggil ulang
   618	    # dgn side="short" (reflection literal, imb -> 1-imb -- lihat docstring
   619	    # _score_imbalance utk verifikasi simetrinya).
   620	    if total_w > 0:
   621	        imb = round(bid_vol_w / total_w, 4)
   622	        result["bid_ask_imbalance"] = imb
   623	        result["imbalance_score"] = _score_imbalance(imb)
   624	        result["imbalance_score_short"] = _score_imbalance(imb, side="short")
   625	
   626	    # ── Whale walls (single level) ────────────────────────────────────────────
   627	    wb_price, wb_str = _find_whale_wall(bids_f, bid_vol_w)
   628	    wa_price, wa_str = _find_whale_wall(asks_f, ask_vol_w)
   629	    result["whale_bid_wall"]    = wb_price
   630	    result["bid_wall_strength"] = wb_str
   631	    result["whale_ask_wall"]    = wa_price
   632	    result["ask_wall_strength"] = wa_str
   633	
   634	    # ── Cluster walls (MSL-3) ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   635	    cb_price, cb_str = _find_cluster_wall(bids_f, bid_vol_w)
   636	    ca_price, ca_str = _find_cluster_wall(asks_f, ask_vol_w)
   637	    result["cluster_bid_wall"] = cb_price
   638	    result["cluster_bid_str"]  = cb_str
   639	    result["cluster_ask_wall"] = ca_price
   640	    result["cluster_ask_str"]  = ca_str
   641	
   642	    # ── Wall distance relevance factor (MSL-5) ────────────────────────────────
   643	    effective_bid_wall = wb_price or cb_price
   644	    effective_ask_wall = wa_price or ca_price
   645	    bid_dist_factor = _wall_distance_factor(effective_bid_wall, mid)
   646	    ask_dist_factor = _wall_distance_factor(effective_ask_wall, mid)
   647	    result["bid_wall_dist"] = bid_dist_factor
   648	    result["ask_wall_dist"] = ask_dist_factor
   649	
   650	    # ── Absorption detection (BUG-1 + MSL-1 fix) ─────────────────────────────
   651	    curr_bid_dict = _walls_to_dict(bids_f, total_raw)
   652	    curr_ask_dict = _walls_to_dict(asks_f, total_raw)
   653	
   654	    if state.prev_ts > 0:  # Hanya cek jika ada snapshot sebelumnya
   655	        result["absorbed_bid"] = _detect_absorption(curr_bid_dict, state.prev_bid_walls)
   656	        result["absorbed_ask"] = _detect_absorption(curr_ask_dict, state.prev_ask_walls)
   657	
   658	    # [BUG-A FIX] Simpan snapshot prev SEBELUM state di-update — dipakai spoofing di bawah.
   659	    # Sebelumnya spoofing menggunakan state.prev_bid_walls SETELAH di-overwrite curr,
   660	    # sehingga membandingkan current vs current → _spoofing_penalty selalu return 1.0.
   661	    # [BUG-FIX TAMBAHAN] Snapshot utk spoofing sekarang pakai prev_bid_raw/prev_ask_raw
   662	    # (mentah, bukan whale-filtered) -- lihat penjelasan lengkap di docstring
   663	    # _SnapshotState. prev_bid_walls/prev_ask_walls (whale-filtered) TETAP dipakai
   664	    # HANYA utk absorption di bawah, tidak diubah.
   665	    prev_bid_raw_snapshot = dict(state.prev_bid_raw)
   666	    prev_ask_raw_snapshot = dict(state.prev_ask_raw)
   667	
   668	    # Update state
   669	    state.prev_bid_walls = curr_bid_dict
   670	    state.prev_ask_walls = curr_ask_dict
   671	    state.prev_bid_raw   = {float(p): float(q) for p, q in bids_f[:20] if float(p) > 0 and float(q) > 0}
   672	    state.prev_ask_raw   = {float(p): float(q) for p, q in asks_f[:20] if float(p) > 0 and float(q) > 0}
   673	    state.prev_ts        = time.time()
   674	
   675	    # ── Spoofing confidence ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   676	    # [BUG-A FIX] Pakai prev_snapshot (sebelum update) bukan state.prev yang sudah = curr
   677	    # [BUG-FIX TAMBAHAN] Pakai snapshot MENTAH (prev_bid_raw_snapshot), bukan
   678	    # whale-filtered -- supaya heuristik ">2x median" _spoofing_penalty punya
   679	    # himpunan campuran utk mendeteksi outlier, konsisten dgn WhaleDetector.analyze().
   680	    pen_b = _spoofing_penalty(bids_f, prev_bid_raw_snapshot)
   681	    pen_a = _spoofing_penalty(asks_f, prev_ask_raw_snapshot)
   682	    result["spoofing_confidence"] = round((pen_b + pen_a) / 2, 3)
   683	
   684	    # ── Liquidity score (MSL-6) ───────────────────────────────────────────────
   685	    result["liquidity_score"] = _liquidity_score(total_raw)
   686	
   687	    # ── Whale sub-score (dengan distance factor — MSL-5) ─────────────────────
   688	    # Logic dipindah ke _score_whale() [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7] supaya bisa
   689	    # dipanggil ulang dgn side="short" (role-swap penuh bid<->ask -- lihat
   690	    # docstring _score_whale utk verifikasi simetrinya).
   691	    result["whale_score"] = _score_whale(
   692	        wb_str, bid_dist_factor, cb_str, cb_price, wb_price,
   693	        wa_str, ask_dist_factor, ca_str, ca_price, wa_price,
   694	    )
   695	    result["whale_score_short"] = _score_whale(
   696	        wb_str, bid_dist_factor, cb_str, cb_price, wb_price,
   697	        wa_str, ask_dist_factor, ca_str, ca_price, wa_price,
   698	        side="short",
   699	    )
   700	
   701	    # ── Spread sub-score (kontekstual — MSL-4) ────────────────────────────────
   702	    spread_score = 80.0  # default bagus
   703	    if result["spread_pct"] is not None:
   704	        sp = result["spread_pct"]
   705	        # Gunakan median historis sebagai baseline "normal" untuk coin ini
   706	        baseline = statistics.median(state.spread_history) if len(state.spread_history) >= 3 else 0.1
   707	        relative = sp / max(baseline, 0.01)
   708	        if relative > 3.0:
   709	            spread_score = 20.0   # spread 3x+ normal = sangat buruk
   710	        elif relative > 2.0:
   711	            spread_score = 40.0
   712	        elif relative > 1.5:
   713	            spread_score = 60.0
   714	        elif relative > 1.0:
   715	            spread_score = 70.0
   716	        else:
   717	            spread_score = 85.0
   718	    result["spread_score"] = spread_score
   719	
   720	    # ── Absorption sub-score ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   721	    # Logic dipindah ke _score_absorption() [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7] supaya bisa
   722	    # dipanggil ulang dgn side="short" (role-swap penuh absorbed_bid<->
   723	    # absorbed_ask -- lihat docstring _score_absorption utk verifikasi
   724	    # simetrinya).
   725	    result["absorption_score"] = _score_absorption(result["absorbed_bid"], result["absorbed_ask"])
   726	    result["absorption_score_short"] = _score_absorption(
   727	        result["absorbed_bid"], result["absorbed_ask"], side="short"
   728	    )
   729	
   730	    return result
   731	
   732	
   733	def score_orderbook(data: dict, side: str = "long") -> float:
   734	    """
   735	    Hitung composite orderbook score 0-100 dari semua sub-komponen.
   736	    Komponen: imbalance (40%) + whale (25%) + absorption (20%) + spread (10%) + liquidity (5%).
   737	
   738	    [BIAS-FIX -- Batch 7, wiring composite] side="short": baca
   739	    imbalance_score_short/whale_score_short/absorption_score_short (SELALU
   740	    terisi -- dijamin oleh calculate_orderbook(), tidak perlu fallback
   741	    manual). spread_score, liquidity_score, spoofing_confidence dipakai
   742	    IDENTIK di kedua sisi -- diverifikasi eksplisit (Tahap 0 investigasi):
   743	    spoofing_confidence = rata-rata pen_b & pen_a (komutatif, arah-agnostic
   744	    scr matematis DAN empiris via 2000 fuzz swap-test, 0 mismatch);
   745	    spread_score/liquidity_score sudah dikonfirmasi arah-agnostic sebelum
   746	    Batch 7 dimulai. Bobot (40/25/20/10/5) & formula penalti spoofing
   747	    TIDAK berubah antar side.
   748	    """
   749	    if data.get("bid_ask_imbalance") is None:
   750	        return 50.0
   751	
   752	    suffix = "_short" if side == "short" else ""
   753	    imb_score  = data.get(f"imbalance_score{suffix}",  50.0)
   754	    whl_score  = data.get(f"whale_score{suffix}",       50.0)
   755	    abs_score  = data.get(f"absorption_score{suffix}",  50.0)
   756	    spr_score  = data.get("spread_score",       80.0)
   757	    liq_score  = data.get("liquidity_score",    50.0)
   758	    spoof_conf = data.get("spoofing_confidence", 1.0)
   759	
   760	    # Weighted composite
   761	    raw = (
   762	        imb_score * 0.40
   763	        + whl_score  * 0.25
   764	        + abs_score  * 0.20
   765	        + spr_score  * 0.10
   766	        + liq_score  * 0.05
   767	    )
   768	
   769	    # Spoofing confidence penalty: jika banyak spoof, skor menuju netral
   770	    score = raw * spoof_conf + 50.0 * (1.0 - spoof_conf)
   771	
   772	    return clamp_score(score)
   773	
   774	
   775	# ── Public entry point ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   776	def score_orderbook_data(ob: dict, errors: Optional[list] = None, symbol: str = "_default") -> OrderbookIndicators:
   777	    """
   778	    Entry point utama — dipanggil dari observer.py.
   779	    Menerima ob dict dari live_orderbooks[symbol] dan mengembalikan OrderbookIndicators.
   780	
   781	    Args:
   782	        ob:     Dict {"bids": [...], "asks": [...], "_ts": float}
   783	        errors: List untuk append pesan error (opsional)
   784	        symbol: Nama simbol untuk state tracking per-coin
   785	    """
   786	    result = OrderbookIndicators()
   787	    if not ob:
   788	        return result
   789	    try:
   790	        sym  = ob.get("symbol", symbol)
   791	        data = calculate_orderbook(ob, symbol=sym)
   792	
   793	        result.bid_ask_imbalance    = data["bid_ask_imbalance"]
   794	        result.whale_bid_wall       = data["whale_bid_wall"]
   795	        result.whale_ask_wall       = data["whale_ask_wall"]
   796	        result.bid_wall_strength    = data["bid_wall_strength"]
   797	        result.ask_wall_strength    = data["ask_wall_strength"]
   798	        result.cluster_bid_wall     = data["cluster_bid_wall"]
   799	        result.cluster_bid_str      = data["cluster_bid_str"]
   800	        result.cluster_ask_wall     = data["cluster_ask_wall"]
   801	        result.cluster_ask_str      = data["cluster_ask_str"]
   802	        result.spread_pct           = data["spread_pct"]
   803	        result.absorbed_bid         = data["absorbed_bid"]
   804	        result.absorbed_ask         = data["absorbed_ask"]
   805	        result.bid_wall_dist        = data["bid_wall_dist"]
   806	        result.ask_wall_dist        = data["ask_wall_dist"]
   807	        result.liquidity_score      = data["liquidity_score"]
   808	        result.spoofing_confidence  = data["spoofing_confidence"]
   809	        result.imbalance_score      = data["imbalance_score"]
   810	        result.imbalance_score_short = data["imbalance_score_short"]
   811	        result.whale_score          = data["whale_score"]
   812	        result.whale_score_short    = data["whale_score_short"]
   813	        result.spread_score         = data["spread_score"]
   814	        result.absorption_score     = data["absorption_score"]
   815	        result.absorption_score_short = data["absorption_score_short"]
   816	        result.orderbook_score      = score_orderbook(data)
   817	        result.orderbook_score_short = score_orderbook(data, side="short")
   818	        result.composite_score      = result.orderbook_score
   819	    except Exception as exc:
   820	        if errors is not None:
   821	            errors.append(f"orderbook: {exc}")
   822	        log.exception("Error kalkulasi orderbook [%s]: %s", symbol, exc)
   823	    return result
